// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// WingAxe
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class WingAxe : HeldAxe
{
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject wings;

	[SerializeField]
	private Animator anim;

	public override bool Swing()
	{
		StartCoroutine(FlyAway());
		PlayerController.instance.StopHoldingAxe(destroy: false);
		return false;
	}

	private IEnumerator FlyAway()
	{
		PlayerData.activeFile.RecordAxeBreak(AxeType.Wings);
		base.transform.SetParent(null);
		wings.SetActive(value: true);
		anim.speed = 4f;
		anim.SetBool("fly", value: true);
		wings.transform.DOScale(1f, 0.4f);
		base.transform.DORotate(Vector3.zero, 0.3f);
		Vector3 endValue = PlayerController.instance.transform.position + PlayerController.instance.transform.forward * 0.5f + Vector3.up;
		base.transform.DOMove(endValue, 0.3f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.6f);
		base.transform.DOMoveY(100f, 50f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(50f);
		Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Adjacencies
using System;

[Serializable]
public class Adjacencies
{
	public RuleType n = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType e = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType s = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType w = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType nw = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType ne = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType se = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType sw = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType above = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_nw = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_n = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_ne = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_w = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_e = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_sw = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_s = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType a_se = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType below = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_nw = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_n = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_ne = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_w = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_e = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_sw = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_s = RuleType.DontCare;

	public RuleType b_se = RuleType.DontCare;

	public void RotateClockwise()
	{
		RuleType ruleType = nw;
		nw = sw;
		sw = se;
		se = ne;
		ne = ruleType;
		ruleType = n;
		n = w;
		w = s;
		s = e;
		e = ruleType;
		ruleType = a_nw;
		a_nw = a_sw;
		a_sw = a_se;
		a_se = a_ne;
		a_ne = ruleType;
		ruleType = a_n;
		a_n = a_w;
		a_w = a_s;
		a_s = a_e;
		a_e = ruleType;
		ruleType = b_nw;
		b_nw = b_sw;
		b_sw = b_se;
		b_se = b_ne;
		b_ne = ruleType;
		ruleType = b_n;
		b_n = b_w;
		b_w = b_s;
		b_s = b_e;
		b_e = ruleType;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// AllAxesCheck
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class AllAxesCheck : MonoBehaviour
{
	public UnityEvent onAllAxesBroken;

	private bool inRange;

	private bool activated;

	private void Start()
	{
		Check();
		if (SceneStuff.inst != null)
		{
			SceneStuff.inst.allAxesCheck = this;
		}
	}

	public void Check()
	{
		if (!activated && !inRange && PlayerData.activeFile.axesBroken.Count >= PlayerController.instance.axes.Length)
		{
			onAllAxesBroken.Invoke();
			activated = true;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if ((bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = true;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if ((bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = false;
			Check();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Angel
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using MoreMountains.Feedbacks;
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class Angel : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private CinemachineCamera focusCam;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject rightWall;

	[SerializeField]
	private float knockOffTime = 0.5f;

	[SerializeField]
	private UnityEvent onHit;

	[SerializeField]
	private MMF_Player feedback;

	[SerializeField]
	private Animator anim;

	[SerializeField]
	private FallingSequence fallingSequence;

	private bool sabotaging;

	private void Start()
	{
		StartCoroutine(FlyAway());
	}

	private IEnumerator FlyAway()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3f);
		anim.SetBool("fly", value: true);
		base.transform.DOMoveY(30f, 10f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3f);
		focusCam.Priority = -1;
	}

	public void Sabotage()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoSabotage());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoSabotage()
	{
		PlayerController player = PlayerController.instance;
		base.transform.position = player.transform.position + Vector3.left * 20f;
		base.transform.DOMoveX(-5f, 5f);
		for (float t = 0f; t < 5f; t += Time.fixedDeltaTime)
		{
			base.transform.position = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, player.transform.position.y, player.transform.position.z);
			yield return new WaitForFixedUpdate();
		}
		rightWall.SetActive(value: false);
		sabotaging = true;
		base.transform.DOMoveX(2f, knockOffTime);
		for (float t = 0f; t < knockOffTime; t += Time.deltaTime)
		{
			base.transform.position = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, player.transform.position.y, player.transform.position.z);
			yield return new WaitForFixedUpdate();
		}
	}

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		PlayerController component = collision.collider.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null && !component.dead && sabotaging)
		{
			SceneStuff.inst.StopMusic();
			PlayerController.instance.autoRespawn = false;
			feedback.transform.SetParent(null);
			feedback.transform.position = collision.contacts[0].point;
			feedback.PlayFeedbacks();
			component.Kill();
			component.AddForce(Vector3.up * 10f + Vector3.right * 20f);
			fallingSequence.StartFall();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// AppleLauncher
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class AppleLauncher : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Rigidbody apple;

	[SerializeField]
	private Rigidbody brick;

	[SerializeField]
	private float timeBetweenLaunches = 0.5f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float launchSpeed = 20f;

	[SerializeField]
	private Vector3 maxRandomOffset;

	[SerializeField]
	private float aimHeight = 2.5f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float timeReduction = 0.95f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float brickTime = 0.05f;

	private void Start()
	{
		StartCoroutine(LaunchApples());
	}

	private IEnumerator LaunchApples()
	{
		Vector3 vector;
		while (true)
		{
			vector = new Vector3(Random.Range(0f - maxRandomOffset.x, maxRandomOffset.x), Random.Range(0f - maxRandomOffset.y, maxRandomOffset.y), Random.Range(0f - maxRandomOffset.z, maxRandomOffset.z));
			if (timeBetweenLaunches <= brickTime)
			{
				break;
			}
			Rigidbody rigidbody = Object.Instantiate(apple, base.transform.position + vector, Random.rotation);
			rigidbody.linearVelocity = (PlayerController.instance.transform.position + Vector3.up * aimHeight - rigidbody.transform.position).normalized * launchSpeed;
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(timeBetweenLaunches);
			timeBetweenLaunches *= timeReduction;
		}
		Rigidbody rigidbody2 = Object.Instantiate(brick, base.transform.position + vector, Random.rotation);
		rigidbody2.linearVelocity = (PlayerController.instance.transform.position + Vector3.up * aimHeight - rigidbody2.transform.position).normalized * launchSpeed;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Arcade
using System;
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using TMPro;
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Rendering;

public class Arcade : MonoBehaviour
{
	public CinemachineCamera cineCam;

	public Volume gameVolume;

	public ArcadePlayer arcadePlayer;

	public ArcadeTree[] trees;

	public Transform title;

	public Transform gameOver;

	public AudioSource deathSound;

	public TMP_Text scoreboard;

	public GameObject finalScoreScreen;

	public TMP_Text finalScoreDisplay;

	public GameObject realTreeCircle;

	public InteractionTrigger interaction;

	public AudioClip music;

	public TMP_Text[] otherScores;

	public int highScore = 99999;

	public bool requiresCoin = true;

	[NonSerialized]
	public float timeSurvived;

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool stopped;

	public void StartPlaying()
	{
		if (requiresCoin)
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.coinCount--;
		}
		stopped = false;
		arcadePlayer.transform.localPosition = Vector2.zero;
		cineCam.Priority.Enabled = true;
		DOTween.To(() => gameVolume.weight, delegate(float x)
		{
			gameVolume.weight = x;
		}, 1f, 0.5f);
		PlayerController.instance.AddBlocker(this);
		stopped = false;
		StartCoroutine(IntroSequence());
	}

	public void Replay()
	{
		if (requiresCoin)
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.coinCount--;
		}
		stopped = false;
		StartCoroutine(IntroSequence());
	}

	public void StopPlaying()
	{
		if (requiresCoin)
		{
			interaction.enabled = false;
		}
		if (requiresCoin)
		{
			realTreeCircle.SetActive(value: true);
		}
		cineCam.Priority.Enabled = false;
		DOTween.To(() => gameVolume.weight, delegate(float x)
		{
			gameVolume.weight = x;
		}, 0f, 0.5f);
		PlayerController.instance.RemoveBlocker(this);
		arcadePlayer.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		if (requiresCoin)
		{
			ArcadeTree[] array = trees;
			for (int num = 0; num < array.Length; num++)
			{
				array[num].gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			}
			StartCoroutine(KillAfterTime());
		}
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (arcadePlayer.gameObject.activeInHierarchy && !stopped)
		{
			timeSurvived += Time.fixedDeltaTime;
			scoreboard.SetText($"SCORE {(int)timeSurvived}");
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator IntroSequence()
	{
		finalScoreScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		scoreboard.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		timeSurvived = 0f;
		gameOver.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
		GameManager.instance.StartMusic(music);
		title.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		title.transform.localPosition = Vector3.up * 4f;
		title.transform.DOLocalMove(Vector3.zero, 2f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3f);
		scoreboard.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		title.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		arcadePlayer.dead = false;
		arcadePlayer.transform.localPosition = Vector3.zero;
		arcadePlayer.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		ArcadeTree[] array = trees;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			array[i].Activate();
		}
	}

	public void DoDeath()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DeathSequence());
	}

	private IEnumerator DeathSequence()
	{
		GameManager.instance.StopMusic(music);
		stopped = true;
		deathSound.Play();
		arcadePlayer.transform.DOLocalRotate(new Vector3(0f, 0f, 360f), 0.5f, RotateMode.FastBeyond360);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.5f);
		arcadePlayer.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
		ArcadeTree[] array = trees;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			array[i].gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		}
		gameOver.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
		gameOver.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		finalScoreDisplay.text = ((int)timeSurvived).ToString();
		for (int j = 0; j < otherScores.Length; j++)
		{
			otherScores[j].text = (highScore - j).ToString();
		}
		finalScoreScreen.SetActive(value: true);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(2f);
		string node = (requiresCoin ? "replayArcade" : "replayArcadeFree");
		GameManager.instance.RunDialogue(node);
	}

	private IEnumerator KillAfterTime()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3.5f);
		PlayerController.instance.Kill();
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ArcadePlayer
using System;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem;

public class ArcadePlayer : MonoBehaviour
{
	[Serializable]
	public class WalkFrame
	{
		public Sprite sprite;

		public bool footstep;

		public float time = 0.2f;
	}

	public Arcade arcade;

	public float moveSpeed = 1f;

	public Vector2 maxDist = new Vector2(4f, 3f);

	public AudioSource aud;

	public SpriteRenderer rend;

	public WalkFrame[] walkCycle;

	private float walkTimer;

	private int walkState;

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool dead;

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		Vector2 vector = InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Move").ReadValue<Vector2>();
		Move(vector);
	}

	public void Move(Vector3 move)
	{
		if (dead)
		{
			return;
		}
		if (move.magnitude > 0f)
		{
			walkTimer += Time.fixedDeltaTime;
			if (walkTimer > walkCycle[walkState].time)
			{
				walkTimer -= walkCycle[walkState].time;
				walkState = (walkState + 1) % walkCycle.Length;
				rend.sprite = walkCycle[walkState].sprite;
				if (walkCycle[walkState].footstep)
				{
					aud.Play();
				}
			}
		}
		Vector3 vector = base.transform.localPosition + move * moveSpeed * Time.fixedDeltaTime;
		vector = new Vector2(Mathf.Clamp(vector.x, 0f - maxDist.x, maxDist.x), Mathf.Clamp(vector.y, 0f - maxDist.y, maxDist.y));
		base.transform.localPosition = vector;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter2D(Collider2D collision)
	{
		if (!dead && collision.tag == "Tree")
		{
			dead = true;
			arcade.DoDeath();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ArcadeTree
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

public class ArcadeTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public ArcadePlayer target;

	public Arcade arcade;

	public float chaseSpeed = 5f;

	public float wanderSpeed = 0.5f;

	public float avoidSpeed = 2f;

	public float minStateTime = 1f;

	public float maxStateTime = 4f;

	public float fastSpeed = 30f;

	private bool hurrying;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	private List<ArcadeTree> treesInRange = new List<ArcadeTree>();

	private bool chasing;

	private Vector3 wanderDir = Vector3.up;

	private void Start()
	{
		startPos = base.transform.position;
		base.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
	}

	private void OnDisable()
	{
		StopAllCoroutines();
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (!target.gameObject.activeInHierarchy || arcade.stopped)
		{
			base.enabled = false;
		}
		Vector3 zero = Vector3.zero;
		foreach (ArcadeTree item in treesInRange)
		{
			Vector3 normalized = (base.transform.localPosition - item.transform.localPosition).normalized;
			zero += normalized * avoidSpeed;
		}
		if (chasing)
		{
			Vector3 normalized2 = (target.transform.localPosition - base.transform.localPosition).normalized;
			zero += normalized2 * (hurrying ? fastSpeed : chaseSpeed);
		}
		else
		{
			zero += wanderDir * wanderSpeed;
		}
		if (!hurrying && arcade.timeSurvived > (float)(arcade.highScore - 4))
		{
			HurryUp();
		}
		Vector3 vector = base.transform.localPosition + zero * Time.fixedDeltaTime;
		vector = new Vector3(Mathf.Clamp(vector.x, 0f - target.maxDist.x, target.maxDist.x), Mathf.Clamp(vector.y, 0f - target.maxDist.y, target.maxDist.y), 0f);
		base.transform.localPosition = vector;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter2D(Collider2D collision)
	{
		ArcadeTree component = collision.gameObject.GetComponent<ArcadeTree>();
		if (component != null && !treesInRange.Contains(component))
		{
			treesInRange.Add(component);
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit2D(Collider2D collision)
	{
		ArcadeTree component = collision.gameObject.GetComponent<ArcadeTree>();
		if (component != null && treesInRange.Contains(component))
		{
			treesInRange.Remove(component);
		}
	}

	public void Activate()
	{
		base.transform.position = startPos;
		base.enabled = true;
		hurrying = false;
		base.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		StartCoroutine(CycleStates());
	}

	public void HurryUp()
	{
		hurrying = true;
	}

	private IEnumerator CycleStates()
	{
		chasing = Random.value > 0.5f;
		while (true)
		{
			chasing = !chasing;
			if (!chasing)
			{
				wanderDir = Random.insideUnitCircle.normalized;
			}
			float seconds = Random.Range(minStateTime, maxStateTime);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(seconds);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// AxePickup
using UnityEngine;

public class AxePickup : MonoBehaviour
{
	public AxeType axeType;

	private void Start()
	{
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.axesBroken.Contains(axeType))
		{
			Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
		}
	}

	public void PickUp()
	{
		PlayerController.instance.HoldAxe((int)axeType);
		Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// AxeStump
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class AxeStump : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Animator anim;

	public float timeBetweenAttacks = 2f;

	private bool activated;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider col)
	{
		if (!activated && col.GetComponent<PlayerController>() != null)
		{
			activated = true;
			anim.SetBool("activated", value: true);
			StartCoroutine(DoAttacks());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoAttacks()
	{
		while (true)
		{
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(timeBetweenAttacks);
			anim.SetTrigger("swing");
		}
	}
}

	Shatter,
	Bomb,
	Wings,
	Bounce,
	Shrink,
	Grow
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// BallTree
using UnityEngine;

public class BallTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Rigidbody rb;

	public float chaseAcceleration = 5f;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	public void StartRolling()
	{
		rb.isKinematic = false;
		startPos = rb.transform.position;
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (!rb.isKinematic)
		{
			Vector3 vector = PlayerController.instance.transform.position - base.transform.position;
			rb.AddForce(vector * chaseAcceleration, ForceMode.Acceleration);
		}
	}

	public void ResetState()
	{
		rb.isKinematic = true;
		rb.transform.position = startPos;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// BasicTile
using System;
using UnityEngine;

[Serializable]
[CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "BasicTile", menuName = "3D Tile/Basic Tile", order = 5)]
public class BasicTile : TileType
{
	public GameObject prefab;

	public bool randomize;

	public bool randomizeRotation;

	public GameObject[] prefabChoices;

	public bool[,,] occupiedSpace;

	public Vector3 maxOffset = Vector3.zero;

	public Vector3 origin = Vector3.zero;

	public GameObject GetObject(Vector3 worldPos, int rotation)
	{
		GameObject original = prefab;
		if (randomize)
		{
			original = prefabChoices[UnityEngine.Random.Range(0, prefabChoices.Length)];
		}
		Vector3 position = worldPos + origin + new Vector3(UnityEngine.Random.Range(0f - maxOffset.x, maxOffset.x), UnityEngine.Random.Range(0f - maxOffset.y, maxOffset.y), UnityEngine.Random.Range(0f - maxOffset.z, maxOffset.z));
		GameObject gameObject = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(original);
		gameObject.transform.position = position;
		gameObject.transform.rotation = Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.up * 90f * rotation);
		if (randomizeRotation)
		{
			gameObject.transform.rotation *= Quaternion.Euler(0f, UnityEngine.Random.Range(0, 360), 0f);
		}
		return gameObject;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// BazookaTree
using System.Collections;
using BigRookGames.Weapons;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class BazookaTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform revealPos;

	public float revealTime = 0.4f;

	public float afterShootTime = 1f;

	public GunfireController bazooka;

	private bool onCooldown;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	private Vector3 startScale;

	private void Start()
	{
		startPos = bazooka.transform.position;
		startScale = bazooka.transform.localScale;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (other.GetComponent<PlayerController>() != null && !onCooldown)
		{
			StartCoroutine(Shoot());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator Shoot()
	{
		onCooldown = true;
		bazooka.transform.DOScale(revealPos.localScale, revealTime);
		bazooka.transform.DOMove(revealPos.position, revealTime);
		for (float t = 0f; t < revealTime; t += Time.deltaTime)
		{
			bazooka.transform.LookAt(PlayerController.instance.transform.TransformPoint(Vector3.up));
			yield return null;
		}
		bazooka.FireWeapon();
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(afterShootTime);
		bazooka.transform.DOScale(startScale, revealTime);
		bazooka.transform.DOMove(startPos, revealTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(revealTime);
		onCooldown = false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// BounceAxe
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class BounceAxe : HeldAxe
{
	public Rigidbody rb;

	public Collider[] colliders;

	public LayerMask layerMask;

	public float upwardSpeed = 10f;

	public float backwardSpeed = 8f;

	private bool broken;

	private bool swinging;

	public override bool Swing()
	{
		if (!broken)
		{
			StartCoroutine(ResetAfterTime());
		}
		return true;
	}

	private IEnumerator ResetAfterTime()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.1f);
		swinging = true;
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
		swinging = false;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (swinging && InLayerMask(other.gameObject.layer, layerMask))
		{
			broken = true;
			rb.isKinematic = false;
			base.transform.SetParent(null);
			PlayerController.instance.StopHoldingAxe(destroy: false);
			Collider[] array = colliders;
			for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
			{
				array[i].enabled = true;
			}
			rb.linearVelocity = Vector3.up * upwardSpeed - PlayerController.instance.transform.forward * backwardSpeed;
			PlayerData.activeFile.RecordAxeBreak(AxeType.Bounce);
			Object.Destroy(base.gameObject, 0.7f);
		}
	}

	private bool InLayerMask(int layer, LayerMask mask)
	{
		return (mask.value & (1 << layer)) != 0;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// BurnableGrass
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class BurnableGrass : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float spreadTime = 3f;

	public float spreadDistance = 2f;

	public GameObject fire;

	public bool burning;

	public bool fireFollow;

	public float fireSize = 1f;

	public UnityEvent OnCatchFire;

	private Transform fireInst;

	public void Burn()
	{
		burning = true;
		OnCatchFire.Invoke();
		fireInst = Object.Instantiate(fire, base.transform.position, Quaternion.identity).transform;
		fireInst.transform.SetParent(base.transform.parent);
		fireInst.localScale = Vector3.one * fireSize;
		if (fireFollow)
		{
			InvokeRepeating("Spread", spreadTime, spreadTime);
		}
		else
		{
			Invoke("Spread", spreadTime);
		}
	}

	private void Spread()
	{
		Collider[] array = Physics.OverlapSphere(base.transform.position, spreadDistance);
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			BurnableGrass component = array[i].GetComponent<BurnableGrass>();
			if (component != null && !component.burning)
			{
				component.Burn();
			}
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (fireFollow && fireInst != null)
		{
			fireInst.transform.position = base.transform.position;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Chair
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem;

public class Chair : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float prepTime = 0.15f;

	public Light sun;

	public float minSunSpeed = 30f;

	public float maxSunSpeed = 360f;

	public float timeToSpeedUp = 60f;

	private bool sitting;

	private InputAction moveAction;

	private float sunIntensity;

	private void Start()
	{
		moveAction = InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Move");
		sunIntensity = sun.intensity;
	}

	public void Sit()
	{
		sitting = true;
		PlayerController.instance.blockers.Add(this);
		StartCoroutine(SitCoroutine());
	}

	private IEnumerator SitCoroutine()
	{
		PlayerController.instance.rb.isKinematic = true;
		PlayerController.instance.transform.DOMove(base.transform.position, prepTime);
		PlayerController.instance.transform.DORotateQuaternion(base.transform.rotation, prepTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(prepTime);
		PlayerController.instance.anim.SetBool("sitting", value: true);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3f);
		float t = 0f;
		while (sitting)
		{
			float t2 = Mathf.Clamp(t / timeToSpeedUp, 0f, 1f);
			float num = Mathf.Lerp(minSunSpeed, maxSunSpeed, t2);
			sun.transform.Rotate(Vector3.left * num * Time.deltaTime, Space.Self);
			yield return null;
			t += Time.deltaTime;
		}
		PlayerController.instance.anim.SetBool("sitting", value: false);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
		PlayerController.instance.rb.isKinematic = false;
		PlayerController.instance.blockers.Remove(this);
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (sitting && moveAction.ReadValue<Vector2>().magnitude > 0.5f)
		{
			sitting = false;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Checkpoint
using System;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class Checkpoint : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform respawnPt;

	public UnityEvent onCheckpointReached;

	public UnityEvent onCheckpointUnreached;

	private void Start()
	{
		int num = Array.IndexOf(SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints, this);
		if (num != -1 && PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint == num)
		{
			onCheckpointReached.Invoke();
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (!(other.gameObject == PlayerController.instance.gameObject))
		{
			return;
		}
		int num = Array.IndexOf(SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints, this);
		if (num < 0 || num == PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint)
		{
			return;
		}
		int checkpoint = PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint;
		if (checkpoint >= 0 && SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length > checkpoint)
		{
			SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints[checkpoint].onCheckpointUnreached.Invoke();
		}
		onCheckpointReached.Invoke();
		PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint = num;
		if (GameManager.instance.replayMode)
		{
			if (GameManager.instance.currentLevel >= PlayerData.activeFile.levelReached && num >= PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint)
			{
				GameManager.instance.replayMode = false;
				GameManager.instance.Save();
			}
		}
		else
		{
			GameManager.instance.Save();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// CoconutLauncher
using System;
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class CoconutLauncher : MonoBehaviour
{
	[Serializable]
	public struct CoconutLaunchSource
	{
		public Vector3 relativeLaunchVelocity;

		public FlyingCoconut coconut;
	}

	public struct CoconutState
	{
		public Transform parent;

		public Vector3 localPos;

		public Quaternion localRot;

		public bool launched;
	}

	public Animator anim;

	public CoconutLaunchSource[] coconuts;

	public float launchDelay = 0.05f;

	public float hitGroundDelay = 0.1f;

	public float coconutGrowTime = 0.8f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float fallenTime = 0.7f;

	public UnityEvent onHitGround;

	private CoconutState[] coconutStates;

	private void Start()
	{
		coconutStates = new CoconutState[coconuts.Length];
		for (int i = 0; i < coconuts.Length; i++)
		{
			coconutStates[i] = new CoconutState
			{
				parent = coconuts[i].coconut.transform.parent,
				localPos = coconuts[i].coconut.transform.localPosition,
				localRot = coconuts[i].coconut.transform.localRotation,
				launched = false
			};
		}
	}

	public void Launch()
	{
		CoconutState[] array = coconutStates;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			if (array[i].launched)
			{
				return;
			}
		}
		StartCoroutine(DoLaunch());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoLaunch()
	{
		anim.SetBool("fallen", value: true);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(launchDelay);
		for (int i = 0; i < coconuts.Length; i++)
		{
			coconuts[i].coconut.Launch(base.transform.TransformDirection(coconuts[i].relativeLaunchVelocity.normalized).normalized * coconuts[i].relativeLaunchVelocity.magnitude, this);
			coconutStates[i].launched = true;
		}
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(hitGroundDelay - launchDelay);
		onHitGround.Invoke();
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(fallenTime - 0.1f);
		anim.SetBool("fallen", value: false);
	}

	public void ReturnCoconut(FlyingCoconut coconut)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < coconuts.Length; i++)
		{
			if (coconuts[i].coconut == coconut)
			{
				StartCoroutine(GrowCoconut(i));
				break;
			}
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator GrowCoconut(int index)
	{
		FlyingCoconut coconut = coconuts[index].coconut;
		coconut.col.enabled = false;
		coconut.transform.DOScale(0.01f, 0.5f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.5f);
		coconut.enabled = false;
		coconut.rb.isKinematic = true;
		coconut.transform.SetParent(coconutStates[index].parent);
		coconut.transform.localPosition = coconutStates[index].localPos;
		coconut.transform.localRotation = coconutStates[index].localRot;
		coconut.transform.localScale = Vector3.one * 0.01f;
		coconut.transform.DOScale(Vector3.one, coconutGrowTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(coconutGrowTime);
		coconutStates[index].launched = false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Coin
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class Coin : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private string coinId;

	[SerializeField]
	private AudioSource aud;

	[SerializeField]
	private AnimationCurve heightCurve;

	[SerializeField]
	private float maxHeight = 30f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float ascendTime = 2f;

	private bool collected;

	private void Start()
	{
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.coinsCollected.Contains(coinId))
		{
			Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
		}
	}

	public void Collect()
	{
		if (!collected)
		{
			StartCoroutine(DoCollect());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoCollect()
	{
		if (!PlayerData.activeFile.coinsCollected.Contains(coinId))
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.coinsCollected.Add(coinId);
			PlayerData.activeFile.coinCount++;
		}
		aud.Play();
		float startHeight = base.transform.position.y;
		for (float t = 0f; t < ascendTime; t += Time.deltaTime)
		{
			base.transform.position = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, startHeight + heightCurve.Evaluate(t / ascendTime) * maxHeight, base.transform.position.z);
			yield return null;
		}
		Object.Destroy(base.transform.root.gameObject);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// CowerLoop
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class CowerLoop : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Animator playerAnim;

	[SerializeField]
	private PunchTree tree1;

	[SerializeField]
	private PunchTree tree2;

	[SerializeField]
	private float timeBetweenPunches;

	[SerializeField]
	private AudioSource aud;

	[SerializeField]
	private ParticleSystem ps1;

	[SerializeField]
	private ParticleSystem ps2;

	private IEnumerator Start()
	{
		playerAnim.SetBool("cower", value: true);
		bool secondTree = false;
		while (true)
		{
			PunchTree obj = (secondTree ? tree2 : tree1);
			ParticleSystem ps = (secondTree ? ps2 : ps1);
			obj.DoGroundPunch();
			secondTree = !secondTree;
			aud.Play();
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.08f);
			playerAnim.SetTrigger("takeHit");
			ps.Play();
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(timeBetweenPunches - 0.08f);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// CustomButton
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;
using UnityEngine.EventSystems;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class CustomButton : Selectable, IPointerClickHandler, IEventSystemHandler, ISubmitHandler, IPointerEnterHandler
{
	public float scaleTime = 0.3f;

	public float selectScale = 1.2f;

	public UnityEvent onPress;

	public UnityEvent onSelect;

	public static bool lastSelectedWithMouse;

	public void OnPointerClick(PointerEventData eventData)
	{
		onPress.Invoke();
	}

	public void OnSubmit(BaseEventData eventData)
	{
		onPress.Invoke();
	}

	public override void OnSelect(BaseEventData eventData)
	{
		base.OnSelect(eventData);
		onSelect.Invoke();
		base.transform.DOScale(selectScale, scaleTime).SetUpdate(isIndependentUpdate: true);
		GameManager.instance?.menuNavSound?.Play();
		lastSelectedWithMouse = false;
	}

	public override void OnDeselect(BaseEventData eventData)
	{
		base.OnDeselect(eventData);
		base.transform.DOScale(1f, scaleTime).SetUpdate(isIndependentUpdate: true);
	}

	protected override void OnDisable()
	{
		base.OnDisable();
		DOTween.Kill(base.transform);
		base.transform.localScale = Vector3.one;
	}

	public override void OnPointerEnter(PointerEventData pointerEventData)
	{
		Select();
		lastSelectedWithMouse = true;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// DeathRagdoll
using RootMotion.Dynamics;
using UnityEngine;

public class DeathRagdoll : MonoBehaviour
{
	public PuppetMaster puppet;

	public Rigidbody[] rigidbodies;

	public Rigidbody accessory;

	public void RagdollIn()
	{
		//IL_0007: Unknown result type (might be due to invalid IL or missing references)
		puppet.state = (State)1;
	}

	public void AddForce(Vector3 force, bool cancelPrevVelocity = false)
	{
		Rigidbody[] array = rigidbodies;
		foreach (Rigidbody rigidbody in array)
		{
			if (cancelPrevVelocity)
			{
				rigidbody.linearVelocity = Vector3.zero;
			}
			rigidbody.AddForce(force, ForceMode.VelocityChange);
		}
		if (accessory != null && accessory.gameObject.activeInHierarchy)
		{
			accessory.AddForce(force * 0.8f, ForceMode.VelocityChange);
		}
	}

	public void AddExplosionForce(Vector3 source, float force, float radius, float upwardsModifier = 1f)
	{
		Rigidbody[] array = rigidbodies;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			array[i].AddExplosionForce(force, source, radius, upwardsModifier);
		}
		if (accessory != null && accessory.gameObject.activeInHierarchy)
		{
			accessory.AddExplosionForce(force / 20f, source, radius, upwardsModifier);
		}
	}
}
