// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// DynamicBone
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Threading;
using UnityEngine;

[AddComponentMenu("Dynamic Bone/Dynamic Bone")]
public class DynamicBone : MonoBehaviour
{
	public enum UpdateMode
	{
		Normal,
		AnimatePhysics,
		UnscaledTime,
		Default
	}

	public enum FreezeAxis
	{
		None,
		X,
		Y,
		Z
	}

	private class Particle
	{
		public Transform m_Transform;

		public int m_ParentIndex;

		public int m_ChildCount;

		public float m_Damping;

		public float m_Elasticity;

		public float m_Stiffness;

		public float m_Inert;

		public float m_Friction;

		public float m_Radius;

		public float m_BoneLength;

		public bool m_isCollide;

		public bool m_TransformNotNull;

		public Vector3 m_Position;

		public Vector3 m_PrevPosition;

		public Vector3 m_EndOffset;

		public Vector3 m_InitLocalPosition;

		public Quaternion m_InitLocalRotation;

		public Vector3 m_TransformPosition;

		public Vector3 m_TransformLocalPosition;

		public Matrix4x4 m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix;
	}

	private class ParticleTree
	{
		public Transform m_Root;

		public Vector3 m_LocalGravity;

		public Matrix4x4 m_RootWorldToLocalMatrix;

		public float m_BoneTotalLength;

		public List<Particle> m_Particles = new List<Particle>();

		public Vector3 m_RestGravity;
	}

	[Tooltip("The roots of the transform hierarchy to apply physics.")]
	public Transform m_Root;

	public List<Transform> m_Roots;

	[Tooltip("Internal physics simulation rate.")]
	public float m_UpdateRate = 60f;

	public UpdateMode m_UpdateMode = UpdateMode.Default;

	[Tooltip("How much the bones slowed down.")]
	[Range(0f, 1f)]
	public float m_Damping = 0.1f;

	public AnimationCurve m_DampingDistrib;

	[Tooltip("How much the force applied to return each bone to original orientation.")]
	[Range(0f, 1f)]
	public float m_Elasticity = 0.1f;

	public AnimationCurve m_ElasticityDistrib;

	[Tooltip("How much bone's original orientation are preserved.")]
	[Range(0f, 1f)]
	public float m_Stiffness = 0.1f;

	public AnimationCurve m_StiffnessDistrib;

	[Tooltip("How much character's position change is ignored in physics simulation.")]
	[Range(0f, 1f)]
	public float m_Inert;

	public AnimationCurve m_InertDistrib;

	[Tooltip("How much the bones slowed down when collide.")]
	public float m_Friction;

	public AnimationCurve m_FrictionDistrib;

	[Tooltip("Each bone can be a sphere to collide with colliders. Radius describe sphere's size.")]
	public float m_Radius;

	public AnimationCurve m_RadiusDistrib;

	[Tooltip("If End Length is not zero, an extra bone is generated at the end of transform hierarchy.")]
	public float m_EndLength;

	[Tooltip("If End Offset is not zero, an extra bone is generated at the end of transform hierarchy.")]
	public Vector3 m_EndOffset = Vector3.zero;

	[Tooltip("The force apply to bones. Partial force apply to character's initial pose is cancelled out.")]
	public Vector3 m_Gravity = Vector3.zero;

	[Tooltip("The force apply to bones.")]
	public Vector3 m_Force = Vector3.zero;

	[Tooltip("Control how physics blends with existing animation.")]
	[Range(0f, 1f)]
	public float m_BlendWeight = 1f;

	[Tooltip("Collider objects interact with the bones.")]
	public List<DynamicBoneColliderBase> m_Colliders;

	[Tooltip("Bones exclude from physics simulation.")]
	public List<Transform> m_Exclusions;

	[Tooltip("Constrain bones to move on specified plane.")]
	public FreezeAxis m_FreezeAxis;

	[Tooltip("Disable physics simulation automatically if character is far from camera or player.")]
	public bool m_DistantDisable;

	public Transform m_ReferenceObject;

	public float m_DistanceToObject = 20f;

	[HideInInspector]
	public bool m_Multithread = true;

	private Vector3 m_ObjectMove;

	private Vector3 m_ObjectPrevPosition;

	private float m_ObjectScale;

	private float m_Time;

	private float m_Weight = 1f;

	private bool m_DistantDisabled;

	private int m_PreUpdateCount;

	private List<ParticleTree> m_ParticleTrees = new List<ParticleTree>();

	private float m_DeltaTime;

	private List<DynamicBoneColliderBase> m_EffectiveColliders;

	private bool m_WorkAdded;

	private static List<DynamicBone> s_PendingWorks = new List<DynamicBone>();

	private static List<DynamicBone> s_EffectiveWorks = new List<DynamicBone>();

	private static AutoResetEvent s_AllWorksDoneEvent;

	private static int s_RemainWorkCount;

	private static Semaphore s_WorkQueueSemaphore;

	private static int s_WorkQueueIndex;

	private static int s_UpdateCount;

	private static int s_PrepareFrame;

	private void Start()
	{
		SetupParticles();
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (m_UpdateMode == UpdateMode.AnimatePhysics)
		{
			PreUpdate();
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (m_UpdateMode != UpdateMode.AnimatePhysics)
		{
			PreUpdate();
		}
		if (m_PreUpdateCount > 0 && m_Multithread)
		{
			AddPendingWork(this);
			m_WorkAdded = true;
		}
		s_UpdateCount++;
	}

	private void LateUpdate()
	{
		if (m_PreUpdateCount == 0)
		{
			return;
		}
		if (s_UpdateCount > 0)
		{
			s_UpdateCount = 0;
			s_PrepareFrame++;
		}
		SetWeight(m_BlendWeight);
		if (m_WorkAdded)
		{
			m_WorkAdded = false;
			ExecuteWorks();
		}
		else
		{
			CheckDistance();
			if (IsNeedUpdate())
			{
				Prepare();
				UpdateParticles();
				ApplyParticlesToTransforms();
			}
		}
		m_PreUpdateCount = 0;
	}

	private void Prepare()
	{
		m_DeltaTime = Time.deltaTime;
		if (m_UpdateMode == UpdateMode.UnscaledTime)
		{
			m_DeltaTime = Time.unscaledDeltaTime;
		}
		else if (m_UpdateMode == UpdateMode.AnimatePhysics)
		{
			m_DeltaTime = Time.fixedDeltaTime * (float)m_PreUpdateCount;
		}
		m_ObjectScale = Mathf.Abs(base.transform.lossyScale.x);
		m_ObjectMove = base.transform.position - m_ObjectPrevPosition;
		m_ObjectPrevPosition = base.transform.position;
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			ParticleTree particleTree = m_ParticleTrees[i];
			particleTree.m_RestGravity = particleTree.m_Root.TransformDirection(particleTree.m_LocalGravity);
			for (int j = 0; j < particleTree.m_Particles.Count; j++)
			{
				Particle particle = particleTree.m_Particles[j];
				if (particle.m_TransformNotNull)
				{
					particle.m_TransformPosition = particle.m_Transform.position;
					particle.m_TransformLocalPosition = particle.m_Transform.localPosition;
					particle.m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix = particle.m_Transform.localToWorldMatrix;
				}
			}
		}
		if (m_EffectiveColliders != null)
		{
			m_EffectiveColliders.Clear();
		}
		if (m_Colliders == null)
		{
			return;
		}
		for (int k = 0; k < m_Colliders.Count; k++)
		{
			DynamicBoneColliderBase dynamicBoneColliderBase = m_Colliders[k];
			if (dynamicBoneColliderBase != null && dynamicBoneColliderBase.enabled)
			{
				if (m_EffectiveColliders == null)
				{
					m_EffectiveColliders = new List<DynamicBoneColliderBase>();
				}
				m_EffectiveColliders.Add(dynamicBoneColliderBase);
				if (dynamicBoneColliderBase.PrepareFrame != s_PrepareFrame)
				{
					dynamicBoneColliderBase.Prepare();
					dynamicBoneColliderBase.PrepareFrame = s_PrepareFrame;
				}
			}
		}
	}

	private bool IsNeedUpdate()
	{
		if (m_Weight > 0f)
		{
			if (m_DistantDisable)
			{
				return !m_DistantDisabled;
			}
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	private void PreUpdate()
	{
		if (IsNeedUpdate())
		{
			InitTransforms();
		}
		m_PreUpdateCount++;
	}

	private void CheckDistance()
	{
		if (!m_DistantDisable)
		{
			return;
		}
		Transform referenceObject = m_ReferenceObject;
		if (referenceObject == null && Camera.main != null)
		{
			referenceObject = Camera.main.transform;
		}
		if (!(referenceObject != null))
		{
			return;
		}
		bool flag = (referenceObject.position - base.transform.position).sqrMagnitude > m_DistanceToObject * m_DistanceToObject;
		if (flag != m_DistantDisabled)
		{
			if (!flag)
			{
				ResetParticlesPosition();
			}
			m_DistantDisabled = flag;
		}
	}

	private void OnEnable()
	{
		ResetParticlesPosition();
	}

	private void OnDisable()
	{
		InitTransforms();
	}

	private void OnValidate()
	{
		m_UpdateRate = Mathf.Max(m_UpdateRate, 0f);
		m_Damping = Mathf.Clamp01(m_Damping);
		m_Elasticity = Mathf.Clamp01(m_Elasticity);
		m_Stiffness = Mathf.Clamp01(m_Stiffness);
		m_Inert = Mathf.Clamp01(m_Inert);
		m_Friction = Mathf.Clamp01(m_Friction);
		m_Radius = Mathf.Max(m_Radius, 0f);
		if (Application.isEditor && Application.isPlaying)
		{
			if (IsRootChanged())
			{
				InitTransforms();
				SetupParticles();
			}
			else
			{
				UpdateParameters();
			}
		}
	}

	private bool IsRootChanged()
	{
		List<Transform> list = new List<Transform>();
		if (m_Root != null)
		{
			list.Add(m_Root);
		}
		if (m_Roots != null)
		{
			foreach (Transform root in m_Roots)
			{
				if (root != null && !list.Contains(root))
				{
					list.Add(root);
				}
			}
		}
		if (list.Count != m_ParticleTrees.Count)
		{
			return true;
		}
		for (int i = 0; i < list.Count; i++)
		{
			if (list[i] != m_ParticleTrees[i].m_Root)
			{
				return true;
			}
		}
		return false;
	}

	private void OnDidApplyAnimationProperties()
	{
		UpdateParameters();
	}

	private void OnDrawGizmosSelected()
	{
		if (base.enabled)
		{
			if (Application.isEditor && !Application.isPlaying && base.transform.hasChanged)
			{
				SetupParticles();
			}
			Gizmos.color = Color.white;
			for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
			{
				DrawGizmos(m_ParticleTrees[i]);
			}
		}
	}

	private void DrawGizmos(ParticleTree pt)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			if (particle.m_ParentIndex >= 0)
			{
				Particle particle2 = pt.m_Particles[particle.m_ParentIndex];
				Gizmos.DrawLine(particle.m_Position, particle2.m_Position);
			}
			if (particle.m_Radius > 0f)
			{
				Gizmos.DrawWireSphere(particle.m_Position, particle.m_Radius * m_ObjectScale);
			}
		}
	}

	public void SetWeight(float w)
	{
		if (m_Weight != w)
		{
			if (w == 0f)
			{
				InitTransforms();
			}
			else if (m_Weight == 0f)
			{
				ResetParticlesPosition();
			}
			m_Weight = (m_BlendWeight = w);
		}
	}

	public float GetWeight()
	{
		return m_Weight;
	}

	private void UpdateParticles()
	{
		if (m_ParticleTrees.Count <= 0)
		{
			return;
		}
		int num = 1;
		float timeVar = 1f;
		float deltaTime = m_DeltaTime;
		if (m_UpdateMode == UpdateMode.Default)
		{
			if (m_UpdateRate > 0f)
			{
				timeVar = deltaTime * m_UpdateRate;
			}
		}
		else if (m_UpdateRate > 0f)
		{
			float num2 = 1f / m_UpdateRate;
			m_Time += deltaTime;
			num = 0;
			while (m_Time >= num2)
			{
				m_Time -= num2;
				if (++num >= 3)
				{
					m_Time = 0f;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		if (num > 0)
		{
			for (int i = 0; i < num; i++)
			{
				UpdateParticles1(timeVar, i);
				UpdateParticles2(timeVar);
			}
		}
		else
		{
			SkipUpdateParticles();
		}
	}

	public void SetupParticles()
	{
		m_ParticleTrees.Clear();
		if (m_Root != null)
		{
			AppendParticleTree(m_Root);
		}
		if (m_Roots != null)
		{
			for (int i = 0; i < m_Roots.Count; i++)
			{
				Transform root = m_Roots[i];
				if (!(root == null) && !m_ParticleTrees.Exists((ParticleTree x) => x.m_Root == root))
				{
					AppendParticleTree(root);
				}
			}
		}
		m_ObjectScale = Mathf.Abs(base.transform.lossyScale.x);
		m_ObjectPrevPosition = base.transform.position;
		m_ObjectMove = Vector3.zero;
		for (int num = 0; num < m_ParticleTrees.Count; num++)
		{
			ParticleTree particleTree = m_ParticleTrees[num];
			AppendParticles(particleTree, particleTree.m_Root, -1, 0f);
		}
		UpdateParameters();
	}

	private void AppendParticleTree(Transform root)
	{
		if (!(root == null))
		{
			ParticleTree particleTree = new ParticleTree();
			particleTree.m_Root = root;
			particleTree.m_RootWorldToLocalMatrix = root.worldToLocalMatrix;
			m_ParticleTrees.Add(particleTree);
		}
	}

	private void AppendParticles(ParticleTree pt, Transform b, int parentIndex, float boneLength)
	{
		Particle particle = new Particle();
		particle.m_Transform = b;
		particle.m_TransformNotNull = b != null;
		particle.m_ParentIndex = parentIndex;
		if (b != null)
		{
			particle.m_Position = (particle.m_PrevPosition = b.position);
			particle.m_InitLocalPosition = b.localPosition;
			particle.m_InitLocalRotation = b.localRotation;
		}
		else
		{
			Transform transform = pt.m_Particles[parentIndex].m_Transform;
			if (m_EndLength > 0f)
			{
				Transform parent = transform.parent;
				if (parent != null)
				{
					particle.m_EndOffset = transform.InverseTransformPoint(transform.position * 2f - parent.position) * m_EndLength;
				}
				else
				{
					particle.m_EndOffset = new Vector3(m_EndLength, 0f, 0f);
				}
			}
			else
			{
				particle.m_EndOffset = transform.InverseTransformPoint(base.transform.TransformDirection(m_EndOffset) + transform.position);
			}
			particle.m_Position = (particle.m_PrevPosition = transform.TransformPoint(particle.m_EndOffset));
			particle.m_InitLocalPosition = Vector3.zero;
			particle.m_InitLocalRotation = Quaternion.identity;
		}
		if (parentIndex >= 0)
		{
			boneLength += (pt.m_Particles[parentIndex].m_Transform.position - particle.m_Position).magnitude;
			particle.m_BoneLength = boneLength;
			pt.m_BoneTotalLength = Mathf.Max(pt.m_BoneTotalLength, boneLength);
			pt.m_Particles[parentIndex].m_ChildCount++;
		}
		int count = pt.m_Particles.Count;
		pt.m_Particles.Add(particle);
		if (!(b != null))
		{
			return;
		}
		for (int i = 0; i < b.childCount; i++)
		{
			Transform child = b.GetChild(i);
			bool flag = false;
			if (m_Exclusions != null)
			{
				flag = m_Exclusions.Contains(child);
			}
			if (!flag)
			{
				AppendParticles(pt, child, count, boneLength);
			}
			else if (m_EndLength > 0f || m_EndOffset != Vector3.zero)
			{
				AppendParticles(pt, null, count, boneLength);
			}
		}
		if (b.childCount == 0 && (m_EndLength > 0f || m_EndOffset != Vector3.zero))
		{
			AppendParticles(pt, null, count, boneLength);
		}
	}

	public void UpdateParameters()
	{
		SetWeight(m_BlendWeight);
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			UpdateParameters(m_ParticleTrees[i]);
		}
	}

	private void UpdateParameters(ParticleTree pt)
	{
		pt.m_LocalGravity = pt.m_RootWorldToLocalMatrix.MultiplyVector(m_Gravity).normalized * m_Gravity.magnitude;
		for (int i = 0; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			particle.m_Damping = m_Damping;
			particle.m_Elasticity = m_Elasticity;
			particle.m_Stiffness = m_Stiffness;
			particle.m_Inert = m_Inert;
			particle.m_Friction = m_Friction;
			particle.m_Radius = m_Radius;
			if (pt.m_BoneTotalLength > 0f)
			{
				float time = particle.m_BoneLength / pt.m_BoneTotalLength;
				if (m_DampingDistrib != null && m_DampingDistrib.keys.Length != 0)
				{
					particle.m_Damping *= m_DampingDistrib.Evaluate(time);
				}
				if (m_ElasticityDistrib != null && m_ElasticityDistrib.keys.Length != 0)
				{
					particle.m_Elasticity *= m_ElasticityDistrib.Evaluate(time);
				}
				if (m_StiffnessDistrib != null && m_StiffnessDistrib.keys.Length != 0)
				{
					particle.m_Stiffness *= m_StiffnessDistrib.Evaluate(time);
				}
				if (m_InertDistrib != null && m_InertDistrib.keys.Length != 0)
				{
					particle.m_Inert *= m_InertDistrib.Evaluate(time);
				}
				if (m_FrictionDistrib != null && m_FrictionDistrib.keys.Length != 0)
				{
					particle.m_Friction *= m_FrictionDistrib.Evaluate(time);
				}
				if (m_RadiusDistrib != null && m_RadiusDistrib.keys.Length != 0)
				{
					particle.m_Radius *= m_RadiusDistrib.Evaluate(time);
				}
			}
			particle.m_Damping = Mathf.Clamp01(particle.m_Damping);
			particle.m_Elasticity = Mathf.Clamp01(particle.m_Elasticity);
			particle.m_Stiffness = Mathf.Clamp01(particle.m_Stiffness);
			particle.m_Inert = Mathf.Clamp01(particle.m_Inert);
			particle.m_Friction = Mathf.Clamp01(particle.m_Friction);
			particle.m_Radius = Mathf.Max(particle.m_Radius, 0f);
		}
	}

	private void InitTransforms()
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			InitTransforms(m_ParticleTrees[i]);
		}
	}

	private void InitTransforms(ParticleTree pt)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			if (particle.m_TransformNotNull)
			{
				particle.m_Transform.localPosition = particle.m_InitLocalPosition;
				particle.m_Transform.localRotation = particle.m_InitLocalRotation;
			}
		}
	}

	private void ResetParticlesPosition()
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			ResetParticlesPosition(m_ParticleTrees[i]);
		}
		m_ObjectPrevPosition = base.transform.position;
	}

	private void ResetParticlesPosition(ParticleTree pt)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			if (particle.m_TransformNotNull)
			{
				particle.m_Position = (particle.m_PrevPosition = particle.m_Transform.position);
			}
			else
			{
				Transform transform = pt.m_Particles[particle.m_ParentIndex].m_Transform;
				particle.m_Position = (particle.m_PrevPosition = transform.TransformPoint(particle.m_EndOffset));
			}
			particle.m_isCollide = false;
		}
	}

	private void UpdateParticles1(float timeVar, int loopIndex)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			UpdateParticles1(m_ParticleTrees[i], timeVar, loopIndex);
		}
	}

	private void UpdateParticles1(ParticleTree pt, float timeVar, int loopIndex)
	{
		Vector3 gravity = m_Gravity;
		Vector3 normalized = m_Gravity.normalized;
		Vector3 vector = normalized * Mathf.Max(Vector3.Dot(pt.m_RestGravity, normalized), 0f);
		gravity -= vector;
		gravity = (gravity + m_Force) * (m_ObjectScale * timeVar);
		Vector3 vector2 = ((loopIndex == 0) ? m_ObjectMove : Vector3.zero);
		for (int i = 0; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			if (particle.m_ParentIndex >= 0)
			{
				Vector3 vector3 = particle.m_Position - particle.m_PrevPosition;
				Vector3 vector4 = vector2 * particle.m_Inert;
				particle.m_PrevPosition = particle.m_Position + vector4;
				float num = particle.m_Damping;
				if (particle.m_isCollide)
				{
					num += particle.m_Friction;
					if (num > 1f)
					{
						num = 1f;
					}
					particle.m_isCollide = false;
				}
				particle.m_Position += vector3 * (1f - num) + gravity + vector4;
			}
			else
			{
				particle.m_PrevPosition = particle.m_Position;
				particle.m_Position = particle.m_TransformPosition;
			}
		}
	}

	private void UpdateParticles2(float timeVar)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			UpdateParticles2(m_ParticleTrees[i], timeVar);
		}
	}

	private void UpdateParticles2(ParticleTree pt, float timeVar)
	{
		Plane plane = default(Plane);
		for (int i = 1; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			Particle particle2 = pt.m_Particles[particle.m_ParentIndex];
			float num = ((!particle.m_TransformNotNull) ? particle2.m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix.MultiplyVector(particle.m_EndOffset).magnitude : (particle2.m_TransformPosition - particle.m_TransformPosition).magnitude);
			float num2 = Mathf.Lerp(1f, particle.m_Stiffness, m_Weight);
			if (num2 > 0f || particle.m_Elasticity > 0f)
			{
				Matrix4x4 transformLocalToWorldMatrix = particle2.m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix;
				transformLocalToWorldMatrix.SetColumn(3, particle2.m_Position);
				Vector3 vector = ((!particle.m_TransformNotNull) ? transformLocalToWorldMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(particle.m_EndOffset) : transformLocalToWorldMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(particle.m_TransformLocalPosition));
				Vector3 vector2 = vector - particle.m_Position;
				particle.m_Position += vector2 * (particle.m_Elasticity * timeVar);
				if (num2 > 0f)
				{
					vector2 = vector - particle.m_Position;
					float magnitude = vector2.magnitude;
					float num3 = num * (1f - num2) * 2f;
					if (magnitude > num3)
					{
						particle.m_Position += vector2 * ((magnitude - num3) / magnitude);
					}
				}
			}
			if (m_EffectiveColliders != null)
			{
				float particleRadius = particle.m_Radius * m_ObjectScale;
				for (int j = 0; j < m_EffectiveColliders.Count; j++)
				{
					DynamicBoneColliderBase dynamicBoneColliderBase = m_EffectiveColliders[j];
					particle.m_isCollide |= dynamicBoneColliderBase.Collide(ref particle.m_Position, particleRadius);
				}
			}
			if (m_FreezeAxis != FreezeAxis.None)
			{
				Vector3 inNormal = particle2.m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix.GetColumn((int)(m_FreezeAxis - 1)).normalized;
				plane.SetNormalAndPosition(inNormal, particle2.m_Position);
				particle.m_Position -= plane.normal * plane.GetDistanceToPoint(particle.m_Position);
			}
			Vector3 vector3 = particle2.m_Position - particle.m_Position;
			float magnitude2 = vector3.magnitude;
			if (magnitude2 > 0f)
			{
				particle.m_Position += vector3 * ((magnitude2 - num) / magnitude2);
			}
		}
	}

	private void SkipUpdateParticles()
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			SkipUpdateParticles(m_ParticleTrees[i]);
		}
	}

	private void SkipUpdateParticles(ParticleTree pt)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			if (particle.m_ParentIndex >= 0)
			{
				particle.m_PrevPosition += m_ObjectMove;
				particle.m_Position += m_ObjectMove;
				Particle particle2 = pt.m_Particles[particle.m_ParentIndex];
				float num = ((!particle.m_TransformNotNull) ? particle2.m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix.MultiplyVector(particle.m_EndOffset).magnitude : (particle2.m_TransformPosition - particle.m_TransformPosition).magnitude);
				float num2 = Mathf.Lerp(1f, particle.m_Stiffness, m_Weight);
				if (num2 > 0f)
				{
					Matrix4x4 transformLocalToWorldMatrix = particle2.m_TransformLocalToWorldMatrix;
					transformLocalToWorldMatrix.SetColumn(3, particle2.m_Position);
					Vector3 vector = ((!particle.m_TransformNotNull) ? transformLocalToWorldMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(particle.m_EndOffset) : transformLocalToWorldMatrix.MultiplyPoint3x4(particle.m_TransformLocalPosition));
					Vector3 vector2 = vector - particle.m_Position;
					float magnitude = vector2.magnitude;
					float num3 = num * (1f - num2) * 2f;
					if (magnitude > num3)
					{
						particle.m_Position += vector2 * ((magnitude - num3) / magnitude);
					}
				}
				Vector3 vector3 = particle2.m_Position - particle.m_Position;
				float magnitude2 = vector3.magnitude;
				if (magnitude2 > 0f)
				{
					particle.m_Position += vector3 * ((magnitude2 - num) / magnitude2);
				}
			}
			else
			{
				particle.m_PrevPosition = particle.m_Position;
				particle.m_Position = particle.m_TransformPosition;
			}
		}
	}

	private static Vector3 MirrorVector(Vector3 v, Vector3 axis)
	{
		return v - axis * (Vector3.Dot(v, axis) * 2f);
	}

	private void ApplyParticlesToTransforms()
	{
		Vector3 right = Vector3.right;
		Vector3 up = Vector3.up;
		Vector3 forward = Vector3.forward;
		bool nx = false;
		bool ny = false;
		bool nz = false;
		for (int i = 0; i < m_ParticleTrees.Count; i++)
		{
			ApplyParticlesToTransforms(m_ParticleTrees[i], right, up, forward, nx, ny, nz);
		}
	}

	private void ApplyParticlesToTransforms(ParticleTree pt, Vector3 ax, Vector3 ay, Vector3 az, bool nx, bool ny, bool nz)
	{
		for (int i = 1; i < pt.m_Particles.Count; i++)
		{
			Particle particle = pt.m_Particles[i];
			Particle particle2 = pt.m_Particles[particle.m_ParentIndex];
			if (particle2.m_ChildCount <= 1)
			{
				Vector3 direction = ((!particle.m_TransformNotNull) ? particle.m_EndOffset : particle.m_Transform.localPosition);
				Vector3 fromDirection = particle2.m_Transform.TransformDirection(direction);
				Vector3 toDirection = particle.m_Position - particle2.m_Position;
				Quaternion quaternion = Quaternion.FromToRotation(fromDirection, toDirection);
				particle2.m_Transform.rotation = quaternion * particle2.m_Transform.rotation;
			}
			if (particle.m_TransformNotNull)
			{
				particle.m_Transform.position = particle.m_Position;
			}
		}
	}

	private static void AddPendingWork(DynamicBone db)
	{
		s_PendingWorks.Add(db);
	}

	private static void AddWorkToQueue(DynamicBone db)
	{
		s_WorkQueueSemaphore.Release();
	}

	private static DynamicBone GetWorkFromQueue()
	{
		int index = Interlocked.Increment(ref s_WorkQueueIndex);
		return s_EffectiveWorks[index];
	}

	private static void ThreadProc()
	{
		while (true)
		{
			s_WorkQueueSemaphore.WaitOne();
			GetWorkFromQueue().UpdateParticles();
			if (Interlocked.Decrement(ref s_RemainWorkCount) <= 0)
			{
				s_AllWorksDoneEvent.Set();
			}
		}
	}

	private static void InitThreadPool()
	{
		s_AllWorksDoneEvent = new AutoResetEvent(initialState: false);
		s_WorkQueueSemaphore = new Semaphore(0, int.MaxValue);
		int processorCount = Environment.ProcessorCount;
		for (int i = 0; i < processorCount; i++)
		{
			Thread thread = new Thread(ThreadProc);
			thread.IsBackground = true;
			thread.Start();
		}
	}

	private static void ExecuteWorks()
	{
		if (s_PendingWorks.Count <= 0)
		{
			return;
		}
		s_EffectiveWorks.Clear();
		for (int i = 0; i < s_PendingWorks.Count; i++)
		{
			DynamicBone dynamicBone = s_PendingWorks[i];
			if (dynamicBone != null && dynamicBone.enabled)
			{
				dynamicBone.CheckDistance();
				if (dynamicBone.IsNeedUpdate())
				{
					s_EffectiveWorks.Add(dynamicBone);
				}
			}
		}
		s_PendingWorks.Clear();
		if (s_EffectiveWorks.Count > 0)
		{
			if (s_AllWorksDoneEvent == null)
			{
				InitThreadPool();
			}
			int num = (s_RemainWorkCount = s_EffectiveWorks.Count);
			s_WorkQueueIndex = -1;
			for (int j = 0; j < num; j++)
			{
				DynamicBone dynamicBone2 = s_EffectiveWorks[j];
				dynamicBone2.Prepare();
				AddWorkToQueue(dynamicBone2);
			}
			s_AllWorksDoneEvent.WaitOne();
			for (int k = 0; k < num; k++)
			{
				s_EffectiveWorks[k].ApplyParticlesToTransforms();
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// DynamicBoneCollider
using UnityEngine;

[AddComponentMenu("Dynamic Bone/Dynamic Bone Collider")]
public class DynamicBoneCollider : DynamicBoneColliderBase
{
	[Tooltip("The radius of the sphere or capsule.")]
	public float m_Radius = 0.5f;

	[Tooltip("The height of the capsule.")]
	public float m_Height;

	[Tooltip("The other radius of the capsule.")]
	public float m_Radius2;

	private float m_ScaledRadius;

	private float m_ScaledRadius2;

	private Vector3 m_C0;

	private Vector3 m_C1;

	private float m_C01Distance;

	private int m_CollideType;

	private void OnValidate()
	{
		m_Radius = Mathf.Max(m_Radius, 0f);
		m_Height = Mathf.Max(m_Height, 0f);
		m_Radius2 = Mathf.Max(m_Radius2, 0f);
	}

	public override void Prepare()
	{
		float num = Mathf.Abs(base.transform.lossyScale.x);
		float num2 = m_Height * 0.5f;
		if (m_Radius2 <= 0f || Mathf.Abs(m_Radius - m_Radius2) < 0.01f)
		{
			m_ScaledRadius = m_Radius * num;
			float num3 = num2 - m_Radius;
			if (num3 <= 0f)
			{
				m_C0 = base.transform.TransformPoint(m_Center);
				if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
				{
					m_CollideType = 0;
				}
				else
				{
					m_CollideType = 1;
				}
				return;
			}
			Vector3 center = m_Center;
			Vector3 center2 = m_Center;
			switch (m_Direction)
			{
			case Direction.X:
				center.x += num3;
				center2.x -= num3;
				break;
			case Direction.Y:
				center.y += num3;
				center2.y -= num3;
				break;
			case Direction.Z:
				center.z += num3;
				center2.z -= num3;
				break;
			}
			m_C0 = base.transform.TransformPoint(center);
			m_C1 = base.transform.TransformPoint(center2);
			m_C01Distance = (m_C1 - m_C0).magnitude;
			if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
			{
				m_CollideType = 2;
			}
			else
			{
				m_CollideType = 3;
			}
			return;
		}
		float num4 = Mathf.Max(m_Radius, m_Radius2);
		if (num2 - num4 <= 0f)
		{
			m_ScaledRadius = num4 * num;
			m_C0 = base.transform.TransformPoint(m_Center);
			if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
			{
				m_CollideType = 0;
			}
			else
			{
				m_CollideType = 1;
			}
			return;
		}
		m_ScaledRadius = m_Radius * num;
		m_ScaledRadius2 = m_Radius2 * num;
		float num5 = num2 - m_Radius;
		float num6 = num2 - m_Radius2;
		Vector3 center3 = m_Center;
		Vector3 center4 = m_Center;
		switch (m_Direction)
		{
		case Direction.X:
			center3.x += num5;
			center4.x -= num6;
			break;
		case Direction.Y:
			center3.y += num5;
			center4.y -= num6;
			break;
		case Direction.Z:
			center3.z += num5;
			center4.z -= num6;
			break;
		}
		m_C0 = base.transform.TransformPoint(center3);
		m_C1 = base.transform.TransformPoint(center4);
		m_C01Distance = (m_C1 - m_C0).magnitude;
		if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
		{
			m_CollideType = 4;
		}
		else
		{
			m_CollideType = 5;
		}
	}

	public override bool Collide(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius)
	{
		return m_CollideType switch
		{
			0 => OutsideSphere(ref particlePosition, particleRadius, m_C0, m_ScaledRadius), 
			1 => InsideSphere(ref particlePosition, particleRadius, m_C0, m_ScaledRadius), 
			2 => OutsideCapsule(ref particlePosition, particleRadius, m_C0, m_C1, m_ScaledRadius, m_C01Distance), 
			3 => InsideCapsule(ref particlePosition, particleRadius, m_C0, m_C1, m_ScaledRadius, m_C01Distance), 
			4 => OutsideCapsule2(ref particlePosition, particleRadius, m_C0, m_C1, m_ScaledRadius, m_ScaledRadius2, m_C01Distance), 
			5 => InsideCapsule2(ref particlePosition, particleRadius, m_C0, m_C1, m_ScaledRadius, m_ScaledRadius2, m_C01Distance), 
			_ => false, 
		};
	}

	private static bool OutsideSphere(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius, Vector3 sphereCenter, float sphereRadius)
	{
		float num = sphereRadius + particleRadius;
		float num2 = num * num;
		Vector3 vector = particlePosition - sphereCenter;
		float sqrMagnitude = vector.sqrMagnitude;
		if (sqrMagnitude > 0f && sqrMagnitude < num2)
		{
			float num3 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude);
			particlePosition = sphereCenter + vector * (num / num3);
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	private static bool InsideSphere(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius, Vector3 sphereCenter, float sphereRadius)
	{
		float num = sphereRadius - particleRadius;
		float num2 = num * num;
		Vector3 vector = particlePosition - sphereCenter;
		float sqrMagnitude = vector.sqrMagnitude;
		if (sqrMagnitude > num2)
		{
			float num3 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude);
			particlePosition = sphereCenter + vector * (num / num3);
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	private static bool OutsideCapsule(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius, Vector3 capsuleP0, Vector3 capsuleP1, float capsuleRadius, float dirlen)
	{
		float num = capsuleRadius + particleRadius;
		float num2 = num * num;
		Vector3 vector = capsuleP1 - capsuleP0;
		Vector3 vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP0;
		float num3 = Vector3.Dot(vector2, vector);
		if (num3 <= 0f)
		{
			float sqrMagnitude = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
			if (sqrMagnitude > 0f && sqrMagnitude < num2)
			{
				float num4 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude);
				particlePosition = capsuleP0 + vector2 * (num / num4);
				return true;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			float num5 = dirlen * dirlen;
			if (num3 >= num5)
			{
				vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP1;
				float sqrMagnitude2 = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
				if (sqrMagnitude2 > 0f && sqrMagnitude2 < num2)
				{
					float num6 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude2);
					particlePosition = capsuleP1 + vector2 * (num / num6);
					return true;
				}
			}
			else
			{
				Vector3 vector3 = vector2 - vector * (num3 / num5);
				float sqrMagnitude3 = vector3.sqrMagnitude;
				if (sqrMagnitude3 > 0f && sqrMagnitude3 < num2)
				{
					float num7 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude3);
					particlePosition += vector3 * ((num - num7) / num7);
					return true;
				}
			}
		}
		return false;
	}

	private static bool InsideCapsule(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius, Vector3 capsuleP0, Vector3 capsuleP1, float capsuleRadius, float dirlen)
	{
		float num = capsuleRadius - particleRadius;
		float num2 = num * num;
		Vector3 vector = capsuleP1 - capsuleP0;
		Vector3 vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP0;
		float num3 = Vector3.Dot(vector2, vector);
		if (num3 <= 0f)
		{
			float sqrMagnitude = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
			if (sqrMagnitude > num2)
			{
				float num4 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude);
				particlePosition = capsuleP0 + vector2 * (num / num4);
				return true;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			float num5 = dirlen * dirlen;
			if (num3 >= num5)
			{
				vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP1;
				float sqrMagnitude2 = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
				if (sqrMagnitude2 > num2)
				{
					float num6 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude2);
					particlePosition = capsuleP1 + vector2 * (num / num6);
					return true;
				}
			}
			else
			{
				Vector3 vector3 = vector2 - vector * (num3 / num5);
				float sqrMagnitude3 = vector3.sqrMagnitude;
				if (sqrMagnitude3 > num2)
				{
					float num7 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude3);
					particlePosition += vector3 * ((num - num7) / num7);
					return true;
				}
			}
		}
		return false;
	}

	private static bool OutsideCapsule2(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius, Vector3 capsuleP0, Vector3 capsuleP1, float capsuleRadius0, float capsuleRadius1, float dirlen)
	{
		Vector3 vector = capsuleP1 - capsuleP0;
		Vector3 vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP0;
		float num = Vector3.Dot(vector2, vector);
		if (num <= 0f)
		{
			float num2 = capsuleRadius0 + particleRadius;
			float num3 = num2 * num2;
			float sqrMagnitude = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
			if (sqrMagnitude > 0f && sqrMagnitude < num3)
			{
				float num4 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude);
				particlePosition = capsuleP0 + vector2 * (num2 / num4);
				return true;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			float num5 = dirlen * dirlen;
			if (num >= num5)
			{
				float num6 = capsuleRadius1 + particleRadius;
				float num7 = num6 * num6;
				vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP1;
				float sqrMagnitude2 = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
				if (sqrMagnitude2 > 0f && sqrMagnitude2 < num7)
				{
					float num8 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude2);
					particlePosition = capsuleP1 + vector2 * (num6 / num8);
					return true;
				}
			}
			else
			{
				Vector3 vector3 = vector2 - vector * (num / num5);
				float sqrMagnitude3 = vector3.sqrMagnitude;
				float num9 = Vector3.Dot(vector2, vector / dirlen);
				float num10 = Mathf.Lerp(capsuleRadius0, capsuleRadius1, num9 / dirlen) + particleRadius;
				float num11 = num10 * num10;
				if (sqrMagnitude3 > 0f && sqrMagnitude3 < num11)
				{
					float num12 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude3);
					particlePosition += vector3 * ((num10 - num12) / num12);
					return true;
				}
			}
		}
		return false;
	}

	private static bool InsideCapsule2(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius, Vector3 capsuleP0, Vector3 capsuleP1, float capsuleRadius0, float capsuleRadius1, float dirlen)
	{
		Vector3 vector = capsuleP1 - capsuleP0;
		Vector3 vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP0;
		float num = Vector3.Dot(vector2, vector);
		if (num <= 0f)
		{
			float num2 = capsuleRadius0 - particleRadius;
			float num3 = num2 * num2;
			float sqrMagnitude = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
			if (sqrMagnitude > num3)
			{
				float num4 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude);
				particlePosition = capsuleP0 + vector2 * (num2 / num4);
				return true;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			float num5 = dirlen * dirlen;
			if (num >= num5)
			{
				float num6 = capsuleRadius1 - particleRadius;
				float num7 = num6 * num6;
				vector2 = particlePosition - capsuleP1;
				float sqrMagnitude2 = vector2.sqrMagnitude;
				if (sqrMagnitude2 > num7)
				{
					float num8 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude2);
					particlePosition = capsuleP1 + vector2 * (num6 / num8);
					return true;
				}
			}
			else
			{
				Vector3 vector3 = vector2 - vector * (num / num5);
				float sqrMagnitude3 = vector3.sqrMagnitude;
				float num9 = Vector3.Dot(vector2, vector / dirlen);
				float num10 = Mathf.Lerp(capsuleRadius0, capsuleRadius1, num9 / dirlen) - particleRadius;
				float num11 = num10 * num10;
				if (sqrMagnitude3 > num11)
				{
					float num12 = Mathf.Sqrt(sqrMagnitude3);
					particlePosition += vector3 * ((num10 - num12) / num12);
					return true;
				}
			}
		}
		return false;
	}

	private void OnDrawGizmosSelected()
	{
		if (base.enabled)
		{
			Prepare();
			if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
			{
				Gizmos.color = Color.yellow;
			}
			else
			{
				Gizmos.color = Color.magenta;
			}
			switch (m_CollideType)
			{
			case 0:
			case 1:
				Gizmos.DrawWireSphere(m_C0, m_ScaledRadius);
				break;
			case 2:
			case 3:
				DrawCapsule(m_C0, m_C1, m_ScaledRadius, m_ScaledRadius);
				break;
			case 4:
			case 5:
				DrawCapsule(m_C0, m_C1, m_ScaledRadius, m_ScaledRadius2);
				break;
			}
		}
	}

	private static void DrawCapsule(Vector3 c0, Vector3 c1, float radius0, float radius1)
	{
		Gizmos.DrawLine(c0, c1);
		Gizmos.DrawWireSphere(c0, radius0);
		Gizmos.DrawWireSphere(c1, radius1);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// DynamicBoneColliderBase
using UnityEngine;

public class DynamicBoneColliderBase : MonoBehaviour
{
	public enum Direction
	{
		X,
		Y,
		Z
	}

	public enum Bound
	{
		Outside,
		Inside
	}

	[Tooltip("The axis of the capsule's height.")]
	public Direction m_Direction = Direction.Y;

	[Tooltip("The center of the sphere or capsule, in the object's local space.")]
	public Vector3 m_Center = Vector3.zero;

	[Tooltip("Constrain bones to outside bound or inside bound.")]
	public Bound m_Bound;

	public int PrepareFrame { get; set; }

	public virtual void Start()
	{
	}

	public virtual void Prepare()
	{
	}

	public virtual bool Collide(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius)
	{
		return false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// DynamicBonePlaneCollider
using UnityEngine;

[AddComponentMenu("Dynamic Bone/Dynamic Bone Plane Collider")]
public class DynamicBonePlaneCollider : DynamicBoneColliderBase
{
	private Plane m_Plane;

	private void OnValidate()
	{
	}

	public override void Prepare()
	{
		Vector3 inNormal = Vector3.up;
		switch (m_Direction)
		{
		case Direction.X:
			inNormal = base.transform.right;
			break;
		case Direction.Y:
			inNormal = base.transform.up;
			break;
		case Direction.Z:
			inNormal = base.transform.forward;
			break;
		}
		Vector3 inPoint = base.transform.TransformPoint(m_Center);
		m_Plane.SetNormalAndPosition(inNormal, inPoint);
	}

	public override bool Collide(ref Vector3 particlePosition, float particleRadius)
	{
		float distanceToPoint = m_Plane.GetDistanceToPoint(particlePosition);
		if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
		{
			if (distanceToPoint < 0f)
			{
				particlePosition -= m_Plane.normal * distanceToPoint;
				return true;
			}
		}
		else if (distanceToPoint > 0f)
		{
			particlePosition -= m_Plane.normal * distanceToPoint;
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	private void OnDrawGizmosSelected()
	{
		if (base.enabled)
		{
			Prepare();
			if (m_Bound == Bound.Outside)
			{
				Gizmos.color = Color.yellow;
			}
			else
			{
				Gizmos.color = Color.magenta;
			}
			Vector3 vector = base.transform.TransformPoint(m_Center);
			Gizmos.DrawLine(vector, vector + m_Plane.normal);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// EndCredits
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;

public class EndCredits : MonoBehaviour
{
	public GameObject startRoom;

	public CreditsPhase[] phases;

	public float startDelay = 8f;

	public GameObject finalCam;

	public GameObject finalText;

	private bool started;

	public void RollCredits()
	{
		if (!started)
		{
			started = true;
			StartCoroutine(CreditsCoroutine());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator CreditsCoroutine()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(startDelay);
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(GameManager.instance.fadeout, 1f, 0.2f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
		startRoom?.SetActive(value: false);
		CreditsPhase[] array = phases;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			CreditsPhase phase = array[i];
			phase.ui.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
			if (phase.sceneHolder != null)
			{
				phase.sceneHolder.SetActive(value: true);
			}
			PlayerController.instance.transform.parent.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			Vector3 vector = phase.warpPoint.position - PlayerController.instance.transform.position;
			Vector3 positionDelta = phase.camConfiner.bounds.ClosestPoint(GameManager.instance.cineCam.transform.position + vector) - GameManager.instance.cineCam.transform.position;
			PlayerController.instance.rb.position = phase.warpPoint.position;
			PlayerController.instance.transform.position = phase.warpPoint.position;
			GameManager.instance.cineCam.GetComponent<CinemachineConfiner3D>().BoundingVolume = phase.camConfiner;
			GameManager.instance.cineCam.OnTargetObjectWarped(PlayerController.instance.transform, positionDelta);
			GameManager.instance.ClearCamBlend();
			yield return null;
			PlayerController.instance.transform.parent.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(GameManager.instance.fadeout, 0f, 0.2f);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(phase.time);
			DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(GameManager.instance.fadeout, 1f, 0.2f);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
			phase.ui.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			if (phase.sceneHolder != null)
			{
				phase.sceneHolder.SetActive(value: false);
			}
		}
		GameManager.instance.StopTimer();
		finalCam.SetActive(value: true);
		PlayerController.instance.transform.parent.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		GameManager.instance.ClearCamBlend();
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(GameManager.instance.fadeout, 0f, 0.2f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3f);
		finalText.SetActive(value: true);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// EndScreen
using Heathen.SteamworksIntegration.API;
using Steamworks;
using TMPro;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.SceneManagement;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class EndScreen : MonoBehaviour
{
	public int sceneIndex;

	public Selectable btn;

	public GameObject baseGameMessage;

	public GameObject kaizoMessage;

	public TMP_Text deathCount;

	public TMP_Text time;

	private void Start()
	{
		btn.Select();
		deathCount.text = PlayerData.activeFile.TotalDeaths.ToString();
		time.text = PlayerData.activeFile.GetTotalTime().ToString("hh\\:mm\\:ss\\.fff");
		if (PlayerData.activeFile != null)
		{
			baseGameMessage.SetActive(!PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo);
			kaizoMessage.SetActive(PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo);
		}
		if (PlayerData.sharedData != null)
		{
			PlayerData.sharedData.kaizoModeUnlocked = true;
			GameManager.instance.SaveShared();
		}
	}

	public void Restart()
	{
		SceneManager.LoadScene(sceneIndex);
	}

	public void NewsletterLink()
	{
		Application.OpenURL("https://tykenn.games");
	}

	public void WishlistLink()
	{
		Overlay.Client.Activate(4171850u, EOverlayToStoreFlag.k_EOverlayToStoreFlag_None);
	}

	public void Quit()
	{
		Application.Quit();
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// EndSequence
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class EndSequence : MonoBehaviour
{
	public GameObject endScreen;

	public GameObject corpse;

	public CinemachineCamera cineCam;

	public Animation anim;

	public Selectable continueBtn;

	public AudioSource aud;

	private bool started;

	private bool hit;

	public void StartSequence()
	{
		PlayerController.instance.AddBlocker(this);
		base.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		StartCoroutine(DoSequence());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoSequence()
	{
		PlayerController.instance.enabled = false;
		PlayerController.instance.rb.linearVelocity = Vector3.zero;
		PlayerController.instance.anim.SetFloat("speed", 0f);
		PlayerController.instance.transform.DORotate(new Vector3(0f, 180f, 0f), 0.3f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.5f);
		PlayerController.instance.anim.CrossFade("wave_hand", 0.1f);
		started = true;
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (started && !hit && PlayerController.instance.transform.position.x - base.transform.position.x < 3f && !PlayerController.instance.dead)
		{
			GameManager.instance.musicSource.Stop();
			aud.Stop();
			endScreen.SetActive(value: true);
			continueBtn.Select();
			hit = true;
			PlayerController.instance.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			base.transform.Translate(Vector3.right * 4f, Space.World);
			GetComponent<LinearFlyTree>().enabled = false;
			corpse.SetActive(value: true);
			cineCam.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		}
	}

	public void PlayEnding()
	{
		aud.Play();
		endScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		anim.Play();
	}

	public void ToAfterlife()
	{
		GameManager.instance.fadeout.alpha = 1f;
		GameManager.instance.NextLevel();
	}

	public void StartFade()
	{
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(GameManager.instance.fadeout, 1f, 3f);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ExplodingPresent
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class ExplodingPresent : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject explosion;

	[SerializeField]
	private Material flashMaterial;

	[SerializeField]
	private AnimationCurve velocityOverTime;

	[SerializeField]
	private float maxVelocity;

	[SerializeField]
	private float lifetime = 3f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float timeBetweenFlashes = 0.75f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float flashTime = 0.2f;

	[SerializeField]
	private Rigidbody rb;

	[SerializeField]
	private Renderer[] flashRends;

	[SerializeField]
	private AudioSource aud;

	private bool detonated;

	public void Detonate()
	{
		if (!detonated)
		{
			detonated = true;
			StartCoroutine(DoDetonation());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoDetonation()
	{
		rb.isKinematic = false;
		Material baseMat = flashRends[0].sharedMaterial;
		float flashTimer = 0f;
		bool flashing = false;
		for (float t = 0f; t < lifetime; t += Time.fixedDeltaTime)
		{
			Vector3 vector = PlayerController.instance.transform.position - base.transform.position;
			vector.y = 0f;
			vector.Normalize();
			Vector3 vector2 = vector * velocityOverTime.Evaluate(t / lifetime) * maxVelocity;
			rb.linearVelocity = new Vector3(vector2.x, rb.linearVelocity.y, vector2.z);
			yield return new WaitForFixedUpdate();
			flashTimer += Time.fixedDeltaTime;
			if (flashing)
			{
				if (flashTimer >= flashTime)
				{
					flashing = false;
					flashTimer -= flashTime;
					Renderer[] array = flashRends;
					for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
					{
						array[i].sharedMaterial = baseMat;
					}
				}
			}
			else if (flashTimer >= timeBetweenFlashes)
			{
				flashing = true;
				flashTimer -= timeBetweenFlashes;
				aud.Play();
				Renderer[] array = flashRends;
				for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
				{
					array[i].sharedMaterial = flashMaterial;
				}
			}
		}
		Object.Instantiate(explosion, base.transform.position + Vector3.up, Quaternion.identity);
		Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ExplosionRagdoll
using UnityEngine;

public class ExplosionRagdoll : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private float radius = 4f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float force = 1000f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float upwardsModifier = 3f;

	private void Awake()
	{
		if (Vector3.Distance(base.transform.position, PlayerController.instance.transform.position) <= radius)
		{
			PlayerController.instance.Kill();
			PlayerController.instance.ragdoll.AddExplosionForce(base.transform.position, force, radius * 2f, upwardsModifier);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// FakeCheckpoint
using UnityEngine;

public class FakeCheckpoint : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Animator anim;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform[] growingBones;

	[SerializeField]
	private float growthPerDisplacedUnit = 0.5f;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform avoidanceField;

	private bool inRange;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = true;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = false;
		}
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (inRange)
		{
			avoidanceField.position = new Vector3(PlayerController.instance.transform.position.x, avoidanceField.position.y, PlayerController.instance.transform.position.z);
		}
		else
		{
			avoidanceField.position = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, avoidanceField.position.y, base.transform.position.z - 4f);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// FlattenTree
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class FlattenTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 flatScale;

	public float flattenTime = 0.4f;

	public float stayFlatTime = 0.4f;

	public float unflattenTime = 1f;

	public UnityEvent onFlat;

	private bool flattening;

	private Vector3 startScale;

	private void Start()
	{
		startScale = base.transform.localScale;
	}

	public void Flatten()
	{
		if (!flattening && base.enabled)
		{
			StartCoroutine(DoFlattening());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoFlattening()
	{
		flattening = true;
		ShortcutExtensions.DOScale(endValue: new Vector3(startScale.x * flatScale.x, startScale.y * flatScale.y, startScale.z * flatScale.z), target: base.transform, duration: flattenTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(flattenTime);
		onFlat.Invoke();
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(stayFlatTime);
		base.transform.DOScale(startScale, flattenTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(unflattenTime);
		flattening = false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// FlyingCoconut
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class FlyingCoconut : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Rigidbody rb;

	public Collider col;

	public AudioSource aud;

	public float maxLifetime = 10f;

	public float gravity = 1f;

	public Vector3 rotationAdjust = new Vector3(90f, 0f, 0f);

	public float impactRatio = 0.4f;

	public float upForce = 2f;

	public float nonBounceTime = 0.1f;

	public GameObject collisionEffect;

	public LayerMask killLayerMask;

	public Vector3 lastSpeed;

	public float colEnableDelay = 0.05f;

	private CoconutLauncher sourceTree;

	public void Launch(Vector3 launchVelocity, CoconutLauncher sourceTree)
	{
		this.sourceTree = sourceTree;
		rb.isKinematic = false;
		rb.linearVelocity = Vector3.zero;
		base.transform.SetParent(null, worldPositionStays: true);
		base.enabled = true;
		if (maxLifetime > 0f)
		{
			Invoke("CleanUp", maxLifetime);
		}
		SetMotion(launchVelocity);
		StartCoroutine(EnableCol());
	}

	private IEnumerator EnableCol()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(colEnableDelay);
		col.enabled = true;
	}

	public void SetMotion(Vector3 startVelocity)
	{
		Vector3 force = new Vector3(startVelocity.x - rb.linearVelocity.x, 0f, startVelocity.z - rb.linearVelocity.z);
		rb.isKinematic = false;
		rb.AddForce(force, ForceMode.VelocityChange);
		base.transform.LookAt(base.transform.position + startVelocity);
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		lastSpeed = rb.linearVelocity;
		if (!rb.isKinematic)
		{
			base.transform.LookAt(base.transform.position + rb.linearVelocity);
			base.transform.Rotate(rotationAdjust);
		}
		rb.AddForce(Vector3.down * gravity, ForceMode.Acceleration);
	}

	private void CleanUp()
	{
		sourceTree.ReturnCoconut(this);
	}

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		ContactPoint[] contacts = collision.contacts;
		for (int i = 0; i < contacts.Length; i++)
		{
			ContactPoint contactPoint = contacts[i];
			Object.Destroy(Object.Instantiate(collisionEffect, contactPoint.point, Quaternion.LookRotation(contactPoint.normal)), 5f);
			aud.volume = Mathf.Clamp(collision.relativeVelocity.magnitude / 10f, 0f, 1f);
			aud.time = 0f;
			aud.Play();
		}
		if (((1 << collision.collider.gameObject.layer) & (int)killLayerMask) != 0)
		{
			PlayerController.instance.Kill();
			Vector3 vector = new Vector3(lastSpeed.x, 0f, lastSpeed.z);
			PlayerController.instance.AddForce(vector * impactRatio + Vector3.up * upForce, cancelPrevVelocity: true);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// FlyingHeadAxe
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class FlyingHeadAxe : HeldAxe
{
	public GameObject flyingAxeHead;

	public GameObject attachedAxeHead;

	private bool broken;

	public override bool Swing()
	{
		if (!broken)
		{
			StartCoroutine(BreakOnDelay());
			broken = true;
		}
		return true;
	}

	private IEnumerator BreakOnDelay()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
		attachedAxeHead.SetActive(value: false);
		flyingAxeHead.SetActive(value: true);
		flyingAxeHead.transform.SetParent(null, worldPositionStays: true);
		PlayerData.activeFile.RecordAxeBreak(AxeType.FlyingHead);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Footsteps
using System.Linq;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.VFX;

public class Footsteps : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform[] feet;

	public GenericDictionary<string, AudioClip> clips = new GenericDictionary<string, AudioClip>();

	public VisualEffect leftFootEffect;

	public VisualEffect rightFootEffect;

	public LayerMask layerMask;

	private float stepPos = 0.2f;

	private AudioSource aud;

	private float[] lastYs;

	private AudioClip defaultClip;

	private void Start()
	{
		aud = GetComponent<AudioSource>();
		defaultClip = clips.First().Value;
		lastYs = new float[feet.Length];
		for (int i = 0; i < lastYs.Length; i++)
		{
			lastYs[i] = feet[i].position.y;
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < feet.Length; i++)
		{
			float num = feet[i].position.y - base.transform.position.y;
			if (num <= stepPos && lastYs[i] > stepPos)
			{
				AudioClip audioClip;
				if (Physics.Raycast(base.transform.position + Vector3.up * 0.5f, Vector3.down, out var hitInfo, 1f, layerMask, QueryTriggerInteraction.Ignore))
				{
					string key = hitInfo.collider.tag;
					audioClip = ((!clips.ContainsKey(key)) ? defaultClip : clips[key]);
				}
				else
				{
					audioClip = defaultClip;
				}
				if (audioClip != aud.clip)
				{
					aud.clip = audioClip;
				}
				aud.time = 0f;
				aud.Play();
				if (leftFootEffect != null && rightFootEffect != null)
				{
					((leftFootEffect.transform.position.y < rightFootEffect.transform.position.y) ? leftFootEffect : rightFootEffect).SendEvent("Burst");
				}
			}
			lastYs[i] = num;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// GameManager
using System;
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using DG.Tweening;
using Heathen.SteamworksIntegration;
using Heathen.SteamworksIntegration.API;
using MoreMountains.Feedbacks;
using SteamTools;
using TMPro;
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Audio;
using UnityEngine.Events;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem;
using UnityEngine.Rendering;
using UnityEngine.SceneManagement;
using Yarn.Unity;

public class GameManager : MonoBehaviour
{
	public GameSettings settings;

	public static GameManager instance;

	public InteractPrompt interactPrompt;

	public DialogueRunner dialogueRunner;

	public AudioMixer audioMixer;

	public AudioSource musicSource;

	public CinemachineCamera cineCam;

	public CinemachineBrain cineBrain;

	public CinemachineCamera closeCam;

	public Volume closeUpVolume;

	public GetItemUI getItemUI;

	public PauseMenu pauseMenu;

	public GameObject impactEffect;

	public AudioSource jingleSource;

	public AudioSource menuNavSound;

	public MMF_Player fadeOutFeedbacks;

	public float postDeathTime = 1f;

	public int currentLevel;

	public CanvasGroup fadeout;

	public GameObject initOnceObject;

	public bool replayMode;

	public UnityEvent onSavesLoaded;

	public GameObject hud;

	public TMP_Text timer;

	public TMP_Text deathCount;

	[NonSerialized]
	public int nextAvailableFileId;

	[NonSerialized]
	public InteractionTrigger lastInteraction;

	private List<AudioClip> musicSources = new List<AudioClip>();

	private AudioClip lastSong;

	private float lastSongTime;

	private bool receivedInteract;

	private IEnumerator GetItemCoroutine;

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool transitioning;

	public Dictionary<int, PlayerData> cloudSaves = new Dictionary<int, PlayerData>();

	private DateTime timeOfLastSave;

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool timerStarted;

	private IEnumerator timerCoroutine;

	private bool timerPaused;

	private TimeSpan unsavedPauseTotal = TimeSpan.Zero;

	private DateTime lastPausedTime;

	private void Awake()
	{
		if (instance == null)
		{
			instance = this;
			InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Pause").started += PauseMenuToggle;
			initOnceObject.SetActive(value: true);
			if (PlayerData.activeFile == null)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile = new PlayerData();
			}
			string text = PlayerPrefs.GetString("rebinds");
			if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(text))
			{
				InputSystem.actions.LoadBindingOverridesFromJson(text);
			}
			UnityEngine.Object.DontDestroyOnLoad(base.gameObject);
			InputSystem.onDeviceChange += OnDeviceChange;
			PlayerData.sharedData = new SharedData();
			InitSteam();
		}
		else
		{
			UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
		}
	}

	private void OnDestroy()
	{
		InputSystem.onDeviceChange -= OnDeviceChange;
	}

	private void OnDeviceChange(InputDevice device, InputDeviceChange change)
	{
		if (change == InputDeviceChange.Disconnected && SceneStuff.inst != null && !pauseMenu.showing)
		{
			pauseMenu.Toggle();
		}
	}

	private void Start()
	{
		pauseMenu.settingsMenu.LoadSettings();
	}

	private void PauseMenuToggle(InputAction.CallbackContext context)
	{
		if (SceneStuff.inst != null)
		{
			pauseMenu.Toggle();
		}
	}

	public void RunDialogue(string node)
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoDialogue(node));
	}

	private IEnumerator DoDialogue(string node)
	{
		PlayerController.instance.AddBlocker(dialogueRunner);
		yield return null;
		dialogueRunner.StartDialogue(node);
		while (dialogueRunner.IsDialogueRunning)
		{
			if (PlayerController.instance.dead)
			{
				yield break;
			}
			yield return null;
		}
		PlayerController.instance.RemoveBlocker(dialogueRunner);
	}

	public void GetItem(ItemSO item)
	{
		CancelGetItem();
		GetItemCoroutine = DoItemGet(item);
		StartCoroutine(GetItemCoroutine);
	}

	private IEnumerator DoItemGet(ItemSO item)
	{
		if (!item.HasItem())
		{
			PlayerController.instance.AddBlocker(item);
			closeCam.Priority = 10;
			DOTween.To(() => closeUpVolume.weight, delegate(float x)
			{
				closeUpVolume.weight = x;
			}, 1f, 0.5f);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
			getItemUI.Set(item.getMessage.GetLocalizedString());
			musicSource.Pause();
			jingleSource.Play();
			PlayerController.instance.DoGetItemPose();
			GameObject itemInst = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(item.getPrefab, PlayerController.instance.transform.position + new Vector3(0f, 3f, -1f), Quaternion.Euler(0f, 180f, 0f));
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
			receivedInteract = false;
			while (!receivedInteract)
			{
				yield return null;
			}
			DOTween.To(() => closeUpVolume.weight, delegate(float x)
			{
				closeUpVolume.weight = x;
			}, 0f, 0.5f);
			musicSource.UnPause();
			closeCam.Priority = 0;
			UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(itemInst.gameObject);
			PlayerController.instance.CancelItemPose();
			getItemUI.Hide();
			item.GetItem();
			PlayerController.instance.RemoveBlocker(item);
		}
	}

	public void SetInteractAction()
	{
		receivedInteract = true;
	}

	public void NextLevel()
	{
		if (!transitioning)
		{
			while (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= currentLevel)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
			}
			PlayerData.activeFile.times[currentLevel] += DateTime.Now - timeOfLastSave;
			timeOfLastSave = DateTime.Now;
			currentLevel++;
			PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint = -1;
			StartCoroutine(TransitionLevel(settings.levels[currentLevel].loadName));
		}
	}

	public void ToDemoEnd()
	{
		if (!transitioning)
		{
			while (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= currentLevel)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
			}
			PlayerData.activeFile.times[currentLevel] += DateTime.Now - timeOfLastSave;
			timeOfLastSave = DateTime.Now;
			SceneManager.LoadSceneAsync("end");
		}
	}

	public void JumpToLevel(string level, bool save = true)
	{
		if (!transitioning)
		{
			StartCoroutine(TransitionLevel(level, save));
		}
	}

	public void StartMusic(AudioClip clip, float volume = 1f)
	{
		if (!musicSources.Contains(clip))
		{
			musicSources.Add(clip);
			musicSource.volume = volume;
			musicSource.clip = clip;
			musicSource.time = ((clip == lastSong) ? lastSongTime : 0f);
			musicSource.Play();
		}
	}

	public void StopMusic(AudioClip clip)
	{
		if (musicSource != null && musicSources.Contains(clip))
		{
			lastSong = ((musicSources.Count > 0) ? musicSources.Last() : null);
			lastSongTime = musicSource.time;
			musicSources.Remove(clip);
			if (musicSources.Count > 0)
			{
				AudioClip clip2 = musicSources.Last();
				musicSource.clip = clip2;
				musicSource.time = 0f;
				musicSource.Play();
			}
			else
			{
				musicSource.Stop();
			}
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator TransitionLevel(string level, bool save = true)
	{
		UpdateDeathCount();
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(fadeout, 1f, 0.2f);
		transitioning = true;
		dialogueRunner.Stop();
		CancelGetItem();
		if (currentLevel > PlayerData.activeFile.levelReached)
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.levelReached = currentLevel;
		}
		if (replayMode)
		{
			if (currentLevel > PlayerData.activeFile.levelReached || (currentLevel == PlayerData.activeFile.levelReached && PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint == -1))
			{
				replayMode = false;
				if (save)
				{
					Save();
				}
			}
		}
		else if (save)
		{
			Save();
		}
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
		yield return SceneManager.LoadSceneAsync(level);
		yield return null;
		musicSource.pitch = 1f;
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(fadeout, 0f, 0.5f);
		transitioning = false;
		SceneStuff.altMusicTime = 0f;
	}

	private void CancelGetItem()
	{
		if (GetItemCoroutine != null)
		{
			StopCoroutine(GetItemCoroutine);
		}
		closeUpVolume.weight = 0f;
		closeCam.Priority = 0;
		receivedInteract = false;
		musicSource.UnPause();
		getItemUI.Hide();
	}

	public void Respawn()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoRespawn());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoRespawn()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(postDeathTime);
		fadeOutFeedbacks.PlayFeedbacks();
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
		dialogueRunner.Stop();
		PlayerData.activeFile.RecordDeath(currentLevel);
		UpdateDeathCount();
		AsyncOperation asyncOperation = SceneManager.LoadSceneAsync(SceneManager.GetActiveScene().name);
		CancelGetItem();
		yield return asyncOperation;
		yield return null;
		yield return null;
		musicSource.pitch = 1f;
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOFade(fadeout, 0f, 0.3f);
	}

	public void SaveShared()
	{
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			try
			{
				RemoteStorage.Client.FileWrite("sharedData.json", PlayerData.sharedData, Encoding.UTF8);
				return;
			}
			catch (Exception)
			{
			}
		}
		string contents = JsonUtility.ToJson(PlayerData.sharedData, prettyPrint: true);
		File.WriteAllText(Application.persistentDataPath + "/sharedData.json", contents);
	}

	public void Save()
	{
		if (!replayMode)
		{
			bool flag = false;
			while (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= currentLevel)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
				flag = true;
			}
			if (flag)
			{
				timeOfLastSave = DateTime.Now;
			}
			PlayerData.activeFile.times[currentLevel] += DateTime.Now - timeOfLastSave - unsavedPauseTotal;
			timeOfLastSave = DateTime.Now;
			unsavedPauseTotal = TimeSpan.Zero;
		}
		for (int i = 0; i < PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count; i++)
		{
			if (PlayerData.activeFile.timesSerializeable.Count <= i)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile.timesSerializeable.Add(0L);
			}
			PlayerData.activeFile.timesSerializeable[i] = PlayerData.activeFile.times[i].Ticks;
		}
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			try
			{
				if (RemoteStorage.Client.FileWrite($"save_{PlayerData.activeFile.fileId}.json", PlayerData.activeFile, Encoding.UTF8) && !cloudSaves.ContainsKey(PlayerData.activeFile.fileId))
				{
					cloudSaves.Add(PlayerData.activeFile.fileId, PlayerData.activeFile);
					nextAvailableFileId = ((cloudSaves.Count != 0) ? (cloudSaves.Keys.Max() + 1) : 0);
				}
				return;
			}
			catch (Exception)
			{
			}
		}
		string contents = JsonUtility.ToJson(PlayerData.activeFile, prettyPrint: true);
		File.WriteAllText($"{Application.persistentDataPath}/save_{PlayerData.activeFile.fileId}.json", contents);
	}

	public void Load(int fileId)
	{
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			try
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile = RemoteStorage.Client.FileReadJson<PlayerData>($"save_{fileId}.json", Encoding.UTF8);
				UpdateDeathCount();
				DeserializeTimes();
				return;
			}
			catch (Exception)
			{
			}
		}
		string path = $"{Application.persistentDataPath}/save_{fileId}.json";
		if (File.Exists(path))
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile = JsonUtility.FromJson<PlayerData>(File.ReadAllText(path));
			UpdateDeathCount();
			DeserializeTimes();
		}
	}

	private void DeserializeTimes()
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < PlayerData.activeFile.timesSerializeable.Count; i++)
		{
			if (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= i)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
			}
			PlayerData.activeFile.times[i] = new TimeSpan(PlayerData.activeFile.timesSerializeable[i]);
		}
		timeOfLastSave = DateTime.Now;
	}

	public void DeleteFile(int fileId)
	{
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			try
			{
				RemoteStorage.Client.FileDelete($"save_{fileId}.json");
				if (cloudSaves.ContainsKey(fileId))
				{
					cloudSaves.Remove(fileId);
					nextAvailableFileId = ((cloudSaves.Count != 0) ? (cloudSaves.Keys.Max() + 1) : 0);
				}
				return;
			}
			catch (Exception)
			{
				return;
			}
		}
		string path = $"{Application.persistentDataPath}/save_{fileId}.json";
		if (File.Exists(path))
		{
			File.Delete(path);
		}
	}

	[YarnCommand("specialAction")]
	public static void DoSpecialAction(string key)
	{
		if (instance.lastInteraction != null)
		{
			instance.lastInteraction.DoSpecialAction(key);
		}
	}

	[YarnFunction("hasCoin")]
	public static bool HasCoin()
	{
		return PlayerData.activeFile.coinCount > 0;
	}

	[YarnFunction("hasItem")]
	public static bool HasItem(string itemName)
	{
		return PlayerData.activeFile.otherItems.Any((string x) => x == itemName);
	}

	private void InitSteam()
	{
		Interface.Initialise();
		Interface.WhenReady(OnSteamReady);
	}

	private void OnSteamReady()
	{
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			RemoteStorage.Client.GetQuota(out var _, out var _);
			RemoteStorageFile[] files = RemoteStorage.Client.GetFiles();
			for (int i = 0; i < files.Length; i++)
			{
				RemoteStorageFile remoteStorageFile = files[i];
				if (remoteStorageFile.name == "sharedData.json")
				{
					PlayerData.sharedData = remoteStorageFile.ToJson<SharedData>();
					continue;
				}
				PlayerData playerData = remoteStorageFile.ToJson<PlayerData>();
				cloudSaves.Add(playerData.fileId, playerData);
			}
			if (cloudSaves.Count > 0)
			{
				nextAvailableFileId = ((cloudSaves.Count != 0) ? (cloudSaves.Keys.Max() + 1) : 0);
			}
			UpdateDeathCount();
		}
		onSavesLoaded.Invoke();
	}

	private void UpdateDeathCount()
	{
		deathCount.text = PlayerData.activeFile.TotalDeaths.ToString();
	}

	public void SetHUDVisible(bool visible)
	{
		bool active = visible && (deathCount.gameObject.activeSelf || timer.gameObject.activeSelf);
		hud.SetActive(active);
	}

	public void SetDeathCountVisible(bool visible)
	{
		deathCount.gameObject.SetActive(visible);
		SetHUDVisible(PlayerController.instance != null && !PlayerController.instance.blocked);
	}

	public void SetTimerVisible(bool visible)
	{
		timer.gameObject.SetActive(visible);
		SetHUDVisible(PlayerController.instance != null && !PlayerController.instance.blocked);
	}

	public void StartTimer()
	{
		timerStarted = true;
		while (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= currentLevel)
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
		}
		timeOfLastSave = DateTime.Now;
		unsavedPauseTotal = TimeSpan.Zero;
		timerPaused = false;
		if (timerCoroutine != null)
		{
			StopCoroutine(timerCoroutine);
		}
		timerCoroutine = ProgressTimer();
		StartCoroutine(timerCoroutine);
	}

	private IEnumerator ProgressTimer()
	{
		while (true)
		{
			TimeSpan zero = TimeSpan.Zero;
			for (int i = 0; i < currentLevel; i++)
			{
				while (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= i)
				{
					PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
				}
				zero += PlayerData.activeFile.times[i];
			}
			TimeSpan timeSpan = zero + PlayerData.activeFile.times[currentLevel] + (DateTime.Now - timeOfLastSave) - unsavedPauseTotal;
			timer.text = timeSpan.ToString("hh\\:mm\\:ss\\.fff");
			yield return null;
		}
	}

	public void UpdateTimeWithSaved()
	{
		TimeSpan zero = TimeSpan.Zero;
		for (int i = 0; i < currentLevel; i++)
		{
			while (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count <= i)
			{
				PlayerData.activeFile.times.Add(TimeSpan.Zero);
			}
			zero += PlayerData.activeFile.times[i];
		}
		TimeSpan timeSpan = zero;
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.times.Count > currentLevel)
		{
			timeSpan += PlayerData.activeFile.times[currentLevel];
		}
		timer.text = timeSpan.ToString("hh\\:mm\\:ss\\.fff");
	}

	public void PauseTimer()
	{
		if (!timerPaused)
		{
			timerPaused = true;
			lastPausedTime = DateTime.Now;
		}
	}

	public void UnpauseTimer()
	{
		if (timerPaused)
		{
			timerPaused = false;
			unsavedPauseTotal += DateTime.Now - lastPausedTime;
		}
	}

	public void StopTimer()
	{
		if (timerCoroutine != null)
		{
			StopCoroutine(timerCoroutine);
		}
		timerStarted = false;
	}

	public void ClearCamBlend()
	{
		cineCam.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		cineBrain.enabled = false;
		cineCam.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		cineBrain.enabled = true;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// GenericDictionary<TKey,TValue>
using System;
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

[Serializable]
public class GenericDictionary<TKey, TValue> : IDictionary<TKey, TValue>, ICollection<KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue>>, IEnumerable<KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue>>, IEnumerable, ISerializationCallbackReceiver
{
	[Serializable]
	private struct KeyValuePair(TKey Key, TValue Value)
	{
		public TKey Key = Key;

		public TValue Value = Value;
	}

	[SerializeField]
	private List<KeyValuePair> list = new List<KeyValuePair>();

	[SerializeField]
	private Dictionary<TKey, int> indexByKey = new Dictionary<TKey, int>();

	[SerializeField]
	[HideInInspector]
	private Dictionary<TKey, TValue> dict = new Dictionary<TKey, TValue>();

	[SerializeField]
	[HideInInspector]
	private bool keyCollision;

	public TValue this[TKey key]
	{
		get
		{
			return dict[key];
		}
		set
		{
			dict[key] = value;
			if (indexByKey.ContainsKey(key))
			{
				int index = indexByKey[key];
				list[index] = new KeyValuePair(key, value);
			}
			else
			{
				list.Add(new KeyValuePair(key, value));
				indexByKey.Add(key, list.Count - 1);
			}
		}
	}

	public ICollection<TKey> Keys => dict.Keys;

	public ICollection<TValue> Values => dict.Values;

	public int Count => dict.Count;

	public bool IsReadOnly { get; set; }

	public void OnBeforeSerialize()
	{
	}

	public void OnAfterDeserialize()
	{
		dict.Clear();
		indexByKey.Clear();
		keyCollision = false;
		for (int i = 0; i < list.Count; i++)
		{
			TKey key = list[i].Key;
			if (key != null && !ContainsKey(key))
			{
				dict.Add(key, list[i].Value);
				indexByKey.Add(key, i);
			}
			else
			{
				keyCollision = true;
			}
		}
	}

	public void Add(TKey key, TValue value)
	{
		dict.Add(key, value);
		list.Add(new KeyValuePair(key, value));
		indexByKey.Add(key, list.Count - 1);
	}

	public bool ContainsKey(TKey key)
	{
		return dict.ContainsKey(key);
	}

	public bool Remove(TKey key)
	{
		if (dict.Remove(key))
		{
			int num = indexByKey[key];
			list.RemoveAt(num);
			UpdateIndexes(num);
			indexByKey.Remove(key);
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	private void UpdateIndexes(int removedIndex)
	{
		for (int i = removedIndex; i < list.Count; i++)
		{
			TKey key = list[i].Key;
			indexByKey[key]--;
		}
	}

	public bool TryGetValue(TKey key, out TValue value)
	{
		return dict.TryGetValue(key, out value);
	}

	public void Add(KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue> pair)
	{
		Add(pair.Key, pair.Value);
	}

	public void Clear()
	{
		dict.Clear();
		list.Clear();
		indexByKey.Clear();
	}

	public bool Contains(KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue> pair)
	{
		if (dict.TryGetValue(pair.Key, out var value))
		{
			return EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(value, pair.Value);
		}
		return false;
	}

	public void CopyTo(KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue>[] array, int arrayIndex)
	{
		if (array == null)
		{
			throw new ArgumentException("The array cannot be null.");
		}
		if (arrayIndex < 0)
		{
			throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException("The starting array index cannot be negative.");
		}
		if (array.Length - arrayIndex < dict.Count)
		{
			throw new ArgumentException("The destination array has fewer elements than the collection.");
		}
		foreach (KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue> item in dict)
		{
			array[arrayIndex] = item;
			arrayIndex++;
		}
	}

	public bool Remove(KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue> pair)
	{
		if (dict.TryGetValue(pair.Key, out var value) && EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(value, pair.Value))
		{
			return Remove(pair.Key);
		}
		return false;
	}

	public IEnumerator<KeyValuePair<TKey, TValue>> GetEnumerator()
	{
		return dict.GetEnumerator();
	}

	IEnumerator IEnumerable.GetEnumerator()
	{
		return dict.GetEnumerator();
	}
}

// GrabTree
using UnityEngine;

public class GrabTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform grabPoint;

	public Animator anim;

	public string animTrigger;

	public float upAccelerate = 15f;

	private bool grabbing;

	public void Grab()
	{
		anim.SetTrigger(animTrigger);
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (grabbing)
		{
			PlayerController.instance.ragdoll.AddForce(Vector3.up * upAccelerate * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
		}
	}

	public void StartGrab()
	{
		PlayerController.instance.ragdoll.RagdollIn();
		grabbing = true;
	}

	public void StopGrab()
	{
		grabbing = false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// GrowAxe
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class GrowAxe : HeldAxe
{
	public float growTime = 6f;

	public float growScale = 10f;

	public ConfigurableJoint joint;

	private void Awake()
	{
		joint.connectedBody = PlayerController.instance.puppetHand.GetComponent<Rigidbody>();
		StartCoroutine(DoGrow());
	}

	public override bool Swing()
	{
		return true;
	}

	private IEnumerator DoGrow()
	{
		base.transform.DOScale(growScale, growTime).SetEase(Ease.InQuad);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(growTime);
		PlayerData.activeFile.RecordAxeBreak(AxeType.Shrink);
		PlayerController.instance.StopHoldingAxe();
	}
}

		leftHalf.SetParent(leftHand, worldPositionStays: true);
