// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// HatBtn
using System;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class HatBtn : MonoBehaviour
{
	public CustomButton button;

	public Image icon;

	public Sprite unknownIcon;

	public Image lostIcon;

	public Image selectedIcon;

	private HatSO hat;

	private HatState state = HatState.Found;

	[NonSerialized]
	public PauseMenu menu;

	public void Set(HatSO hatInfo, HatState state, bool selected)
	{
		icon.sprite = ((state == HatState.NotFound) ? unknownIcon : hatInfo.icon);
		lostIcon.gameObject.SetActive(state == HatState.Lost);
		hat = hatInfo;
		selectedIcon.gameObject.SetActive(selected);
		this.state = state;
	}

	public void OnPress()
	{
		if (state == HatState.Found)
		{
			int currentHat = ((hat == null) ? (-1) : Array.IndexOf(GameManager.instance.settings.hats, hat));
			PlayerData.activeFile.currentHat = currentHat;
			PlayerController.instance.SetHat(currentHat);
			menu.RefreshHatStates();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// HatSO
using System;
using UnityEngine;

[CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "HatSO", menuName = "Scriptable Objects/HatSO")]
public class HatSO : ItemSO
{
	public Hat prefab;

	public Vector3 hairCutoffPoint;

	public Vector3 hairCutoffNormal;

	public bool hideNose;

	public override void GetItem()
	{
		int num = Array.IndexOf(GameManager.instance.settings.hats, this);
		PlayerData.activeFile.SetHatState(this, HatState.Found);
		PlayerData.activeFile.currentHat = num;
		PlayerController.instance.SetHat(num);
	}

	public override bool HasItem()
	{
		int num = Array.IndexOf(GameManager.instance.settings.hats, this);
		return PlayerData.activeFile.hatStates[num] != HatState.NotFound;
	}
}

	Found,
	Lost

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// HatThief
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class HatThief : MonoBehaviour
{
	public UnityEvent onSteal;

	public ThiefTree tree;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		Hat componentInParent = other.GetComponentInParent<Hat>();
		if (componentInParent != null)
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.SetHatState(componentInParent.hatSO, HatState.Lost);
			componentInParent.transform.SetParent(base.transform, worldPositionStays: true);
			componentInParent.transform.DOLocalMove(Vector3.zero, 0.3f);
			componentInParent.transform.DOLocalRotate(Vector3.zero, 0.3f);
			tree.hat = componentInParent;
			onSteal.Invoke();
			PlayerData.activeFile.currentHat = -1;
			PlayerController.instance.SetHat(-1);
		}
	}
}

[Serializable]
public class HouseTileSet
{

	public GameObject wallSide;

	public GameObject wallBottomSide;

	public GameObject roofBottomCorner;

	public GameObject roofBottomSide;

	public GameObject roofFrontSide;

	public GameObject roofSide;

	public GameObject roofFrontTop;

	public GameObject roofTop;

	public GameObject PickObject(Vector3Int pos, BoundsInt bounds)
	{
		GameObject gameObject = null;
		int num = 0;
		bool flag = false;
		GameObject gameObject2 = null;
		if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y == bounds.yMin && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomCorner;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y == bounds.yMin && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomCorner;
			num = 1;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y == bounds.yMin && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomCorner;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y == bounds.yMin && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomCorner;
			num = 3;
		}
		else if (pos.z == bounds.zMin && pos.y == bounds.yMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomSide;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y == bounds.yMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomSide;
			num = 1;
		}
		else if (pos.z == bounds.zMax && pos.y == bounds.yMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomSide;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y == bounds.yMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallBottomSide;
			num = 3;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y <= bounds.yMax && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallCorner;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y <= bounds.yMax && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallCorner;
			num = 1;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y <= bounds.yMax && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallCorner;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y <= bounds.yMax && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallCorner;
			num = 3;
		}
		else if (pos.z == bounds.zMin && pos.y <= bounds.yMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallSide;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y <= bounds.yMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallSide;
			num = 1;
		}
		else if (pos.z == bounds.zMax && pos.y <= bounds.yMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallSide;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y <= bounds.yMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallSide;
			num = 3;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == bounds.xMax - pos.x && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = roofFrontTop;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == bounds.xMax - pos.x && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = roofFrontTop;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == bounds.xMax - pos.x)
		{
			gameObject = roofTop;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y == bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = roofBottomCorner;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y == bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = roofBottomCorner;
			flag = true;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y == bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = roofBottomCorner;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y == bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = roofBottomCorner;
			num = 2;
			flag = true;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMin && pos.y == bounds.yMax + 1)
		{
			gameObject = roofBottomSide;
		}
		else if (pos.x == bounds.xMax && pos.y == bounds.yMax + 1)
		{
			gameObject = roofBottomSide;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = roofFrontSide;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = roofFrontSide;
			flag = true;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == bounds.xMax - pos.x && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = roofFrontSide;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == bounds.xMax - pos.x && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = roofFrontSide;
			flag = true;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == pos.x - bounds.xMin)
		{
			gameObject = roofSide;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax + 1 && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 == bounds.xMax - pos.x)
		{
			gameObject = roofSide;
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 < pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 < bounds.xMax - pos.x && pos.z == bounds.zMin)
		{
			gameObject = wallSide;
		}
		else if (pos.y > bounds.yMax && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 < pos.x - bounds.xMin && pos.y - bounds.yMax - 1 < bounds.xMax - pos.x && pos.z == bounds.zMax)
		{
			gameObject = wallSide;
			num = 2;
		}
		if (gameObject != null)
		{
			gameObject2 = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(gameObject, Vector3.zero, Quaternion.identity);
			if (flag)
			{
				gameObject2.transform.localScale = new Vector3(1f, 1f, -1f);
			}
			gameObject2.transform.Rotate(Vector3.up * 90f * num);
		}
		return gameObject2;
	}
}

using System;
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem.Utilities;

public class InputSystem_Actions : IInputActionCollection2, IInputActionCollection, IEnumerable<InputAction>, IEnumerable, IDisposable
{
	public struct PlayerActions(InputSystem_Actions wrapper)
	{
		private InputSystem_Actions m_Wrapper = wrapper;

		public InputAction Move => m_Wrapper.m_Player_Move;

		public InputAction Interact => m_Wrapper.m_Player_Interact;

		public InputAction Pause => m_Wrapper.m_Player_Pause;

		public InputAction CharacterCreatorTurn => m_Wrapper.m_Player_CharacterCreatorTurn;

		public InputAction Chop => m_Wrapper.m_Player_Chop;

		public InputAction Teleport => m_Wrapper.m_Player_Teleport;

		public bool enabled => Get().enabled;

		public InputActionMap Get()
		{
			return m_Wrapper.m_Player;
		}

		public void Enable()
		{
			Get().Enable();
		}

		public void Disable()
		{
			Get().Disable();
		}

		public static implicit operator InputActionMap(PlayerActions set)
		{
			return set.Get();
		}

		public void AddCallbacks(IPlayerActions instance)
		{
			if (instance != null && !m_Wrapper.m_PlayerActionsCallbackInterfaces.Contains(instance))
			{
				m_Wrapper.m_PlayerActionsCallbackInterfaces.Add(instance);
				Move.started += instance.OnMove;
				Move.performed += instance.OnMove;
				Move.canceled += instance.OnMove;
				Interact.started += instance.OnInteract;
				Interact.performed += instance.OnInteract;
				Interact.canceled += instance.OnInteract;
				Pause.started += instance.OnPause;
				Pause.performed += instance.OnPause;
				Pause.canceled += instance.OnPause;
				CharacterCreatorTurn.started += instance.OnCharacterCreatorTurn;
				CharacterCreatorTurn.performed += instance.OnCharacterCreatorTurn;
				CharacterCreatorTurn.canceled += instance.OnCharacterCreatorTurn;
				Chop.started += instance.OnChop;
				Chop.performed += instance.OnChop;
				Chop.canceled += instance.OnChop;
				Teleport.started += instance.OnTeleport;
				Teleport.performed += instance.OnTeleport;
				Teleport.canceled += instance.OnTeleport;
			}
		}

		private void UnregisterCallbacks(IPlayerActions instance)
		{
			Move.started -= instance.OnMove;
			Move.performed -= instance.OnMove;
			Move.canceled -= instance.OnMove;
			Interact.started -= instance.OnInteract;
			Interact.performed -= instance.OnInteract;
			Interact.canceled -= instance.OnInteract;
			Pause.started -= instance.OnPause;
			Pause.performed -= instance.OnPause;
			Pause.canceled -= instance.OnPause;
			CharacterCreatorTurn.started -= instance.OnCharacterCreatorTurn;
			CharacterCreatorTurn.performed -= instance.OnCharacterCreatorTurn;
			CharacterCreatorTurn.canceled -= instance.OnCharacterCreatorTurn;
			Chop.started -= instance.OnChop;
			Chop.performed -= instance.OnChop;
			Chop.canceled -= instance.OnChop;
			Teleport.started -= instance.OnTeleport;
			Teleport.performed -= instance.OnTeleport;
			Teleport.canceled -= instance.OnTeleport;
		}

		public void RemoveCallbacks(IPlayerActions instance)
		{
			if (m_Wrapper.m_PlayerActionsCallbackInterfaces.Remove(instance))
			{
				UnregisterCallbacks(instance);
			}
		}

		public void SetCallbacks(IPlayerActions instance)
		{
			foreach (IPlayerActions playerActionsCallbackInterface in m_Wrapper.m_PlayerActionsCallbackInterfaces)
			{
				UnregisterCallbacks(playerActionsCallbackInterface);
			}
			m_Wrapper.m_PlayerActionsCallbackInterfaces.Clear();
			AddCallbacks(instance);
		}
	}

			Get().Disable();

				TrackedDevicePosition.started += instance.OnTrackedDevicePosition;
				TrackedDevicePosition.performed += instance.OnTrackedDevicePosition;
				TrackedDevicePosition.canceled += instance.OnTrackedDevicePosition;
				TrackedDeviceOrientation.started += instance.OnTrackedDeviceOrientation;
				TrackedDeviceOrientation.performed += instance.OnTrackedDeviceOrientation;
				TrackedDeviceOrientation.canceled += instance.OnTrackedDeviceOrientation;
			}
		}

		private void UnregisterCallbacks(IUIActions instance)
		{
			Navigate.started -= instance.OnNavigate;
			Navigate.performed -= instance.OnNavigate;
			Navigate.canceled -= instance.OnNavigate;
			Submit.started -= instance.OnSubmit;
			Submit.performed -= instance.OnSubmit;
			Submit.canceled -= instance.OnSubmit;
			Cancel.started -= instance.OnCancel;
			Cancel.performed -= instance.OnCancel;
			Cancel.canceled -= instance.OnCancel;
			Point.started -= instance.OnPoint;
			Point.performed -= instance.OnPoint;
			Point.canceled -= instance.OnPoint;
			Click.started -= instance.OnClick;
			Click.performed -= instance.OnClick;
			Click.canceled -= instance.OnClick;
			RightClick.started -= instance.OnRightClick;
			RightClick.performed -= instance.OnRightClick;
			RightClick.canceled -= instance.OnRightClick;
			MiddleClick.started -= instance.OnMiddleClick;
			MiddleClick.performed -= instance.OnMiddleClick;
			MiddleClick.canceled -= instance.OnMiddleClick;
			ScrollWheel.started -= instance.OnScrollWheel;
			ScrollWheel.performed -= instance.OnScrollWheel;
			ScrollWheel.canceled -= instance.OnScrollWheel;
			TrackedDevicePosition.started -= instance.OnTrackedDevicePosition;
			TrackedDevicePosition.performed -= instance.OnTrackedDevicePosition;
			TrackedDevicePosition.canceled -= instance.OnTrackedDevicePosition;
			TrackedDeviceOrientation.started -= instance.OnTrackedDeviceOrientation;
			TrackedDeviceOrientation.performed -= instance.OnTrackedDeviceOrientation;
			TrackedDeviceOrientation.canceled -= instance.OnTrackedDeviceOrientation;
		}

		public void RemoveCallbacks(IUIActions instance)
		{
			if (m_Wrapper.m_UIActionsCallbackInterfaces.Remove(instance))
			{
				UnregisterCallbacks(instance);
			}
		}

		public void SetCallbacks(IUIActions instance)
		{
			foreach (IUIActions uIActionsCallbackInterface in m_Wrapper.m_UIActionsCallbackInterfaces)
			{
				UnregisterCallbacks(uIActionsCallbackInterface);

		}

	public InputControlScheme KeyboardMouseScheme
	{
		get
		{
			if (m_KeyboardMouseSchemeIndex == -1)
			{
				m_KeyboardMouseSchemeIndex = asset.FindControlSchemeIndex("Keyboard&Mouse");
			}
			return asset.controlSchemes[m_KeyboardMouseSchemeIndex];
		}
	}

	public InputControlScheme GamepadScheme
	{
		get
		{
			if (m_GamepadSchemeIndex == -1)
			{
				m_GamepadSchemeIndex = asset.FindControlSchemeIndex("Gamepad");
			}
			return asset.controlSchemes[m_GamepadSchemeIndex];
		}
	}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// InteractionTrigger
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class InteractionTrigger : MonoBehaviour
{
	public UnityEvent onInteract;

	public string promptLabel = "Interact";

	public float promptHeight = 2f;

	public bool lookAt = true;

	public GenericDictionary<string, UnityEvent> specialActions;

	public void Interact()
	{
		Vector3 towards = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, PlayerController.instance.transform.position.y, base.transform.position.z);
		if (lookAt)
		{
			PlayerController.instance.transform.DOLookAt(towards, 0.2f);
		}
		GameManager.instance.lastInteraction = this;
		onInteract.Invoke();
	}

	public void DoSpecialAction(string key)
	{
		specialActions[key].Invoke();
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// InteractPrompt
using TMPro;
using UnityEngine;

public class InteractPrompt : MonoBehaviour
{
	public TMP_Text label;

	public Canvas canvas;

	private Transform target;

	private float promptHeight = 2f;

	public void Set(Transform target, string text, float promptHeight)
	{
		base.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		label.SetText(text);
		this.promptHeight = promptHeight;
		this.target = target;
		UpdatePos();
	}

	public void Hide()
	{
		target = null;
		base.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (target != null)
		{
			UpdatePos();
		}
		else
		{
			Hide();
		}
	}

	private void UpdatePos()
	{
		Vector2 screenSpace = Camera.main.WorldToScreenPoint(target.position + Vector3.up * promptHeight);
		Vector2 anchoredPosition = ScreenSpaceToUISpace(screenSpace);
		((RectTransform)base.transform).anchoredPosition = anchoredPosition;
	}

	private Vector2 ScreenSpaceToUISpace(Vector2 screenSpace)
	{
		float num = Screen.height;
		float num2 = Screen.width;
		float x = screenSpace.x - num2 / 2f;
		float y = screenSpace.y - num / 2f;
		float scaleFactor = canvas.scaleFactor;
		return new Vector2(x, y) / scaleFactor;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ItemSO
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Localization;

[CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "ItemSO", menuName = "Scriptable Objects/ItemSO")]
public class ItemSO : ScriptableObject
{
	public string displayName;

	public LocalizedString getMessage;

	public Sprite icon;

	public GameObject getPrefab;

	public virtual void GetItem()
	{
		if (!PlayerData.activeFile.otherItems.Contains(displayName))
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.otherItems.Add(displayName);
		}
	}

	public virtual bool HasItem()
	{
		return PlayerData.activeFile.otherItems.Contains(displayName);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Ladder
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class Ladder : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform top;

	public Transform bottom;

	public Vector3 topStandOffset = new Vector3(0f, 1f, 1f);

	public InteractionTrigger trigger;

	private bool climbing;

	public void StartClimbing()
	{
		climbing = true;
		PlayerController.instance.StartLaddering(this);
		trigger.enabled = false;
	}

	public void StopClimbing()
	{
		climbing = false;
		PlayerController.instance.StopLaddering();
		trigger.enabled = true;
	}

	private IEnumerator ReachTop()
	{
		climbing = false;
		PlayerController.instance.anim.SetBool("onLadder", value: false);
		PlayerController.instance.transform.DOMove(base.transform.TransformPoint(top.localPosition + topStandOffset), 0.4f);
		PlayerController.instance.AddBlocker(this);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.25f);
		PlayerController.instance.RemoveBlocker(this);
		StopClimbing();
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (climbing)
		{
			if (PlayerController.instance.transform.position.y < bottom.position.y)
			{
				StopClimbing();
			}
			else if (PlayerController.instance.transform.position.y > top.position.y)
			{
				StartCoroutine(ReachTop());
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LevelEnd
using UnityEngine;

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LevelSelect
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

public class LevelSelect : MonoBehaviour
{
	public LabeledButton levelBtn;

	public GameObject lockedBtn;

	public RectTransform[] rows;

	private List<GameObject> spawnBtns = new List<GameObject>();

	public void Set(int maxLevel, int saveIndex)
	{
		foreach (GameObject spawnBtn in spawnBtns)
		{
			Object.Destroy(spawnBtn);
		}
		spawnBtns.Clear();
		for (int i = 0; i < GameManager.instance.settings.levels.Length; i++)
		{
			LevelInfo level = GameManager.instance.settings.levels[i];
			if (i <= maxLevel)
			{
				LabeledButton labeledButton = Object.Instantiate(levelBtn, rows[level.act - 1]);
				labeledButton.label.text = level.displayName.GetLocalizedString();
				spawnBtns.Add(labeledButton.gameObject);
				labeledButton.btn.onPress.AddListener(delegate
				{
					GameManager.instance.Load(saveIndex);
					PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint = -1;
					GameManager.instance.replayMode = true;
					GameManager.instance.JumpToLevel(level.loadName);
				});
				if (i == 0)
				{
					labeledButton.btn.Select();
				}
			}
			else
			{
				GameObject item = Object.Instantiate(lockedBtn, rows[level.act - 1]);
				spawnBtns.Add(item);
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LinearFlyTree
using MoreMountains.Feedbacks;
using UnityEngine;

public class LinearFlyTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 totalChange;

	public float speed = 6f;

	public MMF_Player feedbacks;

	private bool moving = true;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	private void Awake()
	{
		startPos = base.transform.position;
	}

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		PlayerController component = collision.collider.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null && !component.dead && moving)
		{
			feedbacks.transform.SetParent(null);
			feedbacks.transform.position = collision.contacts[0].point;
			feedbacks.PlayFeedbacks();
			component.Kill();
		}
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (moving)
		{
			base.transform.position = Vector3.MoveTowards(base.transform.position, startPos + totalChange, speed * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
			if (base.transform.position == startPos + totalChange)
			{
				moving = false;
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LineTile
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

[CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "LineTile", menuName = "3D Tile/Line Tile", order = 2)]
public class LineTile : TileType
{
	public GameObject endTile;

	public GameObject middleTile;

	public bool useEnds = true;

	public GameObject GetObject(Vector3Int pos, Vector3Int startPos, Vector3Int endPos, TileGroupData groupData = null)
	{
		GameObject gameObject = null;
		bool flag = pos == startPos;
		bool flag2 = pos == endPos;
		GameObject original = ((!useEnds && (flag || flag2)) ? endTile : middleTile);
		int num = 0;
		if (endPos.x > startPos.x)
		{
			num = 0;
		}
		else if (endPos.z < startPos.z)
		{
			num = 1;
		}
		else if (endPos.x < startPos.x)
		{
			num = 2;
		}
		else if (endPos.z > startPos.z)
		{
			num = 3;
		}
		if (useEnds && flag2)
		{
			num = (num + 2) % 4;
		}
		gameObject = Object.Instantiate(original);
		gameObject.transform.rotation = Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.up * 90f * num);
		if (groupData == null)
		{
			gameObject.AddComponent<TileGroupData>();
		}
		else
		{
			groupData.otherTilePositions.Add(pos);
		}
		return gameObject;
	}

	public List<GameObject> GetObjects(Vector3Int startPos, Vector3Int endPos)
	{
		List<GameObject> list = new List<GameObject>();
		TileGroupData component = GetObject(startPos, startPos, endPos).GetComponent<TileGroupData>();
		list.Add(component.gameObject);
		Vector3Int vector3Int = startPos;
		while (vector3Int != endPos)
		{
			if (endPos.x > startPos.x)
			{
				vector3Int.x++;
			}
			else if (endPos.z < startPos.z)
			{
				vector3Int.z--;
			}
			else if (endPos.x < startPos.x)
			{
				vector3Int.x--;
			}
			else if (endPos.z > startPos.z)
			{
				vector3Int.z++;
			}
			GameObject item = GetObject(vector3Int, startPos, endPos, component);
			list.Add(item);
		}
		return list;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LocaleDropdown
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using TMPro;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Localization;
using UnityEngine.Localization.Settings;

public class LocaleDropdown : MonoBehaviour
{
	public TMP_Dropdown dropdown;

	private IEnumerator Start()
	{
		yield return LocalizationSettings.InitializationOperation;
		List<TMP_Dropdown.OptionData> list = new List<TMP_Dropdown.OptionData>();
		int value = 0;
		for (int i = 0; i < LocalizationSettings.AvailableLocales.Locales.Count; i++)
		{
			Locale locale = LocalizationSettings.AvailableLocales.Locales[i];
			if (LocalizationSettings.SelectedLocale == locale)
			{
				value = i;
			}
			string text = locale.LocaleName;
			if (locale.Identifier.Code == "zh")
			{
				text = "<font=\"Noto_SC\">" + text + "</font>";
			}
			else if (locale.Identifier.Code == "zh-TW")
			{
				text = "<font=\"Noto_TC\">" + text + "</font>";
			}
			else if (locale.Identifier.Code == "ja")
			{
				text = "<font=\"mplus_JP\">" + text + "</font>";
			}
			else if (locale.Identifier.Code == "ko")
			{
				text = "<font=\"Noto_KR\">" + text + "</font>";
			}
			list.Add(new TMP_Dropdown.OptionData(text));
		}
		dropdown.AddOptions(list);
		dropdown.value = value;
		dropdown.onValueChanged.AddListener(LocaleSelected);
	}

	private static void LocaleSelected(int index)
	{
		LocalizationSettings.SelectedLocale = LocalizationSettings.AvailableLocales.Locales[index];
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LogBridge
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class LogBridge : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private CapsuleCollider col;

	[SerializeField]
	private float moveTime = 0.4f;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform log;

	public void Roll(float amount)
	{
		Vector3 vector = new Vector3(log.localPosition.x, log.localPosition.y, amount);
		Vector3 vector2 = vector - log.localPosition;
		int num = ((vector.z > log.localPosition.z) ? 1 : (-1));
		float num2 = vector2.magnitude * col.radius * (float)num;
		Quaternion endValue = log.localRotation * Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.forward * num2 * 57.29578f);
		log.DOLocalRotateQuaternion(endValue, moveTime);
		log.DOLocalMove(log.localPosition + vector2, moveTime);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LookDetector
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

public class LookDetector : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private PlayerController controller;

	private List<Transform> treesInRange = new List<Transform>();

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (other.CompareTag("Tree") & !treesInRange.Contains(other.transform))
		{
			treesInRange.Add(other.transform);
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (other.CompareTag("Tree") && treesInRange.Contains(other.transform))
		{
			treesInRange.Remove(other.transform);
		}
	}

	public Transform ClosestTree(float facingThreshold)
	{
		Transform result = null;
		if (treesInRange.Count > 0)
		{
			float num = facingThreshold;
			for (int num2 = treesInRange.Count - 1; num2 >= 0; num2--)
			{
				if (treesInRange[num2] == null)
				{
					treesInRange.RemoveAt(num2);
				}
				else
				{
					Transform transform = treesInRange[num2];
					Vector3 lhs = transform.transform.position - base.transform.position;
					lhs.y = 0f;
					lhs.Normalize();
					float num3 = Vector3.Dot(lhs, base.transform.forward);
					if (num3 > num)
					{
						result = transform;
						num = num3;
					}
				}
			}
		}
		return result;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// LostWoodsChanger
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;

public class LostWoodsChanger : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float teleportDistance = 16f;

	public Transform RoomMiddlePos;

	public Transform RoomNorthPos;

	public Transform RoomEastPos;

	public Transform RoomSouthPos;

	public Transform RoomWestPos;

	public LostWoodsRoom currentRoom;

	private void Start()
	{
		LoadRoom(currentRoom);
	}

	public void GoNorth()
	{
		DoJump(Vector3.back);
		LoadRoom(currentRoom?.RoomNorth);
	}

	public void GoEast()
	{
		DoJump(Vector3.left);
		LoadRoom(currentRoom?.RoomEast);
	}

	public void GoSouth()
	{
		DoJump(Vector3.forward);
		LoadRoom(currentRoom?.RoomSouth);
	}

	public void GoWest()
	{
		DoJump(Vector3.right);
		LoadRoom(currentRoom?.RoomWest);
	}

	private void DoJump(Vector3 jump)
	{
		CinemachineCamera cineCam = GameManager.instance.cineCam;
		PlayerController.instance.rb.position += jump * teleportDistance;
		PlayerController.instance.transform.position = PlayerController.instance.rb.position;
		cineCam.OnTargetObjectWarped(PlayerController.instance.transform, jump * teleportDistance);
	}

	private void LoadRoom(LostWoodsRoom newRoom)
	{
		if (currentRoom != null)
		{
			currentRoom.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			if (currentRoom.RoomNorth != null)
			{
				currentRoom.RoomNorth.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			}
			if (currentRoom.RoomEast != null)
			{
				currentRoom.RoomEast.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			}
			if (currentRoom.RoomSouth != null)
			{
				currentRoom.RoomSouth.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			}
			if (currentRoom.RoomWest != null)
			{
				currentRoom.RoomWest.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			}
		}
		if (newRoom != null)
		{
			newRoom.transform.position = RoomMiddlePos.position;
			newRoom.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			if (newRoom.RoomNorth != null)
			{
				newRoom.RoomNorth.transform.position = RoomNorthPos.position;
				newRoom.RoomNorth.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			}
			if (newRoom.RoomEast != null)
			{
				newRoom.RoomEast.transform.position = RoomEastPos.position;
				newRoom.RoomEast.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			}
			if (newRoom.RoomSouth != null)
			{
				newRoom.RoomSouth.transform.position = RoomSouthPos.position;
				newRoom.RoomSouth.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			}
			if (newRoom.RoomWest != null)
			{
				newRoom.RoomWest.transform.position = RoomWestPos.position;
				newRoom.RoomWest.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			}
		}
		currentRoom = newRoom;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// MainMenu
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using Heathen.SteamworksIntegration.API;
using Steamworks;
using TMPro;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Localization;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class MainMenu : MonoBehaviour
{
	[Header("Buttons")]
	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable continueBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable startBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable creditsBackBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable settingsStartBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable charaChoiceDefaultBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable fileConfirmContinueBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable kaizoOption;

	[Header("Menus")]
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject firstMenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject saveSelectMenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject creditsScreen;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject charaChoiceScreen;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject fileConfirmScreen;

	[SerializeField]
	private LevelSelect levelSelectScreen;

	[SerializeField]
	private SettingsMenu settingsMenu;

	[Header("Other Refs")]
	public ScrollRect saveScrollView;

	public RectTransform saveList;

	public TMP_Text fileConfirmText;

	public GameObject kaizoInfo;

	[Header("Prefabs")]
	[SerializeField]
	private SaveSelectSlot saveSelectSlotPrefab;

	private Dictionary<int, PlayerData> saves = new Dictionary<int, PlayerData>();

	private int lastChosenSave;

	private bool kaizoSelected;

	private void Start()
	{
		LoadSaves();
		ShowFirstMenu();
		GameManager.instance.onSavesLoaded.AddListener(OnSavesLoaded);
	}

	private void OnSavesLoaded()
	{
		kaizoOption.gameObject.SetActive(PlayerData.sharedData.kaizoModeUnlocked);
	}

	public void ShowFirstMenu()
	{
		saveSelectMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		creditsScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		charaChoiceScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		fileConfirmScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		settingsMenu.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		levelSelectScreen.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: true);
		bool flag = saves.Count > 0;
		continueBtn.gameObject.SetActive(flag);
		if (flag)
		{
			continueBtn.Select();
		}
		else
		{
			startBtn.Select();
		}
		kaizoSelected = false;
		if (saves.Count >= 100)
		{
			startBtn.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		}
	}

	public void ShowSavesList()
	{
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			saves = GameManager.instance.cloudSaves;
		}
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		fileConfirmScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		saveSelectMenu.SetActive(value: true);
		levelSelectScreen.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		foreach (Transform save in saveList)
		{
			Object.Destroy(save.gameObject);
		}
		SaveSelectSlot saveSelectSlot = null;
		foreach (KeyValuePair<int, PlayerData> safe in saves)
		{
			SaveSelectSlot saveSelectSlot2 = Object.Instantiate(saveSelectSlotPrefab, saveList);
			saveSelectSlot2.Set(this, safe.Value);
			if (saveSelectSlot == null)
			{
				saveSelectSlot = saveSelectSlot2;
			}
		}
		if (saveSelectSlot != null)
		{
			saveSelectSlot.button.Select();
		}
	}

	public void StartNewGame(bool kaizo = false)
	{
		kaizoSelected = kaizo;
		kaizoInfo.SetActive(kaizo);
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		charaChoiceScreen.SetActive(value: true);
		charaChoiceDefaultBtn.Select();
	}

	public void ShowCredits()
	{
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		creditsScreen.SetActive(value: true);
		creditsBackBtn.Select();
		levelSelectScreen.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
	}

	public void WishlistLink()
	{
		Overlay.Client.Activate(4171850u, EOverlayToStoreFlag.k_EOverlayToStoreFlag_None);
	}

	public void DiscordLink()
	{
		Application.OpenURL("https://discord.gg/zteGwprHT5");
	}

	public void ToLevelSelect()
	{
		fileConfirmScreen.SetActive(value: false);
		levelSelectScreen.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		levelSelectScreen.Set(saves[lastChosenSave].levelReached, lastChosenSave);
	}

	public void ConfirmSave(int fileId)
	{
		lastChosenSave = fileId;
		saveSelectMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		fileConfirmScreen.SetActive(value: true);
		levelSelectScreen.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		PlayerData playerData = saves[fileId];
		LocalizedString displayName = GameManager.instance.settings.levels[playerData.levelReached].displayName;
		fileConfirmText.SetText(displayName.GetLocalizedString());
		fileConfirmContinueBtn.Select();
	}

	public void ToSettings()
	{
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		settingsMenu.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		settingsStartBtn.Select();
	}

	public void DeleteSave()
	{
		GameManager.instance.DeleteFile(lastChosenSave);
		LoadSaves();
		if (saves.Count > 0)
		{
			ShowSavesList();
		}
		else
		{
			ShowFirstMenu();
		}
	}

	public void ChooseSave()
	{
		LevelInfo levelInfo = GameManager.instance.settings.levels[saves[lastChosenSave].levelReached];
		GameManager.instance.Load(lastChosenSave);
		GameManager.instance.JumpToLevel(levelInfo.loadName);
	}

	public void Quit()
	{
		Application.Quit();
	}

	public void ChooseDefaultChara()
	{
		PlayerData.activeFile = new PlayerData
		{
			fileId = GameManager.instance.nextAvailableFileId,
			appearance = GameManager.instance.settings.defaultChara,
			kaizo = kaizoSelected
		};
		GameManager.instance.Save();
		GameManager.instance.JumpToLevel(GameManager.instance.settings.levels[0].loadName);
	}

	public void ChooseCustomChara()
	{
		PlayerData.activeFile = new PlayerData
		{
			fileId = GameManager.instance.nextAvailableFileId,
			appearance = GameManager.instance.settings.defaultChara,
			kaizo = kaizoSelected
		};
		GameManager.instance.JumpToLevel("characterCreator", save: false);
	}

	private void LoadSaves()
	{
		if (RemoteStorage.Client.IsEnabled)
		{
			saves = GameManager.instance.cloudSaves;
			OnSavesLoaded();
			return;
		}
		saves.Clear();
		string persistentDataPath = Application.persistentDataPath;
		if (!Directory.Exists(persistentDataPath))
		{
			Directory.CreateDirectory(persistentDataPath);
		}
		string[] files = Directory.GetFiles(persistentDataPath, "*.json");
		foreach (string path in files)
		{
			string json = File.ReadAllText(path);
			if (Path.GetFileName(path) == "sharedData.json")
			{
				PlayerData.sharedData = JsonUtility.FromJson<SharedData>(json);
				continue;
			}
			PlayerData playerData = JsonUtility.FromJson<PlayerData>(json);
			if (playerData != null)
			{
				saves.Add(playerData.fileId, playerData);
			}
		}
		GameManager.instance.nextAvailableFileId = ((saves.Count != 0) ? (saves.Keys.Max() + 1) : 0);
		OnSavesLoaded();
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// MusicSpeedUp
using UnityEngine;

public class MusicSpeedUp : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float maxPitch = 2f;

	public float timeToMax = 10f;

	private PlayerController player;

	private bool inZone;

	private float pitch = 1f;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
			if (component != null && !component.dead)
			{
				player = component;
				inZone = true;
			}
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled)
		{
			PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
			if (component != null && !component.dead)
			{
				inZone = false;
				player = null;
				GameManager.instance.musicSource.pitch = 1f;
				GameManager.instance.audioMixer.SetFloat("MusicPitch", 1f);
				pitch = 1f;
			}
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (inZone && player != null && !player.dead)
		{
			pitch = Mathf.Clamp(pitch + (maxPitch - 1f) / timeToMax * Time.deltaTime, 1f, maxPitch);
			GameManager.instance.musicSource.pitch = pitch;
			GameManager.instance.audioMixer.SetFloat("MusicPitch", 1f / pitch);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// OnCollideEvent
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class OnCollideEvent : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Rigidbody rb;

	[SerializeField]
	private float minRelativeVelocity;

	[SerializeField]
	private UnityEvent onCollide;

	[SerializeField]
	private bool onlyOnce = true;

	private bool hit;

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		if ((!onlyOnce || !hit) && collision.relativeVelocity.magnitude >= minRelativeVelocity)
		{
			onCollide.Invoke();
			if (onlyOnce)
			{
				base.enabled = false;
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// OverrideTextureRule
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

[Serializable]
public class OverrideTextureRule
{
	public string label;

	public Adjacencies adjacencies;

	public bool rotate;

	public Vector2Int tilePos;

	public bool randomize;

	public List<Vector2Int> randomTilesPos = new List<Vector2Int>();
}

	public TempChunkObject GetObject(Adjacencies adj)
	{
		int rotation = 0;
		OverrideTextureRule overrideTextureRule = null;
		foreach (OverrideTextureRule rule in rules)
		{
			bool flag = false;
			if ((!rule.rotate) ? CheckAdjacency(adj, rule.adjacencies) : CheckAdjacencyWithRotation(adj, rule.adjacencies, out rotation))
			{
				overrideTextureRule = rule;
				break;
			}
		}
		if (overrideTextureRule != null)
		{
			Vector2Int vector2Int = ((!overrideTextureRule.randomize) ? overrideTextureRule.tilePos : overrideTextureRule.randomTilesPos[Random.Range(0, overrideTextureRule.randomTilesPos.Count)]);
			Mesh mesh = Object.Instantiate(quad.meshFilter.sharedMesh);
			Vector2Int vector2Int2 = new Vector2Int(vector2Int.x * tilePixelSize.x + (vector2Int.x + 1) * padding, vector2Int.y * tilePixelSize.y + (vector2Int.y + 1) * padding);
			Vector2Int vector2Int3 = new Vector2Int((vector2Int.x + 1) * tilePixelSize.x + (vector2Int.x + 1) * padding, (vector2Int.y + 1) * tilePixelSize.y + (vector2Int.y + 1) * padding);
			Vector2 vector = new Vector2((float)vector2Int2.x / (float)textureSize.x, (float)vector2Int2.y / (float)textureSize.y);
			Vector2 vector2 = new Vector2((float)vector2Int3.x / (float)textureSize.x, (float)vector2Int3.y / (float)textureSize.y);
			mesh.uv = new Vector2[4]
			{
				new Vector2(vector.x, vector.y),
				new Vector2(vector.x, vector2.y),
				new Vector2(vector2.x, vector.y),
				new Vector2(vector2.x, vector2.y)
			};
			return new TempChunkObject
			{
				mat = quad.rend.sharedMaterial,
				mesh = mesh,
				rot = rotation
			};
		}
		return null;
	}

	private bool CheckAdjacencyWithRotation(Adjacencies actual, Adjacencies required, out int rotation)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++)
		{
			if (CheckAdjacency(actual, required))
			{
				rotation = i;
				return true;
			}
			actual.RotateClockwise();
		}
		rotation = -1;
		return false;
	}

	private bool CheckAdjacency(Adjacencies actual, Adjacencies required)
	{
		if ((required.nw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.nw == required.nw) && (required.n == RuleType.DontCare || actual.n == required.n) && (required.ne == RuleType.DontCare || actual.ne == required.ne) && (required.w == RuleType.DontCare || actual.w == required.w) && (required.e == RuleType.DontCare || actual.e == required.e) && (required.sw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.sw == required.sw) && (required.s == RuleType.DontCare || actual.s == required.s))
		{
			if (required.se != RuleType.DontCare)
			{
				return actual.se == required.se;
			}
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PalmTreeCycle
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class PalmTreeCycle : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Animator anim;

	[SerializeField]
	private float startDelay = 0.1f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float fallenTime = 0.7f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float raisedTime = 1.2f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float inRangeFallenTime = 0.7f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float inRangeRaisedTime = 1.2f;

	[SerializeField]
	public UnityEvent onHitGround;

	private bool inRange;

	private void Start()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoCycle());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoCycle()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(startDelay);
		while (true)
		{
			anim.SetBool("fallen", value: true);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.1f);
			onHitGround.Invoke();
			yield return new WaitForSeconds((inRange ? inRangeFallenTime : fallenTime) - 0.1f);
			anim.SetBool("fallen", value: false);
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(inRange ? inRangeRaisedTime : raisedTime);
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if ((bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = true;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if ((bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = false;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PathTile
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Rendering;

[CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "PathTile", menuName = "3D Tile/Path Tile", order = 3)]
public class PathTile : TileType
{
	public bool canBuildUpward;

	public PathTile upwardPaths;

	public TileChunkData start;

	public TileChunkData straight;

	public TileChunkData corner;

	public TileChunkData invertCorner;

	public TileChunkData end;

	private int GetRot(Vector3Int startPt, Vector3Int endPt)
	{
		if (endPt.x > startPt.x)
		{
			return 0;
		}
		if (endPt.z < startPt.z)
		{
			return 1;
		}
		if (endPt.x < startPt.x)
		{
			return 2;
		}
		return 3;
	}

	public (GameObject, List<Vector3Int>) GetObjects(Vector3Int[] pts, Tilemap tilemap, int height = 1)
	{
		List<Vector3Int> list = new List<Vector3Int>();
		int num = -1;
		List<Bounds?> list2 = new List<Bounds?>();
		GameObject gameObject = new GameObject();
		gameObject.transform.SetParent(tilemap.mapContainer);
		gameObject.name = "ObjectGroup";
		MeshFilter meshFilter = gameObject.AddComponent<MeshFilter>();
		MeshRenderer meshRenderer = gameObject.AddComponent<MeshRenderer>();
		Dictionary<Material, List<CombineInstance>> dictionary = new Dictionary<Material, List<CombineInstance>>();
		for (int i = 0; i < height; i++)
		{
			PathTile pathTile = ((i == 0) ? this : ((upwardPaths != null) ? upwardPaths : this));
			for (int j = 0; j < pts.Length - 1; j++)
			{
				int rot = GetRot(pts[j], pts[j + 1]);
				TileChunkData tileChunkData = ((num == -1) ? pathTile.start : (((rot + 1) % 4 == num) ? pathTile.corner : (((num + 1) % 4 != rot) ? pathTile.straight : pathTile.invertCorner)));
				Matrix4x4 transform = Matrix4x4.Translate(new Vector3((float)pts[j].x * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f, (float)(pts[j].y + i) * tilemap.levelHeight + tilemap.levelHeight / 2f, (float)pts[j].z * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f)) * Matrix4x4.Rotate(Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.up * 90f * rot));
				if (tileChunkData != null)
				{
					list.Add(pts[j]);
					for (int k = 0; k < tileChunkData.meshFilter.sharedMesh.subMeshCount; k++)
					{
						Material key = tileChunkData.rend.sharedMaterials[k];
						CombineInstance item = new CombineInstance
						{
							mesh = ExtractSubmesh(tileChunkData.meshFilter.sharedMesh, k),
							transform = transform
						};
						if (!dictionary.ContainsKey(key))
						{
							dictionary.Add(key, new List<CombineInstance>());
						}
						dictionary[key].Add(item);
					}
					BoxCollider[] col = tileChunkData.col;
					foreach (BoxCollider boxCollider in col)
					{
						Bounds value = GeometryUtility.CalculateBounds(new Vector3[2]
						{
							boxCollider.transform.TransformPoint(boxCollider.center + boxCollider.size / 2f),
							boxCollider.transform.TransformPoint(boxCollider.center - boxCollider.size / 2f)
						}, transform);
						list2.Add(value);
					}
				}
				Vector3Int vector3Int = pts[j];
				while (vector3Int != pts[j + 1])
				{
					if (pts[j + 1].x > pts[j].x)
					{
						vector3Int.x++;
					}
					else if (pts[j + 1].z < pts[j].z)
					{
						vector3Int.z--;
					}
					else if (pts[j + 1].x < pts[j].x)
					{
						vector3Int.x--;
					}
					else if (pts[j + 1].z > pts[j].z)
					{
						vector3Int.z++;
					}
					if (vector3Int == pts[^1])
					{
						tileChunkData = pathTile.end;
					}
					else
					{
						if (vector3Int == pts[j + 1])
						{
							break;
						}
						tileChunkData = pathTile.straight;
					}
					if (tileChunkData == null)
					{
						continue;
					}
					list.Add(vector3Int);
					transform = Matrix4x4.Translate(new Vector3((float)vector3Int.x * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f, (float)(vector3Int.y + i) * tilemap.levelHeight + tilemap.levelHeight / 2f, (float)vector3Int.z * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f)) * Matrix4x4.Rotate(Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.up * 90f * rot));
					for (int m = 0; m < tileChunkData.meshFilter.sharedMesh.subMeshCount; m++)
					{
						Material key2 = tileChunkData.rend.sharedMaterials[m];
						CombineInstance item2 = new CombineInstance
						{
							mesh = ExtractSubmesh(tileChunkData.meshFilter.sharedMesh, m),
							transform = transform
						};
						if (!dictionary.ContainsKey(key2))
						{
							dictionary.Add(key2, new List<CombineInstance>());
						}
						dictionary[key2].Add(item2);
					}
					BoxCollider[] col = tileChunkData.col;
					foreach (BoxCollider boxCollider2 in col)
					{
						Bounds value2 = GeometryUtility.CalculateBounds(new Vector3[2]
						{
							boxCollider2.transform.TransformPoint(boxCollider2.center + boxCollider2.size / 2f),
							boxCollider2.transform.TransformPoint(boxCollider2.center - boxCollider2.size / 2f)
						}, transform);
						list2.Add(value2);
					}
				}
				num = rot;
			}
			num = -1;
		}
		List<Material> list3 = new List<Material>();
		List<CombineInstance> list4 = new List<CombineInstance>();
		foreach (KeyValuePair<Material, List<CombineInstance>> item4 in dictionary)
		{
			Mesh mesh = new Mesh();
			mesh.CombineMeshes(item4.Value.ToArray(), mergeSubMeshes: true);
			CombineInstance item3 = new CombineInstance
			{
				mesh = mesh,
				transform = Matrix4x4.identity
			};
			list4.Add(item3);
			list3.Add(item4.Key);
		}
		meshRenderer.sharedMaterials = list3.ToArray();
		Mesh mesh2 = new Mesh();
		mesh2.CombineMeshes(list4.ToArray(), mergeSubMeshes: false);
		meshFilter.mesh = mesh2;
		MakeColliders(gameObject, list2);
		return (gameObject, list);
	}

	public Mesh ExtractSubmesh(Mesh m, int meshIndex)
	{
		Vector3[] vertices = m.vertices;
		Vector3[] normals = m.normals;
		Vector4[] tangents = m.tangents;
		List<Vector3> list = new List<Vector3>();
		List<Vector3> list2 = new List<Vector3>();
		List<Vector4> list3 = new List<Vector4>();
		List<int> list4 = new List<int>();
		int[] triangles = m.GetTriangles(meshIndex);
		List<Vector2> list5 = new List<Vector2>();
		for (int i = 0; i < triangles.Length; i += 3)
		{
			int num = triangles[i];
			int num2 = triangles[i + 1];
			int num3 = triangles[i + 2];
			list.Add(vertices[num]);
			list.Add(vertices[num2]);
			list.Add(vertices[num3]);
			list2.Add(normals[num]);
			list2.Add(normals[num2]);
			list2.Add(normals[num3]);
			list4.Add(list4.Count);
			list4.Add(list4.Count);
			list4.Add(list4.Count);
			list3.Add(tangents[num]);
			list3.Add(tangents[num3]);
			list3.Add(tangents[num3]);
			list5.Add(m.uv[num]);
			list5.Add(m.uv[num2]);
			list5.Add(m.uv[num3]);
		}
		Mesh mesh = new Mesh();
		mesh.indexFormat = ((list.Count > 65536) ? IndexFormat.UInt32 : IndexFormat.UInt16);
		mesh.SetVertices(list);
		mesh.SetNormals(list2);
		mesh.SetTriangles(list4, 0, calculateBounds: true);
		mesh.SetTangents(list3);
		mesh.SetUVs(0, list5);
		return mesh;
	}

	private List<Bounds?> BoundsPass(List<Bounds?> bounds)
	{
		float num = 0.05f;
		List<Bounds?> list = new List<Bounds?>();
		for (int i = 0; i < bounds.Count; i++)
		{
			if (!bounds[i].HasValue)
			{
				continue;
			}
			Bounds value = bounds[i].Value;
			for (int j = i + 1; j < bounds.Count; j++)
			{
				if (bounds[j].HasValue)
				{
					bool flag = Mathf.Abs(value.max.x - bounds[j].Value.max.x) < num;
					bool flag2 = Mathf.Abs(value.min.x - bounds[j].Value.min.x) < num;
					bool flag3 = Mathf.Abs(value.max.y - bounds[j].Value.max.y) < num;
					bool flag4 = Mathf.Abs(value.min.y - bounds[j].Value.min.y) < num;
					bool flag5 = Mathf.Abs(value.max.z - bounds[j].Value.max.z) < num;
					bool flag6 = Mathf.Abs(value.min.z - bounds[j].Value.min.z) < num;
					bool flag7 = Mathf.Abs(value.max.x - bounds[j].Value.min.x) < num || Mathf.Abs(value.min.x - bounds[j].Value.max.x) < num;
					bool flag8 = Mathf.Abs(value.max.y - bounds[j].Value.min.y) < num || Mathf.Abs(value.min.y - bounds[j].Value.max.y) < num;
					bool flag9 = Mathf.Abs(value.max.z - bounds[j].Value.min.z) < num || Mathf.Abs(value.min.z - bounds[j].Value.max.z) < num;
					if ((flag && flag2 && flag3 && flag4 && flag9) || (flag3 && flag4 && flag5 && flag6 && flag7) || (flag && flag2 && flag5 && flag6 && flag8))
					{
						value.Encapsulate(bounds[j].Value);
						bounds[j] = null;
					}
				}
			}
			list.Add(value);
		}
		return list;
	}

	private void MakeColliders(GameObject ob, List<Bounds?> b)
	{
		List<Bounds?> bounds = BoundsPass(b);
		foreach (Bounds? item in BoundsPass(bounds))
		{
			BoxCollider boxCollider = ob.AddComponent<BoxCollider>();
			boxCollider.center = item.Value.center;
			boxCollider.size = item.Value.size;
		}
	}
}

public class PathTileData : MonoBehaviour

	public Vector3Int rightTile;
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PauseMenu
using System;

public class PauseMenu : MonoBehaviour
{
