	private GameObject firstMenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject quitConfirmMenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable defaultBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject hatMenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private HatBtn hatDefaultBtn;

	public SettingsMenu settingsMenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable settingsDefaultBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Selectable quitConfirmDefaultBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform hatList;

	[SerializeField]
	private HatBtn hatBtnPrefab;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Text coinCount;

	[Header("Tree Button")]
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject treeBtn;

	[SerializeField]
	private RectTransform attackTree;

	[SerializeField]
	private RectTransform windUpPos;

	[SerializeField]
	private float windUpTime = 1f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float waitTime = 1f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float attackSpeed = 1000f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float attackLife = 3f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float hitForce = 2000f;

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool showing;

	private Vector3 treeStartLocalPos;

	private Transform treeStartParent;

	private Vector3 treeStartScale;

	private List<HatBtn> hatBtns = new List<HatBtn>();

	private IEnumerator attackCoroutine;

	private void Start()
	{
		treeStartLocalPos = attackTree.localPosition;
		treeStartParent = attackTree.parent;
		treeStartScale = attackTree.localScale;
		hatDefaultBtn.menu = this;
		for (int i = 0; i < PlayerData.activeFile.hatStates.Length; i++)
		{
			HatBtn hatBtn = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(hatBtnPrefab, hatList);
			hatBtn.menu = this;
			hatBtns.Add(hatBtn);
		}
		RefreshHatStates();
	}

	public void RefreshHatStates()
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < PlayerData.activeFile.hatStates.Length; i++)
		{
			hatBtns[i].Set(GameManager.instance.settings.hats[i], PlayerData.activeFile.hatStates[i], PlayerData.activeFile.currentHat == i);
		}
	}

	public void Toggle()
	{
		if (showing || (!(PlayerController.instance == null) && !PlayerController.instance.blocked && !PlayerController.instance.dead))
		{
			showing = !showing;
			if (showing)
			{
				Show();
			}
			else
			{
				Hide();
			}
		}
	}

	private void Show()
	{
		PlayerController.instance?.AddBlocker(this);
		Time.timeScale = 0f;
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: true);
		defaultBtn.Select();
		GameManager.instance.interactPrompt.Hide();
		GameManager.instance.PauseTimer();
	}

	private void Hide()
	{
		PlayerController.instance?.RemoveBlocker(this);
		Time.timeScale = 1f;
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		hatMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		settingsMenu.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		quitConfirmMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		EventSystem.current.SetSelectedGameObject(null);
		GameManager.instance.UnpauseTimer();
	}

	public void ToFirstMenu()
	{
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: true);
		settingsMenu.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		hatMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		quitConfirmMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		defaultBtn.Select();
	}

	public void ToHatMenu()
	{
		RefreshHatStates();
		coinCount.text = PlayerData.activeFile.coinCount.ToString();
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		hatMenu.SetActive(value: true);
		hatDefaultBtn.button.Select();
	}

	public void ToSettingsMenu()
	{
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		settingsMenu.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		settingsDefaultBtn.Select();
	}

	public void ToQuitConfirm()
	{
		firstMenu.SetActive(value: false);
		quitConfirmMenu.SetActive(value: true);
		quitConfirmDefaultBtn.Select();
	}

	public void ToMainMenu()
	{
		CancelTreeBtn();
		showing = false;
		Hide();
		GameManager.instance.StopTimer();
		PlayerData.activeFile = new PlayerData();
		SceneManager.LoadScene(0);
	}

	public void Quit()
	{
		Application.Quit();
	}

	public void WishlistLink()
	{
		Overlay.Client.Activate(4171850u, EOverlayToStoreFlag.k_EOverlayToStoreFlag_None);
	}

	public void TreeBtn()
	{
		treeBtn.SetActive(value: false);
		attackTree.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		attackTree.SetParent(base.transform, worldPositionStays: true);
		attackTree.SetAsFirstSibling();
		Toggle();
		attackCoroutine = DoAttack();
		GameManager.instance.StartCoroutine(attackCoroutine);
	}

	private IEnumerator DoAttack()
	{
		DOTweenModuleUI.DOAnchorPos(attackTree, windUpPos.anchoredPosition, 1f, false);
		attackTree.DOScale(windUpPos.localScale, 1f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(windUpTime + waitTime);
		bool hit = false;
		Vector2 vector = RectTransformUtility.WorldToScreenPoint(Camera.main, PlayerController.instance.transform.position + Vector3.up);
		Vector2 playerAnchorPos = base.transform.InverseTransformPoint(vector);
		Vector2 diff = playerAnchorPos - attackTree.anchoredPosition;
		for (float t = 0f; t < attackLife; t += Time.deltaTime)
		{
			attackTree.anchoredPosition += diff.normalized * attackSpeed * Time.deltaTime;
			if (!hit && Vector2.Distance(attackTree.anchoredPosition, playerAnchorPos) < 50f)
			{
				PlayerController.instance.Kill();
				PlayerController.instance.AddForce(diff.normalized * hitForce);
				UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(GameManager.instance.impactEffect, PlayerController.instance.transform.position + Vector3.up, Quaternion.identity);
				hit = true;
			}
			yield return null;
		}
		attackTree.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		attackTree.SetParent(treeStartParent);
		attackTree.localPosition = treeStartLocalPos;
		attackTree.localScale = treeStartScale;
		treeBtn.SetActive(value: true);
	}

	private void CancelTreeBtn()
	{
		if (attackCoroutine != null)
		{
			DOTween.Kill(attackTree);
			GameManager.instance.StopCoroutine(attackCoroutine);
			attackTree.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			attackTree.SetParent(treeStartParent);
			attackTree.localPosition = treeStartLocalPos;
			attackTree.localScale = treeStartScale;
			treeBtn.SetActive(value: true);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PeakFallZone
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;

public class PeakFallZone : MonoBehaviour
{
	public CinemachineCamera cam;

	public void Fall()
	{
		PlayerController.instance.autoRespawn = false;
		PlayerController.instance.Kill();
		cam.Priority.Enabled = true;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PlayerController
using System;
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using CharacterCreator;
using DG.Tweening;
using MoreMountains.Feedbacks;
using RootMotion.Dynamics;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem;

public class PlayerController : MonoBehaviour
{
	public CreatedCharacter createdChara;

	public LookDetector lookDetector;

	public float maxSpeed = 6f;

	public float acceleration = 10f;

	public Rigidbody rb;

	public float accelerate = 13f;

	public float raycastDistance = 0.5f;

	public LayerMask raycastLayerMask;

	public float maxStep = 0.15f;

	public DeathRagdoll ragdoll;

	public bool autoRespawn = true;

	public UnityEvent onDeath;

	public float maxRotPerSecond = 360f;

	public GameObject wornGlasses;

	public GameObject fallingGlasses;

	public SkinnedMeshRenderer mouth;

	public SkinnedMeshRenderer eyes;

	public Material deadEyes;

	public Material deadMouth;

	public HeldAxe[] axes;

	public Transform axeHoldPos;

	public Transform axeHoldPosPuppet;

	public Transform puppetHand;

	public Transform[] puppetWeightDisableOnActive;

	public float interactionFacingThreshold = 0.2f;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform hatPos;

	private Vector3 lastMove = Vector3.zero;

	public Animator anim;

	public MMF_Player feedbacks;

	public static PlayerController instance;

	[NonSerialized]
	public List<UnityEngine.Object> blockers = new List<UnityEngine.Object>();

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool dead;

	private bool rootMotioning;

	private Vector3 impact = Vector3.zero;

	private PhysicsMaterial physicsMat;

	public Collider col;

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool usingGamepad;

	private InteractionTrigger currentTrigger;

	private List<InteractionTrigger> triggersInRange = new List<InteractionTrigger>();

	[NonSerialized]
	public float speedMult = 1f;

	private Hat hatInst;

	private HeldAxe activeAxe;

	private bool tripping;

	private InputAction moveAction;

	private Vector3 rootMotion = Vector3.zero;

	private bool laddering;

	public bool blocked => blockers.Count > 0;

	private void Awake()
	{
		instance = this;
	}

	private void Start()
	{
		//IL_0032: Unknown result type (might be due to invalid IL or missing references)
		//IL_003c: Expected O, but got Unknown
		//IL_003c: Unknown result type (might be due to invalid IL or missing references)
		//IL_0046: Expected O, but got Unknown
		//IL_005e: Unknown result type (might be due to invalid IL or missing references)
		//IL_0068: Expected O, but got Unknown
		//IL_0068: Unknown result type (might be due to invalid IL or missing references)
		//IL_0072: Expected O, but got Unknown
		GameManager.instance.SetHUDVisible(!blocked);
		SetPuppetWeights(enable: false);
		PuppetMaster puppet = ragdoll.puppet;
		puppet.OnDeath = (UpdateDelegate)Delegate.Combine((Delegate)(object)puppet.OnDeath, (Delegate)new UpdateDelegate(EnablePuppetWeights));
		PuppetMaster puppet2 = ragdoll.puppet;
		puppet2.OnResurrection = (UpdateDelegate)Delegate.Combine((Delegate)(object)puppet2.OnResurrection, (Delegate)new UpdateDelegate(DisablePuppetWeights));
		GameManager.instance.audioMixer.SetFloat("MusicPitch", 1f);
		physicsMat = col.material;
		InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Interact").started += Interact;
		InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Chop").started += Chop;
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.Target.TrackingTarget = base.transform;
		GameManager.instance.closeCam.Target.TrackingTarget = base.transform;
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.PreviousStateIsValid = false;
		moveAction = InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Move");
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint >= 0 && SceneStuff.inst != null && SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length > PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint)
		{
			base.transform.parent.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			base.transform.position = SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints[PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint].respawnPt.position;
		}
		GameManager.instance.StartCoroutine(FinishInit());
	}

	private void DisablePuppetWeights()
	{
		SetPuppetWeights(enable: false);
	}

	private void EnablePuppetWeights()
	{
		SetPuppetWeights(enable: true);
	}

	private IEnumerator FinishInit()
	{
		yield return null;
		base.transform.parent.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.currentHat != -1)
		{
			SetHat(PlayerData.activeFile.currentHat);
		}
	}

	private void OnDestroy()
	{
		InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Interact").started -= Interact;
		InputSystem.actions.FindAction("Chop").started += Chop;
		GameManager.instance.SetHUDVisible(visible: false);
	}

	private void Chop(InputAction.CallbackContext context)
	{
		if (!blocked && activeAxe != null)
		{
			StartCoroutine(DoChop());
		}
	}

	public void TeleportBtn(InputAction.CallbackContext context)
	{
		int checkpoint = PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint;
		PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint++;
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint >= SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length)
		{
			GameManager.instance.NextLevel();
			return;
		}
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.Target.TrackingTarget = base.transform;
		GameManager.instance.closeCam.Target.TrackingTarget = base.transform;
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.PreviousStateIsValid = false;
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint >= 0 && SceneStuff.inst != null && SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length > PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint)
		{
			base.transform.parent.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			base.transform.position = SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints[PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint].respawnPt.position;
		}
		GameManager.instance.StartCoroutine(FinishInit());
		if (checkpoint >= 0 && checkpoint < SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length)
		{
			SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints[checkpoint].onCheckpointUnreached.Invoke();
		}
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint >= 0 && PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint < SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length)
		{
			SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints[PlayerData.activeFile.checkpoint].onCheckpointReached.Invoke();
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoChop()
	{
		AddBlocker(this);
		activeAxe.transform.SetParent(axeHoldPosPuppet, worldPositionStays: false);
		if (activeAxe.Swing())
		{
			anim.SetBool("holdAxe", value: true);
			anim.SetTrigger("chop");
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.5f);
		}
		if (activeAxe != null)
		{
			activeAxe.transform.SetParent(axeHoldPos, worldPositionStays: false);
		}
		RemoveBlocker(this);
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		Vector2 vector = ((blocked || tripping) ? Vector2.zero : moveAction.ReadValue<Vector2>());
		Vector3 move = new Vector3(vector.x, 0f, vector.y);
		Move(move);
		lastMove = move;
		ChooseInteract();
		FixEyes();
		if (move.magnitude > 0f && !GameManager.instance.timerStarted)
		{
			GameManager.instance.StartTimer();
		}
	}

	public void HoldAxe(int axeType)
	{
		if (activeAxe != null)
		{
			UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(activeAxe.gameObject);
		}
		activeAxe = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(axes[axeType], axeHoldPos);
		activeAxe.transform.localPosition = Vector3.zero;
		activeAxe.transform.localRotation = Quaternion.identity;
		anim.SetBool("holdAxe", value: true);
	}

	public void StopHoldingAxe(bool destroy = true)
	{
		if (activeAxe != null)
		{
			if (destroy)
			{
				UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(activeAxe.gameObject);
			}
			anim.SetBool("holdAxe", value: false);
			activeAxe = null;
		}
	}

	public void FixEyes()
	{
		Transform transform = lookDetector.ClosestTree(interactionFacingThreshold);
		if (transform == null)
		{
			createdChara.LookAt(base.transform.TransformPoint(Vector3.forward));
		}
		else
		{
			createdChara.LookAt(transform.position);
		}
	}

	public void Move(Vector3 move)
	{
		if (dead)
		{
			return;
		}
		if (laddering)
		{
			anim.SetFloat("climbSpeed", move.z);
			rb.MovePosition(rb.position + Vector3.up * move.z * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
			return;
		}
		move = Vector3.MoveTowards(lastMove, move, accelerate * Time.deltaTime);
		if (impact.magnitude > 0.2f)
		{
			move += impact;
		}
		impact = Vector3.zero;
		Vector3 vector = AdjustForSlope(move * maxSpeed * speedMult);
		Vector3 force = ((rootMotion.magnitude > 0f) ? rootMotion : vector) - rb.linearVelocity;
		force.y = 0f;
		rb.AddForce(force, ForceMode.VelocityChange);
		anim.SetFloat("speed", move.magnitude * speedMult);
		if (move.magnitude > 0f && !blocked)
		{
			Quaternion to = Quaternion.LookRotation(new Vector3(move.x, 0f, move.z), Vector3.up);
			Quaternion rotation = Quaternion.RotateTowards(base.transform.rotation, to, maxRotPerSecond * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
			base.transform.rotation = rotation;
		}
		col.material = ((move.magnitude < 0.001f) ? null : physicsMat);
		lastMove = move;
	}

	private void Interact(InputAction.CallbackContext ctx)
	{
		GameManager.instance.SetInteractAction();
		if (!blocked && (bool)currentTrigger)
		{
			currentTrigger.Interact();
		}
	}

	private Vector3 AdjustForSlope(Vector3 vel)
	{
		if (Physics.Raycast(base.transform.position + vel.normalized * raycastDistance + Vector3.up, Vector3.down, out var hitInfo, 1f + maxStep, raycastLayerMask, QueryTriggerInteraction.Ignore))
		{
			float num = Mathf.Abs(hitInfo.point.y - base.transform.position.y);
			if (num < maxStep && num > 0.01f)
			{
				if (vel.magnitude > 0f)
				{
					Debug.Log("Stepping up");
				}
				return (hitInfo.point - base.transform.position).normalized * vel.magnitude;
			}
		}
		return vel;
	}

	private void OnAnimatorMove()
	{
		Vector3 velocity = anim.velocity;
		rootMotioning = velocity.magnitude > 0f;
		rootMotion = (rootMotioning ? velocity : Vector3.zero);
	}

	public void Kill()
	{
		if (!dead)
		{
			GameManager.instance.musicSource.pitch = 0.7f;
			GameManager.instance.audioMixer.SetFloat("MusicPitch", 1.4285715f);
			dead = true;
			eyes = createdChara.FindOptionByType(CharacterMeshOptionType.Eyes)?.meshObject;
			mouth = createdChara.FindOptionByType(CharacterMeshOptionType.Mouth)?.meshObject;
			createdChara.FindOptionByType(CharacterMeshOptionType.Iris)?.meshObject?.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
			wornGlasses = createdChara.FindOptionByType(CharacterMeshOptionType.Accessory)?.unskinnedMeshObject?.gameObject;
			if (mouth != null)
			{
				mouth.material = deadMouth;
			}
			if (eyes != null)
			{
				eyes.material = deadEyes;
			}
			if (fallingGlasses != null && wornGlasses != null && wornGlasses.activeInHierarchy)
			{
				fallingGlasses.transform.SetParent(null);
				fallingGlasses.SetActive(value: true);
				fallingGlasses.GetComponent<MeshFilter>().sharedMesh = wornGlasses.GetComponent<MeshFilter>().sharedMesh;
				fallingGlasses.GetComponent<MeshRenderer>().sharedMaterial = wornGlasses.GetComponent<MeshRenderer>().sharedMaterial;
			}
			if (wornGlasses != null)
			{
				wornGlasses.SetActive(value: false);
			}
			anim.enabled = false;
			rb.isKinematic = true;
			col.enabled = false;
			feedbacks.PlayFeedbacks();
			ragdoll.RagdollIn();
			onDeath.Invoke();
			if (autoRespawn)
			{
				GameManager.instance.Respawn();
			}
		}
	}

	public void Trip()
	{
		if (!tripping)
		{
			StartCoroutine(DoTrip());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoTrip()
	{
		tripping = true;
		anim.SetTrigger("trip");
		while (anim.GetCurrentAnimatorStateInfo(0).IsName("default"))
		{
			yield return null;
		}
		yield return null;
		rootMotioning = true;
		while (!anim.GetCurrentAnimatorStateInfo(0).IsName("default"))
		{
			yield return null;
		}
		rootMotioning = false;
		tripping = false;
	}

	public void AddForce(Vector3 force, bool cancelPrevVelocity = false)
	{
		ragdoll.AddForce(force, cancelPrevVelocity);
	}

	public void ChooseInteract()
	{
		currentTrigger = null;
		if (!blocked && triggersInRange.Count > 0)
		{
			float num = interactionFacingThreshold;
			for (int num2 = triggersInRange.Count - 1; num2 >= 0; num2--)
			{
				if (triggersInRange[num2] == null || !triggersInRange[num2].enabled)
				{
					triggersInRange.RemoveAt(num2);
				}
				else
				{
					InteractionTrigger interactionTrigger = triggersInRange[num2];
					Vector3 lhs = interactionTrigger.transform.position - base.transform.position;
					lhs.y = 0f;
					lhs.Normalize();
					float num3 = Vector3.Dot(lhs, base.transform.forward);
					if (num3 > num)
					{
						currentTrigger = interactionTrigger;
						num = num3;
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if ((bool)currentTrigger)
		{
			GameManager.instance.interactPrompt.Set(currentTrigger.transform, currentTrigger.promptLabel, currentTrigger.promptHeight);
		}
		else
		{
			GameManager.instance.interactPrompt.Hide();
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		InteractionTrigger component = other.GetComponent<InteractionTrigger>();
		if ((bool)component && !triggersInRange.Contains(component))
		{
			triggersInRange.Add(component);
		}
		ChooseInteract();
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		InteractionTrigger component = other.GetComponent<InteractionTrigger>();
		if ((bool)component && triggersInRange.Contains(component))
		{
			triggersInRange.Remove(component);
		}
		ChooseInteract();
	}

	public void DoGetItemPose()
	{
		base.transform.DORotate(new Vector3(0f, 180f, 0f), 0.3f);
		anim.SetBool("handsUp", value: true);
	}

	public void CancelItemPose()
	{
		anim.SetBool("handsUp", value: false);
	}

	public void RaiseHands()
	{
		anim.SetBool("handsUp", value: true);
	}

	public void SetHat(int hat)
	{
		if (hatInst != null && hatInst.transform.IsChildOf(base.transform))
		{
			UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(hatInst.gameObject);
		}
		if (hat >= 0 && hat < GameManager.instance.settings.hats.Length)
		{
			hatInst = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(GameManager.instance.settings.hats[hat].prefab, hatPos);
			hatInst.transform.localPosition = Vector3.zero;
			hatInst.transform.localRotation = Quaternion.identity;
			createdChara.FixHairCutoff(hatInst);
		}
		else
		{
			createdChara.FixHairCutoff(null);
		}
	}

	public void DropHead()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoHeadDrop());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoHeadDrop()
	{
		anim.CrossFade("sigh_head_drop", 0.1f);
		AddBlocker(this);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(1f);
		anim.CrossFade("default", 1f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.3f);
		RemoveBlocker(this);
	}

	public void StartLaddering(Ladder ladder)
	{
		laddering = true;
		anim.SetBool("onLadder", value: true);
		anim.applyRootMotion = true;
		rb.isKinematic = true;
		Vector3 towards = base.transform.position + ladder.transform.forward;
		base.transform.DOLookAt(towards, 0.25f);
		Vector3 vector = ladder.transform.position + ladder.transform.forward * -0.5f;
		base.transform.DOMoveX(vector.x, 0.25f);
		base.transform.DOMoveZ(vector.z, 0.25f);
	}

	public void StopLaddering()
	{
		laddering = false;
		anim.SetBool("onLadder", value: false);
		anim.applyRootMotion = false;
		rb.isKinematic = false;
	}

	public void SetPuppetWeights(bool enable)
	{
		Muscle[] muscles = ragdoll.puppet.muscles;
		foreach (Muscle val in muscles)
		{
			Transform[] array = puppetWeightDisableOnActive;
			foreach (Transform transform in array)
			{
				if (val.target == transform)
				{
					val.props.mappingWeight = (enable ? 1 : 0);
					break;
				}
			}
		}
	}

	public void AddBlocker(UnityEngine.Object blocker)
	{
		blockers.Add(blocker);
		GameManager.instance.SetHUDVisible(!blocked);
	}

	public void RemoveBlocker(UnityEngine.Object blocker)
	{
		if (blockers.Contains(blocker))
		{
			blockers.Remove(blocker);
		}
		GameManager.instance.SetHUDVisible(!blocked);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PlayerData
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using CharacterCreator;

public class PlayerData
{
	public static PlayerData activeFile;

	public static SharedData sharedData;

	public SerializeableChosenOptions appearance;

	public int fileId;

	public int levelReached;

	public int checkpoint = -1;

	public int currentHat = -1;

	public HatState[] hatStates;

	public List<List<int>> deaths = new List<List<int>>();

	public List<string> coinsCollected = new List<string>();

	public List<AxeType> axesBroken = new List<AxeType>();

	public List<string> otherItems = new List<string>();

	public List<long> timesSerializeable = new List<long>();

	public List<TimeSpan> times = new List<TimeSpan>();

	public int coinCount;

	public bool kaizo;

	public bool Kaizo
	{
		get
		{
			if (!kaizo)
			{
				if (SceneStuff.inst != null)
				{
					return SceneStuff.inst.forceKaizo;
				}
				return false;
			}
			return true;
		}
	}

	public int TotalDeaths => GetTotalDeaths();

	private int GetTotalDeaths()
	{
		int num = 0;
		foreach (List<int> death in activeFile.deaths)
		{
			foreach (int item in death)
			{
				num += item;
			}
		}
		return num;
	}

	public TimeSpan GetTotalTime()
	{
		TimeSpan zero = TimeSpan.Zero;
		for (int i = 0; i < times.Count; i++)
		{
			zero += times[i];
		}
		return zero;
	}

	public PlayerData()
	{
		hatStates = new HatState[GameManager.instance.settings.hats.Length];
		for (int i = 0; i < hatStates.Length; i++)
		{
			hatStates[i] = HatState.NotFound;
		}
	}

	public void RecordDeath(int level)
	{
		while (deaths.Count < level + 1)
		{
			deaths.Add(new List<int>());
			deaths.Last().Add(0);
			for (int i = 0; i < SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length; i++)
			{
				deaths.Last().Add(0);
			}
		}
		deaths[level][checkpoint + 1]++;
	}

	public void RecordAxeBreak(AxeType axeType)
	{
		if (!axesBroken.Contains(axeType))
		{
			axesBroken.Add(axeType);
			if (SceneStuff.inst != null && SceneStuff.inst.allAxesCheck != null)
			{
				SceneStuff.inst.allAxesCheck.Check();
			}
		}
	}

	public int DeathCount(Checkpoint checkpoint)
	{
		int currentLevel = GameManager.instance.currentLevel;
		while (deaths.Count < currentLevel + 1)
		{
			deaths.Add(new List<int>());
			deaths.Last().Add(0);
			for (int i = 0; i < SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints.Length; i++)
			{
				deaths.Last().Add(0);
			}
		}
		if (checkpoint == null)
		{
			return deaths[currentLevel].Sum();
		}
		int num = ((SceneStuff.inst != null) ? Array.IndexOf(SceneStuff.inst.checkpoints, checkpoint) : (-1));
		return deaths[currentLevel][num + 1];
	}

	public void SetHatState(HatSO hat, HatState state)
	{
		int num = Array.IndexOf(GameManager.instance.settings.hats, hat);
		if (num >= 0)
		{
			hatStates[num] = state;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PressureButton
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class PressureButton : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float pressDist = 0.1f;

	public UnityEvent onPress;

	public UnityEvent onRelease;

	private bool pressed;

	private float startHeight;

	private void Start()
	{
		startHeight = base.transform.position.y;
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (!pressed && base.transform.position.y < startHeight - pressDist)
		{
			pressed = true;
			onPress.Invoke();
		}
		else if (pressed && base.transform.position.y > startHeight - pressDist)
		{
			pressed = false;
			onRelease.Invoke();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ProcRoots
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using UnityEngine;

public class ProcRoots : MonoBehaviour
{
	public BoxCollider bounds;

	public ProcRoots subRootPrefab;

	public float iterationTime = 1f;

	public float nodeDist = 0.2f;

	public int circleVerts = 8;

	public float radius = 0.1f;

	public float maxRadius = 0.2f;

	public float maxTurn = 10f;

	public int maxIterations = 20;

	public LayerMask growthLayerMask;

	public float chanceOfSubRoot = 0.2f;

	public int seed = 100;

	private MeshFilter mf;

	private Vector3 growDir = Vector3.forward;

	private List<Vector3> nodes = new List<Vector3>();

	private float fallAngle;

	private float fallAngleChange = 12f;

	private float maxFall = 20f;

	private float minFallHeight = 0.3f;

	private void Start()
	{
		mf = GetComponent<MeshFilter>();
		nodes.Add(Vector3.zero);
		StartCoroutine(SpreadRoots());
	}

	private IEnumerator SpreadRoots()
	{
		MeshCollider col = base.gameObject.AddComponent<MeshCollider>();
		for (int i = 0; i < maxIterations; i++)
		{
			TurnGrowthHorizontally();
			Vector3 position = nodes.Last() + growDir * nodeDist;
			Vector3 vector = base.transform.TransformPoint(position);
			if ((bounds != null && !bounds.bounds.Contains(vector)) || Physics.CheckSphere(vector, 0.1f, growthLayerMask, QueryTriggerInteraction.Ignore))
			{
				if (nodes.Count < 2)
				{
					Object.Destroy(base.gameObject);
				}
				break;
			}
			RaycastHit hitInfo;
			float groundDist = (Physics.Raycast(vector, Vector3.down, out hitInfo, 100f, growthLayerMask, QueryTriggerInteraction.Ignore) ? (vector.y - radius - hitInfo.point.y) : float.MaxValue);
			Vector3 vector2 = TurnGrowthVertically(groundDist);
			Vector3 item = nodes[nodes.Count - 1] + vector2 * nodeDist;
			nodes.Add(item);
			RebuildMesh();
			col.sharedMesh = mf.sharedMesh;
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(iterationTime);
			if (nodes.Count > 3)
			{
				TryMakingSubroots(nodes[nodes.Count - 3], i);
			}
		}
	}

	private void TryMakingSubroots(Vector3 pos, int iteration)
	{
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo)
		{
			Random.InitState(seed);
		}
		if (Random.value < chanceOfSubRoot && maxIterations > 4 && iteration < maxIterations - 3 && !Physics.CheckSphere(pos, 0.5f, growthLayerMask, QueryTriggerInteraction.Ignore))
		{
			int num = Random.Range(-45, 45);
			Quaternion rotation = Quaternion.Euler(0f, num, 0f) * base.transform.rotation;
			ProcRoots procRoots = Object.Instantiate(subRootPrefab, base.transform.TransformPoint(pos), rotation);
			procRoots.bounds = bounds;
			procRoots.maxIterations = (int)((float)maxIterations * 0.5f);
			procRoots.maxRadius = radius;
			procRoots.radius = radius * (radius / maxRadius);
		}
		seed = (int)(Random.value * 10000f);
	}

	private Vector3 TurnGrowthVertically(float groundDist)
	{
		if (groundDist <= 0f)
		{
			return growDir;
		}
		if (groundDist > minFallHeight)
		{
			fallAngle = Mathf.Clamp(fallAngle + fallAngleChange, 0f, maxFall);
		}
		else
		{
			fallAngle = Mathf.Clamp(fallAngle - fallAngleChange, 0f, maxFall);
		}
		return Quaternion.Euler(fallAngle, 0f, 0f) * growDir;
	}

	private void TurnGrowthHorizontally()
	{
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo)
		{
			Random.InitState(seed);
		}
		float y = Random.Range(0f - maxTurn, maxTurn);
		growDir = Quaternion.Euler(0f, y, 0f) * growDir;
		seed = (int)(Random.value * 10000f);
	}

	private void RebuildMesh()
	{
		Mesh mesh = new Mesh();
		Vector3[] array = new Vector3[circleVerts * (nodes.Count - 1) + 1];
		for (int i = 0; i < nodes.Count - 1; i++)
		{
			float num = Mathf.Lerp(radius, maxRadius, (float)(nodes.Count - i - 1) / (float)nodes.Count);
			for (int j = 0; j < circleVerts; j++)
			{
				Vector3 normalized = (nodes[i + 1] - nodes[i]).normalized;
				Vector3 normalized2 = Vector3.Cross(normalized, base.transform.up).normalized;
				float angle = 360f / (float)circleVerts * (float)j;
				Vector3 vector = nodes[i] + Quaternion.AngleAxis(angle, normalized) * normalized2 * num;
				array[i * circleVerts + j] = vector;
			}
		}
		array[^1] = nodes[nodes.Count - 1];
		mesh.vertices = array;
		int[] array2 = new int[circleVerts * (nodes.Count - 2) * 6 + circleVerts * 3];
		for (int k = 0; k < nodes.Count - 2; k++)
		{
			for (int l = 0; l < circleVerts; l++)
			{
				int num2 = k * circleVerts + l;
				int num3 = k * circleVerts + (l + 1) % circleVerts;
				int num4 = (k + 1) * circleVerts + l;
				int num5 = (k + 1) * circleVerts + (l + 1) % circleVerts;
				int num6 = (k * circleVerts + l) * 6;
				array2[num6] = num2;
				array2[num6 + 1] = num3;
				array2[num6 + 2] = num4;
				array2[num6 + 3] = num5;
				array2[num6 + 4] = num4;
				array2[num6 + 5] = num3;
			}
		}
		for (int m = 0; m < circleVerts; m++)
		{
			int num7 = (nodes.Count - 2) * circleVerts + m;
			int num8 = (nodes.Count - 2) * circleVerts + (m + 1) % circleVerts;
			int num9 = array.Length - 1;
			int num10 = (nodes.Count - 2) * circleVerts * 6 + m * 3;
			array2[num10] = num7;
			array2[num10 + 1] = num8;
			array2[num10 + 2] = num9;
		}
		mesh.triangles = array2;
		Vector2[] array3 = new Vector2[array.Length];
		for (int n = 0; n < array3.Length; n++)
		{
			array3[n] = new Vector2(0.5f, 0.5f);
		}
		mesh.uv = array3;
		mesh.RecalculateNormals();
		mesh.RecalculateBounds();
		mesh.RecalculateTangents();
		mf.mesh = mesh;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ProjectileController
using UnityEngine;

public class ProjectileController : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float speed = 100f;

	public LayerMask collisionLayerMask;

	public GameObject rocketExplosion;

	public MeshRenderer projectileMesh;

	private bool targetHit;

	public AudioSource inFlightAudioSource;

	public ParticleSystem disableOnHit;

	private void Update()
	{
		if (!targetHit)
		{
			base.transform.position += base.transform.forward * (speed * Time.deltaTime);
		}
	}

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		if (base.enabled)
		{
			Explode();
			projectileMesh.enabled = false;
			targetHit = true;
			inFlightAudioSource.Stop();
			Collider[] components = GetComponents<Collider>();
			for (int i = 0; i < components.Length; i++)
			{
				components[i].enabled = false;
			}
			disableOnHit.Stop();
			Object.Destroy(base.gameObject, 5f);
		}
	}

	private void Explode()
	{
		Object.Instantiate(rocketExplosion, base.transform.position, rocketExplosion.transform.rotation, null);
		Collider[] array = Physics.OverlapSphere(base.transform.position, 5f);
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			PlayerController componentInParent = array[i].GetComponentInParent<PlayerController>();
			if (componentInParent != null)
			{
				componentInParent.Kill();
				componentInParent.ragdoll.AddExplosionForce(base.transform.position, 10000f, 5f);
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ProximitySpike
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class ProximitySpike : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform spike;

	public float height = 3f;

	public float upSpeed = 15f;

	public float downSpeed = 3f;

	public AudioSource aud;

	public bool returnAfter = true;

	public float launchForce = 1000f;

	public float upForce = 3000f;

	public UnityEvent onSpike;

	private bool activated;

	private List<Collider> inRange = new List<Collider>();

	private Vector3 downPos;

	private Vector3 upPos;

	private void Start()
	{
		downPos = spike.position;
		upPos = spike.position + Vector3.up * height;
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (activated)
		{
			spike.position = Vector3.MoveTowards(spike.position, upPos, upSpeed * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
		}
		else
		{
			spike.position = Vector3.MoveTowards(spike.position, downPos, downSpeed * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (other.isTrigger || inRange.Contains(other))
		{
			return;
		}
		inRange.Add(other);
		if (!activated)
		{
			PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
			if ((bool)component)
			{
				onSpike.Invoke();
				component.Kill();
				component.ragdoll.AddExplosionForce(base.transform.position, launchForce, 5f);
				component.AddForce(Vector3.up * upForce);
				activated = true;
				aud.Play();
			}
		}
	}

	public void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (inRange.Contains(other))
		{
			inRange.Remove(other);
			if (activated && inRange.Count == 0 && returnAfter)
			{
				activated = false;
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PunchTree
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class PunchTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 punchForce;

	public Animator anim;

	public UnityEvent onHit;

	public Collider trigger;

	public GameObject effect;

	public Vector3 effectOffset = Vector3.zero;

	public string animTrigger = "punch";

	public void DoPunchDelayed(float delay)
	{
		StartCoroutine(DelayedPunch(delay));
	}

	private IEnumerator DelayedPunch(float delay)
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(delay);
		DoPunch();
	}

	public void DoPunch()
	{
		trigger.enabled = true;
		anim.SetTrigger(animTrigger);
	}

	public void DoGroundPunch()
	{
		anim.SetTrigger("groundPunch");
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null && !component.dead)
		{
			onHit.Invoke();
			component.Kill();
			StartCoroutine(delayForce(component));
			effect.transform.SetParent(null);
			effect.transform.position = component.transform.position + new Vector3(0f, 1.2f, 0f) + effectOffset;
			effect.SetActive(value: true);
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator delayForce(PlayerController chara)
	{
		yield return null;
		chara.AddForce(punchForce);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// PushTree
using UnityEngine;

public class PushTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Rigidbody rb;

	public Transform moveGoal;

	public float toSpeed = 17f;

	public float returnSpeed = 8f;

	public Collider pushCollider;

	public float cooldownTime = 1f;

	private bool inRange;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	private float timer;

	private void Awake()
	{
		startPos = rb.transform.position;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null && !component.dead)
		{
			inRange = true;
			pushCollider.enabled = true;
			pushCollider.gameObject.layer = 9;
			rb.gameObject.layer = 9;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null && !component.dead)
		{
			inRange = false;
			pushCollider.enabled = false;
			pushCollider.gameObject.layer = 0;
			rb.gameObject.layer = 0;
		}
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		bool flag = false;
		Vector3 vector;
		if (inRange)
		{
			vector = moveGoal.position - rb.transform.position;
			timer = 0f;
		}
		else if (timer >= cooldownTime)
		{
			vector = startPos - rb.transform.position;
			flag = true;
		}
		else
		{
			vector = Vector3.zero;
		}
		if ((double)vector.magnitude > 0.2)
		{
			rb.linearVelocity = vector.normalized * (flag ? returnSpeed : toSpeed);
		}
		else
		{
			rb.linearVelocity = Vector3.zero;
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (timer < cooldownTime)
		{
			timer += Time.deltaTime;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// QuakingAspen
using System;
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class QuakingAspen : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Animator anim;

	public SphereCollider hitCollider;

	public UnityEvent onHit;

	public float slamTime = 0.1f;

	public float cooldown = 1f;

	public Collider damageCollider;

	private List<PlayerController> charasInRange = new List<PlayerController>();

	[NonSerialized]
	public bool attacking;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if ((bool)component)
		{
			if (!attacking && base.enabled)
			{
				anim.SetTrigger("smack");
				StartCoroutine(DoHit());
			}
			if (!charasInRange.Contains(component))
			{
				charasInRange.Add(component);
			}
		}
	}

	public void SetQuake(bool quaking)
	{
		anim.SetBool("shake0", quaking);
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null && charasInRange.Contains(component))
		{
			charasInRange.Remove(component);
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoHit()
	{
		attacking = true;
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(slamTime);
		base.transform.TransformPoint(hitCollider.center);
		bool flag = false;
		if (damageCollider.enabled)
		{
			foreach (PlayerController item in charasInRange)
			{
				if (item != null)
				{
					item.Kill();
					flag = true;
				}
			}
		}
		if (flag)
		{
			onHit.Invoke();
		}
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(cooldown);
		attacking = false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// RectTile
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

[CreateAssetMenu(fileName = "RectTile", menuName = "3D Tile/Rect Tile", order = 3)]
public class RectTile : TileType
{
	public GameObject endTile;

	public GameObject frontTile;

	public GameObject cornerTile;

	public GameObject middleTile;

	public GameObject GetObject(Vector3Int pos, Vector3Int minPos, Vector3Int maxPos, bool alongZ, TileGroupData groupData = null)
	{
		bool flag = false;
		bool flag2 = false;
		GameObject original;
		if (pos.x == minPos.x && pos.z == minPos.z)
		{
			original = cornerTile;
		}
		else if (pos.x == minPos.x && pos.z == maxPos.z)
		{
			original = cornerTile;
			flag2 = true;
		}
		else if (pos.x == maxPos.x && pos.z == minPos.z)
		{
			original = cornerTile;
			flag = true;
		}
		else if (pos.x == maxPos.x && pos.z == maxPos.z)
		{
			original = cornerTile;
			flag = true;
			flag2 = true;
		}
		else if (pos.x == minPos.x)
		{
			original = endTile;
		}
		else if (pos.x == maxPos.x)
		{
			original = endTile;
			flag = true;
		}
		else if (pos.z == minPos.z)
		{
			original = frontTile;
		}
		else if (pos.z == maxPos.z)
		{
			original = frontTile;
			flag2 = true;
		}
		else
		{
			original = middleTile;
		}
		GameObject gameObject = Object.Instantiate(original);
		Vector3 localScale = new Vector3((!flag) ? 1 : (-1), 1f, (!flag2) ? 1 : (-1));
		gameObject.transform.localScale = localScale;
		if (groupData == null)
		{
			gameObject.AddComponent<TileGroupData>();
		}
		else
		{
			groupData.otherTilePositions.Add(pos);
		}
		return gameObject;
	}

	public List<GameObject> GetObjects(Vector3Int minPos, Vector3Int maxPos)
	{
		List<GameObject> list = new List<GameObject>();
		TileGroupData tileGroupData = null;
		int num = maxPos.x - minPos.x;
		int num2 = maxPos.z - minPos.z;
		for (int i = 0; i <= num; i++)
		{
			for (int j = 0; j <= num2; j++)
			{
				Vector3Int pos = new Vector3Int(minPos.x + i, minPos.y, minPos.z + j);
				GameObject gameObject = GetObject(pos, minPos, maxPos, alongZ: false, tileGroupData);
				list.Add(gameObject);
				if (tileGroupData == null)
				{
					tileGroupData = gameObject.GetComponent<TileGroupData>();
				}
			}
		}
		return list;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ResetDeviceBindings
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.InputSystem;

public class ResetDeviceBindings : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private InputActionAsset inputActions;

	[SerializeField]
	private string targetControlScheme;

	public void ResetAllBindings()
	{
		foreach (InputActionMap actionMap in inputActions.actionMaps)
		{
			actionMap.RemoveAllBindingOverrides();
		}
	}

	public void ResetControlSchemeBinding()
	{
		foreach (InputActionMap actionMap in inputActions.actionMaps)
		{
			foreach (InputAction action in actionMap.actions)
			{
				action.RemoveBindingOverride(InputBinding.MaskByGroup(targetControlScheme));
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// RespawnChanger
using System;
using UnityEngine;

public class RespawnChanger : MonoBehaviour
{
	[Serializable]
	public struct RespawnChange
	{
		public int deathNumber;

		public GameObject ob;

		public Checkpoint checkpoint;
	}

	public RespawnChange[] respawnChanges;

	private void Start()
	{
		MakeChanges();
	}

	private void MakeChanges()
	{
		RespawnChange[] array = respawnChanges;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			RespawnChange respawnChange = array[i];
			respawnChange.ob.SetActive(PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo || respawnChange.deathNumber <= PlayerData.activeFile.DeathCount(respawnChange.checkpoint));
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// RespawnSwitcher
using UnityEngine;

public class RespawnSwitcher : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Checkpoint checkpoint;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject[] options;

	private void Start()
	{
		int num = PlayerData.activeFile.DeathCount(checkpoint);
		int num2 = (PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo ? (options.Length - 1) : (num % options.Length));
		for (int i = 0; i < options.Length; i++)
		{
			options[i].SetActive(i == num2);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// RollingRock
using UnityEngine;

public class RollingRock : MonoBehaviour
{
	private PlayerController playerInRange;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null)
		{
			playerInRange = component;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		PlayerController component = other.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null)
		{
			component.anim.SetBool("handsUp", value: false);
			playerInRange = null;
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if ((bool)playerInRange)
		{
			float num = Vector3.Dot(rhs: new Vector3(base.transform.position.x - playerInRange.transform.position.x, 0f, base.transform.position.z - playerInRange.transform.position.z), lhs: playerInRange.transform.forward);
			playerInRange.anim.SetBool("handsUp", num > 0.3f);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// RollingTree
using MoreMountains.Feedbacks;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class RollingTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Rigidbody rb;

	public MMF_Player feedbacks;

	public MMF_Player groundFeedback;

	public Vector3 startVelocity;

	public UnityEvent onCollide;

	public float deadThreshold = 1.5f;

	public float minLiveTime = 1f;

	public bool limitSpeedCheckToY = true;

	public bool freezeAfter;

	public float freezeHeight = 1f;

	private bool started;

	private bool dead;

	private bool touchedGround;

	private float liveTime;

	private void Awake()
	{
		rb.linearVelocity = startVelocity;
	}

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		if (dead || !(rb.linearVelocity.magnitude > 1.5f))
		{
			return;
		}
		PlayerController component = collision.collider.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
		if (component != null)
		{
			if (!component.dead)
			{
				feedbacks.transform.SetParent(null);
				feedbacks.transform.position = collision.contacts[0].point;
				feedbacks.PlayFeedbacks();
				component.Kill();
			}
		}
		else if (!touchedGround && groundFeedback != null && collision.relativeVelocity.magnitude > 3f)
		{
			onCollide.Invoke();
			groundFeedback.transform.position = collision.contacts[0].point;
			groundFeedback.PlayFeedbacks();
			touchedGround = true;
		}
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		float num = (limitSpeedCheckToY ? Mathf.Abs(rb.linearVelocity.y) : rb.linearVelocity.magnitude);
		if (!started && num > deadThreshold)
		{
			started = true;
		}
		if (started && !dead)
		{
			if (liveTime < minLiveTime)
			{
				liveTime += Time.fixedDeltaTime;
			}
			else if (num < deadThreshold)
			{
				dead = true;
			}
		}
		if (freezeAfter && base.transform.position.y <= freezeHeight)
		{
			rb.isKinematic = true;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SceneStuff
using System;
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;

public class SceneStuff : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Checkpoint[] checkpoints;

	[SerializeField]
	private Collider camConfiner;

	[SerializeField]
	private float camAngle = 30f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float camDistance = 15f;

	[SerializeField]
	private AudioClip music;

	[SerializeField]
	private float musicVolume = 1f;

	[SerializeField]
	private AudioClip altMusic;

	[SerializeField]
	private int loopsToAltMusic = 4;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject challengeTraps;

	public int levelIndex = -1;

	[NonSerialized]
	public AllAxesCheck allAxesCheck;

	public static SceneStuff inst;

	[Header("Debug")]
	public bool forceKaizo;

	private float beforeSample = 1f;

	private static int musicLoop;

	public static float altMusicTime;

	private void Awake()
	{
		inst = this;
	}

	private void Start()
	{
		if (levelIndex >= 0)
		{
			GameManager.instance.currentLevel = levelIndex;
		}
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.GetComponent<CinemachineConfiner3D>().BoundingVolume = camConfiner;
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.transform.rotation = Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.right * camAngle);
		GameManager.instance.cineCam.GetComponent<CinemachinePositionComposer>().CameraDistance = camDistance;
		GameManager.instance.StartMusic(music, musicVolume);
		if (altMusic != null && musicLoop == loopsToAltMusic)
		{
			GameManager.instance.StartMusic(altMusic, musicVolume);
			GameManager.instance.musicSource.time = altMusicTime;
		}
		if (PlayerData.activeFile.Kaizo && challengeTraps != null)
		{
			challengeTraps.SetActive(value: true);
		}
		if (!GameManager.instance.timerStarted)
		{
			GameManager.instance.UpdateTimeWithSaved();
		}
	}

	private void OnDestroy()
	{
		if (altMusic != null)
		{
			altMusicTime = GameManager.instance.musicSource.time;
			GameManager.instance.StopMusic(altMusic);
		}
		if (music != null)
		{
			GameManager.instance.StopMusic(music);
		}
	}

	public void StopMusic()
	{
		GameManager.instance.StopMusic(music);
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (!(altMusic != null) || GameManager.instance.musicSource.timeSamples <= 0)
		{
			return;
		}
		if (beforeSample < (float)GameManager.instance.musicSource.timeSamples)
		{
			beforeSample = (float)GameManager.instance.musicSource.timeSamples - 1f;
		}
		else if (beforeSample > (float)GameManager.instance.musicSource.timeSamples)
		{
			musicLoop++;
			if (musicLoop == loopsToAltMusic)
			{
				GameManager.instance.StartMusic(altMusic, musicVolume);
			}
			else if (musicLoop > loopsToAltMusic)
			{
				musicLoop = 0;
				altMusicTime = 0f;
				GameManager.instance.StopMusic(altMusic);
			}
			beforeSample = (float)GameManager.instance.musicSource.timeSamples - 1f;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ScrollRectExtensions
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public static class ScrollRectExtensions
{
	public static Vector2 GetSnapToPositionToBringChildIntoView(this ScrollRect instance, RectTransform child)
	{
		Canvas.ForceUpdateCanvases();
		Vector2 vector = instance.viewport.localPosition;
		Vector2 vector2 = child.localPosition;
		return new Vector2(0f - (vector.x + vector2.x), 0f - (vector.y + vector2.y));
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Season
public enum Season
{
	Spring = 1,
	Summer = 2,
	Autumn = 4,
	Winter = 8,
	Void = 0x10,
	Glow = 0x20,
	Glitch = 0x40
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SeasonalObject
using System.Collections;
using Heathen.SteamworksIntegration;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class SeasonalObject : MonoBehaviour
{
	public UnityEvent IntoSeason;

	public UnityEvent OutOfSeason;

	public float timeBetweenChecks = 0.1f;

	[EnumFlags]
	public Season seasons;

	private bool inSeason;

	private void Start()
	{
		StartCoroutine(CheckSeason());
	}

	private IEnumerator CheckSeason()
	{
		while (true)
		{
			Season seasonAtPosition = SeasonChanger.instance.GetSeasonAtPosition(base.transform.position);
			if ((seasons & seasonAtPosition) == 0)
			{
				if (inSeason)
				{
					OutOfSeason.Invoke();
					inSeason = false;
				}
			}
			else if (!inSeason)
			{
				IntoSeason.Invoke();
				inSeason = true;
			}
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(timeBetweenChecks);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SeasonChanger
using System;
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class SeasonChanger : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 mapMin = Vector3.zero;

	public Vector3 mapMax = Vector3.zero;

	public RenderTexture seasonMap;

	public MeshRenderer seasonMarkerPrefab;

	public Material[] squareMaterials;

	public Material[] circleMaterials;

	public float timeBetweenSeasons = 3f;

	public float growthTime = 15f;

	private Texture2D lastReadPixel;

	public static SeasonChanger instance;

	private List<Transform> outstandingSeasons = new List<Transform>();

	private void Awake()
	{
		instance = this;
		lastReadPixel = new Texture2D(1, 1, TextureFormat.RGBA32, mipChain: false, linear: false);
		StartCoroutine(DoSeasonSequence());
	}

	public Season GetSeasonAtPosition(Vector3 pos)
	{
		try
		{
			Vector2Int vector2Int = new Vector2Int(Mathf.FloorToInt((pos.x - mapMin.x) * (float)seasonMap.width / (mapMax.x - mapMin.x)), Mathf.FloorToInt((pos.z - mapMin.z) * (float)seasonMap.height / (mapMax.z - mapMin.z)));
			RenderTexture.active = seasonMap;
			lastReadPixel.ReadPixels(new Rect(vector2Int.x, vector2Int.y, 1f, 1f), 0, 0);
			RenderTexture.active = null;
			int num = Mathf.CeilToInt(lastReadPixel.GetPixel(0, 0).r / 0.125f);
			return (Season)(1 << num);
		}
		catch (Exception message)
		{
			Debug.Log(message);
		}
		return Season.Spring;
	}

	private IEnumerator DoSeasonSequence()
	{
		while (true)
		{
			yield return new WaitForSeconds(timeBetweenSeasons);
			if (outstandingSeasons.Count > 30)
			{
				UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(outstandingSeasons[0].gameObject);
				outstandingSeasons.RemoveAt(0);
			}
			foreach (Transform outstandingSeason in outstandingSeasons)
			{
				outstandingSeason.transform.Translate(Vector3.down * 0.2f, Space.World);
			}
			Vector3 position = new Vector3(UnityEngine.Random.Range(mapMin.x, mapMax.x), 10f, UnityEngine.Random.Range(mapMin.z, mapMax.z));
			Quaternion rotation = Quaternion.Euler(0f, UnityEngine.Random.Range(0, 360), 0f);
			MeshRenderer meshRenderer = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(seasonMarkerPrefab, position, rotation);
			Material[] array = ((UnityEngine.Random.value < 0.5f) ? squareMaterials : circleMaterials);
			Material sharedMaterial = array[UnityEngine.Random.Range(0, array.Length)];
			meshRenderer.sharedMaterial = sharedMaterial;
			meshRenderer.transform.localScale = Vector3.one * 0.001f;
			meshRenderer.transform.DOScale(Vector3.one * ((mapMax.x - mapMin.x) * 2f), growthTime);
			outstandingSeasons.Add(meshRenderer.transform);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SettingsMenu
using System.Collections.Generic;
using TMPro;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Audio;
using UnityEngine.EventSystems;

using UnityEngine.Localization.Settings;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class SettingsMenu : MonoBehaviour
{
	[Header("General")]
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject generalSubmenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject generalBtnHighlight;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Dropdown languageDropdown;

	[SerializeField]

	[SerializeField]
	private Toggle deathCountToggle;

	[Header("Audio")]
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject audioSubmenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject audioBtnHighlight;

	[SerializeField]
	private AudioMixer audioMixer;

	[SerializeField]
	private Slider masterVolumeSlider;

	[SerializeField]
	private Slider musicVolumeSlider;

	[SerializeField]
	private Slider sfxVolumeSlider;

	[SerializeField]
	private Slider ambianceVolumeSlider;

	[SerializeField]
	private Slider menuVolumeSlider;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Text masterVolumeNumber;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Text musicVolumeNumber;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Text sfxVolumeNumber;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Text ambianceVolumeNumber;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Text menuVolumeNumber;

	[SerializeField]
	private float saveDelay = 1f;

	[Header("Visuals")]
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject visualsSubmenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject visualsBtnHighlight;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Dropdown fullScreenMode;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Dropdown quality;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Dropdown resolutionsDropdown;

	[SerializeField]
	private TMP_Dropdown vsyncDropdown;

	[Header("Controls")]
	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject controlsSubmenu;

	[SerializeField]
	private GameObject controlsBtnHighlight;

	private float saveTime = float.MaxValue;

	private Resolution[] resolutions;

	private GameObject storedSelection;

	public void ToGeneralSubmenu()
	{
		generalSubmenu.SetActive(value: true);
		audioSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		controlsSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		visualsSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		generalBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: true);
		audioBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		visualsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		controlsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
	}

	public void ToAudioSubmenu()
	{
		generalSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		audioSubmenu.SetActive(value: true);
		controlsSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		visualsSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		generalBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		audioBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: true);
		visualsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		controlsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
	}

	public void ToVisualsSubmenu()
	{
		generalSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		audioSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		controlsSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		visualsSubmenu.SetActive(value: true);
		generalBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		audioBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		visualsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: true);
		controlsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
	}

	public void ToControlsSubmenu()
	{
		generalSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		audioSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		controlsSubmenu.SetActive(value: true);
		visualsSubmenu.SetActive(value: false);
		generalBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		audioBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		visualsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: false);
		controlsBtnHighlight.SetActive(value: true);
	}

	public void LoadSettings()
	{
		int num = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("volume_master", 50);
		masterVolumeSlider.value = num;
		masterVolumeNumber.text = num.ToString();
		audioMixer.SetFloat("MasterVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(num));
		int num2 = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("volume_music", 50);
		musicVolumeSlider.value = num2;
		musicVolumeNumber.text = num2.ToString();
		audioMixer.SetFloat("MusicVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(num2));
		int num3 = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("volume_sfx", 50);
		sfxVolumeSlider.value = num3;
		sfxVolumeNumber.text = num3.ToString();
		audioMixer.SetFloat("SfxVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(num3));
		int num4 = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("volume_ambiance", 50);
		ambianceVolumeSlider.value = num4;
		ambianceVolumeNumber.text = num4.ToString();
		audioMixer.SetFloat("AmbianceVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(num4));
		int num5 = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("volume_menu", 50);
		menuVolumeSlider.value = num5;
		menuVolumeNumber.text = num5.ToString();
		audioMixer.SetFloat("UiVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(num5));
		int num6 = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("shadowQuality", 0);
		quality.value = num6;
		quality.RefreshShownValue();
		QualitySettings.SetQualityLevel(num6);
		switch (PlayerPrefs.GetInt("vsync", 1))
		{
		case 0:
			vsyncDropdown.value = 2;
			break;
		case 1:
			vsyncDropdown.value = 0;
			break;
		case 2:
			vsyncDropdown.value = 1;
			break;
		}
		vsyncDropdown.RefreshShownValue();
		string text = PlayerPrefs.GetString("locale", "en");
		for (int i = 0; i < LocalizationSettings.AvailableLocales.Locales.Count; i++)
		{
			Locale locale = LocalizationSettings.AvailableLocales.Locales[i];
			if (locale.Identifier.Code == text)
			{
				LocalizationSettings.SelectedLocale = locale;
				languageDropdown.value = i;
				break;
			}
		}
		bool flag = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("deathCount", 0) > 0;
		deathCountToggle.isOn = flag;
		GameManager.instance.SetDeathCountVisible(flag);
		bool flag2 = PlayerPrefs.GetInt("timer", 0) > 0;
		timerToggle.isOn = flag2;
		GameManager.instance.SetTimerVisible(flag2);
	}

	private void Awake()
	{
		LoadSettings();
		masterVolumeSlider.onValueChanged.AddListener(MasterVolumeChanged);
		musicVolumeSlider.onValueChanged.AddListener(MusicVolumeChanged);
		sfxVolumeSlider.onValueChanged.AddListener(SfxVolumeChanged);
		ambianceVolumeSlider.onValueChanged.AddListener(AmbianceVolumeChanged);
		menuVolumeSlider.onValueChanged.AddListener(MenuVolumeChanged);
		languageDropdown.onValueChanged.AddListener(OnLanguageChange);
		fullScreenMode.value = (int)Screen.fullScreenMode;
		fullScreenMode.onValueChanged.AddListener(FullScreenChanged);
		vsyncDropdown.onValueChanged.AddListener(VsyncChanged);
		quality.onValueChanged.AddListener(QualityChanged);
		deathCountToggle.onValueChanged.AddListener(DeathCountChanged);
		timerToggle.onValueChanged.AddListener(TimerChanged);
		GetDistinctResolutions();
		resolutionsDropdown.ClearOptions();
		int value = 0;
		List<string> list = new List<string>();
		for (int i = 0; i < resolutions.Length; i++)
		{
			string item = $"{resolutions[i].width} x {resolutions[i].height}";
			list.Add(item);
			if (resolutions[i].width == Screen.currentResolution.width && resolutions[i].height == Screen.currentResolution.height)
			{
				value = i;
			}
		}
		resolutionsDropdown.AddOptions(list);
		resolutionsDropdown.value = value;
		resolutionsDropdown.RefreshShownValue();
		resolutionsDropdown.onValueChanged.AddListener(ChangeResolution);
	}

	private void TimerChanged(bool arg0)
	{
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("timer", arg0 ? 1 : 0);
		GameManager.instance.SetTimerVisible(arg0);
	}

	private void DeathCountChanged(bool arg0)
	{
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("deathCount", arg0 ? 1 : 0);
		GameManager.instance.SetDeathCountVisible(arg0);
	}

	private void OnLanguageChange(int index)
	{
		Locale locale = LocalizationSettings.AvailableLocales.Locales[index];
		PlayerPrefs.SetString("locale", locale.Identifier.Code);
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void ChangeResolution(int index)
	{
		Resolution resolution = resolutions[index];
		Screen.SetResolution(resolution.width, resolution.height, Screen.fullScreen);
	}

	private void QualityChanged(int val)
	{
		QualitySettings.SetQualityLevel(val);
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("shadowQuality", val);
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void FullScreenChanged(int val)
	{
		Screen.fullScreenMode = (FullScreenMode)val;
	}

	private void VsyncChanged(int val)
	{
		switch (val)
		{
		case 0:
			QualitySettings.vSyncCount = 1;
			PlayerPrefs.SetInt("vsync", Mathf.RoundToInt(1f));
			break;
		case 1:
			QualitySettings.vSyncCount = 2;
			PlayerPrefs.SetInt("vsync", Mathf.RoundToInt(2f));
			break;
		case 2:
			QualitySettings.vSyncCount = 0;
			PlayerPrefs.SetInt("vsync", Mathf.RoundToInt(0f));
			break;
		}
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (saveTime < saveDelay)
		{
			saveTime += Time.deltaTime;
			if (saveTime >= saveDelay)
			{
				PlayerPrefs.Save();
			}
		}
	}

	private void MasterVolumeChanged(float val)
	{
		audioMixer.SetFloat("MasterVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(val));
		masterVolumeNumber.text = Mathf.RoundToInt(val).ToString();
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("volume_master", Mathf.RoundToInt(val));
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void MusicVolumeChanged(float val)
	{
		audioMixer.SetFloat("MusicVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(val));
		musicVolumeNumber.text = Mathf.RoundToInt(val).ToString();
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("volume_music", Mathf.RoundToInt(val));
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void SfxVolumeChanged(float val)
	{
		audioMixer.SetFloat("SfxVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(val));
		sfxVolumeNumber.text = Mathf.RoundToInt(val).ToString();
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("volume_sfx", Mathf.RoundToInt(val));
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void AmbianceVolumeChanged(float val)
	{
		audioMixer.SetFloat("AmbianceVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(val));
		ambianceVolumeNumber.text = Mathf.RoundToInt(val).ToString();
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("volume_ambiance", Mathf.RoundToInt(val));
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private void MenuVolumeChanged(float val)
	{
		audioMixer.SetFloat("UiVolume", SliderToMixerVolume(val));
		menuVolumeNumber.text = Mathf.RoundToInt(val).ToString();
		PlayerPrefs.SetInt("volume_menu", Mathf.RoundToInt(val));
		saveTime = 0f;
	}

	private float SliderToMixerVolume(float val)
	{
		return Mathf.Log10(val / 50f + 0.001f) * 20f;
	}

	private void GetDistinctResolutions()
	{
		List<Resolution> list = new List<Resolution>();
		Resolution[] array = Screen.resolutions;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			Resolution item = array[i];
			bool flag = false;
			foreach (Resolution item2 in list)
			{
				if (item.width == item2.width && item.height == item2.height)
				{
					flag = true;
					break;
				}
			}
			if (!flag)
			{
				list.Add(item);
			}
		}
		resolutions = list.ToArray();
	}

	public void StoreSelection()
	{
		storedSelection = EventSystem.current.currentSelectedGameObject;
		EventSystem.current.SetSelectedGameObject(null);
	}

	public void ReturnStoredSelection()
	{
		EventSystem.current.SetSelectedGameObject(storedSelection);
	}
}

}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ShatterAxe
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class ShatterAxe : HeldAxe
{
	public GameObject[] axePieces;

	public GameObject attachedAxeHead;

	public bool breakOnHit;

	public LayerMask layerMask;

	private bool broken;

	private bool swinging;

	public override bool Swing()
	{
		if (!broken)
		{
			StartCoroutine(ResetAfterTime());
		}
		return true;
	}

	private IEnumerator ResetAfterTime()
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.1f);
		swinging = true;
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.2f);
		swinging = false;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (swinging && InLayerMask(other.gameObject.layer, layerMask))
		{
			PlayerData.activeFile.RecordAxeBreak(AxeType.Shatter);
			broken = true;
			attachedAxeHead.SetActive(value: false);
			GameObject[] array = axePieces;
			foreach (GameObject obj in array)
			{
				obj.SetActive(value: true);
				obj.transform.SetParent(null);
			}
		}
	}

	private bool InLayerMask(int layer, LayerMask mask)
	{
		return (mask.value & (1 << layer)) != 0;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ShrinkAxe
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class ShrinkAxe : HeldAxe
{
	public float shrinkTime = 6f;

	private void Awake()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoShrink());
	}

	public override bool Swing()
	{
		return true;
	}

	private IEnumerator DoShrink()
	{
		base.transform.DOScale(0.1f, shrinkTime).SetEase(Ease.InQuad);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(shrinkTime);
		PlayerData.activeFile.RecordAxeBreak(AxeType.Shrink);
		PlayerController.instance.StopHoldingAxe();
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SimpleFollow
using UnityEngine;

public class SimpleFollow : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform target;

	public float speed = 0.2f;

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		Vector3 vector = new Vector3(target.position.x, base.transform.position.y, target.position.z);
		base.transform.position = Vector3.MoveTowards(base.transform.position, vector, speed * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SimpleTriggerEvent
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class SimpleTriggerEvent : MonoBehaviour
{
	public UnityEvent onTrigger;

	public bool triggeredByNonPlayer;

	public bool disableAfter = true;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (triggeredByNonPlayer || (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>()))
		{
			onTrigger.Invoke();
			if (disableAfter)
			{
				base.enabled = false;
			}
		}
	}
}

				s = RuleType.Yes,
				se = RuleType.No
			},
			rotate = false
		}
	};

	public TempChunkObject GetObject(Adjacencies adj, Vector3 worldPos)
	{
		int rotation = 0;
		Rule rule = null;
		if (SkipRender(adj))
		{
			return null;
		}
		foreach (Rule rule2 in rules)
		{
			bool flag = false;
			if ((!rule2.rotate) ? CheckAdjacency(adj, rule2.adjacencies) : CheckAdjacencyWithRotation(adj, rule2.adjacencies, out rotation))
			{
				rule = rule2;
				break;
			}
		}
		if (rule != null && (bool)rule.tileChunkData)
		{
			return new TempChunkObject
			{
				mat = rule.tileChunkData.rend.sharedMaterial,
				mesh = rule.tileChunkData.meshFilter.sharedMesh,
				rot = rotation
			};
		}
		return null;
	}

	private bool CheckAdjacencyWithRotation(Adjacencies actual, Adjacencies required, out int rotation)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++)
		{
			if (CheckAdjacency(actual, required))
			{
				rotation = i;
				return true;
			}
			actual.RotateClockwise();
		}
		rotation = -1;
		return false;
	}

	private bool CheckAdjacency(Adjacencies actual, Adjacencies required)
	{
		if ((required.nw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.nw == required.nw) && (required.n == RuleType.DontCare || actual.n == required.n) && (required.ne == RuleType.DontCare || actual.ne == required.ne) && (required.w == RuleType.DontCare || actual.w == required.w) && (required.e == RuleType.DontCare || actual.e == required.e) && (required.sw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.sw == required.sw) && (required.s == RuleType.DontCare || actual.s == required.s) && (required.se == RuleType.DontCare || actual.se == required.se) && (required.above == RuleType.DontCare || actual.above == required.above) && (required.a_nw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_nw == required.a_nw) && (required.a_n == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_n == required.a_n) && (required.a_ne == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_ne == required.a_ne) && (required.a_w == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_w == required.a_w) && (required.a_e == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_e == required.a_e) && (required.a_sw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_sw == required.a_sw) && (required.a_s == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_s == required.a_s) && (required.a_se == RuleType.DontCare || actual.a_se == required.a_se) && (required.below == RuleType.DontCare || actual.below == required.below) && (required.b_nw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_nw == required.b_nw) && (required.b_n == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_n == required.b_n) && (required.b_ne == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_ne == required.b_ne) && (required.b_w == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_w == required.b_w) && (required.b_e == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_e == required.b_e) && (required.b_sw == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_sw == required.b_sw) && (required.b_s == RuleType.DontCare || actual.b_s == required.b_s))
		{
			if (required.b_se != RuleType.DontCare)
			{
				return actual.b_se == required.b_se;
			}
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	private bool SkipRender(Adjacencies adj)
	{
		if (adj.n == RuleType.Yes && adj.s == RuleType.Yes && adj.e == RuleType.Yes && adj.w == RuleType.Yes && adj.nw == RuleType.Yes && adj.ne == RuleType.Yes && adj.sw == RuleType.Yes && adj.se == RuleType.Yes && adj.above == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_ne == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_n == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_nw == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_e == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_w == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_se == RuleType.Yes && adj.a_s == RuleType.Yes)
		{
			return adj.sw == RuleType.Yes;
		}
		return false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SneakTree
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class SneakTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public enum FollowState
	{
		Inactive,
		Following,
		Hiding
	}

	[SerializeField]
	private float maxSpeed = 10f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float timeToMaxSpeed = 3f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float hideSpeed = 20f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float hideSpotForgiveness = 0.2f;

	[SerializeField]
	private AnimationCurve speedCurve;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform[] hideSpots;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform followStart;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform followEnd;

	[SerializeField]
	private UnityEvent OnHide;

	[SerializeField]
	private UnityEvent OnFollow;

	private FollowState state;

	private float followTimer;

	public void StartFollowing()
	{
		state = FollowState.Hiding;
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (PlayerController.instance.dead || PlayerController.instance.transform.position.z > followStart.position.z + 1f || PlayerController.instance.transform.position.z < followStart.position.z - 1f)
		{
			return;
		}
		if (state == FollowState.Hiding && PlayerController.instance.transform.forward.x >= 0f)
		{
			state = FollowState.Following;
			followTimer = 0f;
			OnFollow.Invoke();
		}
		else if (state == FollowState.Following && PlayerController.instance.transform.forward.x < 0f)
		{
			state = FollowState.Hiding;
			OnHide.Invoke();
		}
		if (state == FollowState.Following && base.transform.position.x < followEnd.position.x)
		{
			float num = speedCurve.Evaluate(followTimer / timeToMaxSpeed) * maxSpeed * Time.deltaTime;
			if (base.transform.position.z < followStart.position.z)
			{
				float num2 = Mathf.Clamp(base.transform.position.z + num, base.transform.position.z, followStart.position.z);
				num -= num2 - base.transform.position.z;
				base.transform.position = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, base.transform.position.y, num2);
			}
			else if (base.transform.position.z > followStart.position.z)
			{
				float num3 = Mathf.Clamp(base.transform.position.z - num, followStart.position.z, base.transform.position.z);
				num -= base.transform.position.z - num3;
				base.transform.position = new Vector3(base.transform.position.x, base.transform.position.y, num3);
			}
			if (num > 0f)
			{
				base.transform.Translate(Vector3.right * num, Space.World);
			}
			followTimer += Time.deltaTime;
		}
		else
		{
			if (state != FollowState.Hiding)
			{
				return;
			}
			Transform transform = hideSpots[0];
			for (int i = 0; i < hideSpots.Length; i++)
			{
				if (hideSpots[i].position.x + hideSpotForgiveness > base.transform.position.x)
				{
					transform = hideSpots[i];
					break;
				}
			}
			base.transform.position = Vector3.MoveTowards(base.transform.position, transform.position, hideSpeed * Time.deltaTime);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SpiderCoordinator
using MoreMountains.Tools;
using UnityEngine;

public class SpiderCoordinator : MonoBehaviour
{
	public SpiderPlant[] spiders;

	public Transform[] destinations;

	public GameObject[] triggers;

	public void Shuffle(GameObject sourceTrigger)
	{
		GameObject[] array = triggers;
		foreach (GameObject obj in array)
		{
			obj.SetActive(obj != sourceTrigger);
		}
		Transform[] array2 = destinations.MMShuffle();
		for (int j = 0; j < spiders.Length; j++)
		{
			spiders[j].controller.followTarget = array2[j];
			spiders[j].Activate();
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// SpiderPlant
using System.Collections;
using DG.Tweening;
using ProceduralSpider;
using UnityEngine;

public class SpiderPlant : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private MonoBehaviour[] scriptsToActivate;

	[SerializeField]
	private Collider col;

	[SerializeField]
	private Collider inactiveCol;

	[SerializeField]
	private Rigidbody rb;

	[SerializeField]
	private Transform[] legs;

	[SerializeField]
	private float legEndScale = 1f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float raiseHeight = 0.5f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float startTime = 0.5f;

	public SpiderNPCController controller;

	private bool activated;

	private void Start()
	{
		Transform[] array = legs;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			array[i].localScale = Vector3.one * 0.01f;
		}
	}

	public void Activate()
	{
		if (!activated && (controller.followTarget == null || Vector3.Distance(base.transform.position, controller.followTarget.position) >= 0.5f))
		{
			activated = true;
			StartCoroutine(DoActivation());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoActivation()
	{
		inactiveCol.enabled = false;
		col.enabled = true;
		rb.isKinematic = false;
		Transform[] array = legs;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			array[i].DOScale(legEndScale, startTime);
		}
		float endValue = base.transform.position.y + raiseHeight;
		base.transform.DOMoveY(endValue, startTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(startTime);
		MonoBehaviour[] array2 = scriptsToActivate;
		for (int i = 0; i < array2.Length; i++)
		{
			array2[i].enabled = true;
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (activated && Vector3.Distance(base.transform.position, controller.followTarget.position) < 0.5f)
		{
			Deactivate();
		}
	}

	public void Deactivate()
	{
		if (activated)
		{
			activated = false;
			StartCoroutine(DoDeactivation());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoDeactivation()
	{
		col.enabled = false;
		rb.isKinematic = true;
		Transform[] array = legs;
		for (int i = 0; i < array.Length; i++)
		{
			array[i].DOScale(0.01f, startTime);
		}
		if (controller.followTarget != null)
		{
			base.transform.DOMove(controller.followTarget.position, startTime);
		}
		else
		{
			float endValue = base.transform.position.y - raiseHeight;
			base.transform.DOMoveY(endValue, startTime);
		}
		base.transform.DORotateQuaternion(Quaternion.identity, startTime);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(startTime);
		MonoBehaviour[] array2 = scriptsToActivate;
		for (int i = 0; i < array2.Length; i++)
		{
			array2[i].enabled = false;
		}
		inactiveCol.enabled = true;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Stickerbush
using UnityEngine;

public class Stickerbush : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private float speedMult = 0.5f;

	[SerializeField]
	private float maxLimbOffset = 0.2f;

	public void Attach()
	{
		Rigidbody[] rigidbodies = PlayerController.instance.ragdoll.rigidbodies;
		Rigidbody rigidbody = rigidbodies[Random.Range(0, rigidbodies.Length)];
		base.transform.SetParent(rigidbody.transform, worldPositionStays: true);
		base.transform.localPosition = new Vector3(Random.Range(0f - maxLimbOffset, maxLimbOffset), Random.Range(0f - maxLimbOffset, maxLimbOffset), Random.Range(0f - maxLimbOffset, maxLimbOffset));
		base.transform.rotation = Random.rotation;
		PlayerController.instance.speedMult *= speedMult;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Teleporter
using Unity.Cinemachine;
using UnityEngine;

public class Teleporter : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 teleportDist;

	public void Teleport()
	{
		CinemachineCamera cineCam = GameManager.instance.cineCam;
		PlayerController.instance.rb.position += teleportDist;
		PlayerController.instance.transform.position = PlayerController.instance.rb.position;
		cineCam.OnTargetObjectWarped(PlayerController.instance.transform, teleportDist);
	}
}
