// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// ThiefTree
using System;
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class ThiefTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	public GameObject[] phaseColliders;

	public Animator anim;

	private int state = -1;

	public Transform leftBranch;

	public Transform rightBranch;

	private bool canAdvance;

	[NonSerialized]
	public Hat hat;

	public void AdvanceState()
	{
		if (canAdvance)
		{
			if (state >= 0)
			{
				anim.SetTrigger("advance");
			}
			if (state >= 0 && state < phaseColliders.Length)
			{
				phaseColliders[state].SetActive(value: false);
			}
			state++;
			if (state >= 0 && state < phaseColliders.Length)
			{
				phaseColliders[state].SetActive(value: true);
			}
		}
	}

	public void AdvanceStateDelay(float time)
	{
		StartCoroutine(AdvanceDelayed(time));
	}

	private IEnumerator AdvanceDelayed(float time)
	{
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(time);
		canAdvance = true;
		AdvanceState();
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		AdvanceState();
	}

	public void BreakHat()
	{
		hat.Break(leftBranch, rightBranch);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TileChunk
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;
using UnityEngine;

[Serializable]
public class TileChunk : ScriptableObject
{
	public List<GameObject> chunkPieces = new List<GameObject>();

	public void RebuildRange(Tilemap tilemap, Vector3Int min, Vector3Int max)
	{
		Dictionary<int, TempChunkData> dictionary = new Dictionary<int, TempChunkData>();
		Vector3 size = new Vector3(tilemap.tileWidth, tilemap.levelHeight, tilemap.tileWidth);
		for (int i = min.x; i < max.x; i++)
		{
			for (int j = min.y; j < max.y; j++)
			{
				for (int k = min.z; k < max.z; k++)
				{
					int num = tilemap.data[i, j, k];
					if (num < 100 && num > 0)
					{
						int index = tilemap.ToTileTypeIndex(num, 0);
						TileType tileType = tilemap.tileSet.tileTypes[index];
						SmartTile smartTile = null;
						if (tileType.GetType() == typeof(MatSwapTile))
						{
							smartTile = ((MatSwapTile)tileType).baseTile;
						}
						else if (tileType.GetType() == typeof(SmartTile))
						{
							smartTile = (SmartTile)tileType;
						}
						if (!(smartTile != null))
						{
							continue;
						}
						Adjacencies adjacencies = tilemap.GetAdjacencies(new Vector3Int(i, j, k));
						Vector3 vector = new Vector3((float)i * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f, (float)j * tilemap.levelHeight + tilemap.levelHeight / 2f, (float)k * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f);
						TempChunkObject tempChunkObject = smartTile.GetObject(adjacencies, vector);
						if (!dictionary.ContainsKey(num))
						{
							TempChunkData tempChunkData = new TempChunkData();
							tempChunkData.tag = tileType.tag;
							tempChunkData.layerMask = smartTile.rules[0].tileChunkData.rend.renderingLayerMask;
							tempChunkData.colliderBounds = new Bounds?[max.x - min.x, max.y - min.y, max.z - min.z];
							dictionary.Add(num, tempChunkData);
						}
						if (tempChunkObject != null)
						{
							if (tileType.GetType() == typeof(MatSwapTile))
							{
								tempChunkObject.mat = ((MatSwapTile)tileType).newMaterial;
							}
							if (dictionary[num].mat == null)
							{
								dictionary[num].mat = tempChunkObject.mat;
							}
							dictionary[num].meshes.Add(tempChunkObject.mesh);
							dictionary[num].worldPos.Add(vector);
							dictionary[num].rotations.Add(tempChunkObject.rot);
						}
						dictionary[num].colliderBounds[i - min.x, j - min.y, k - min.z] = new Bounds(vector, size);
					}
					else
					{
						if (num < 1000)
						{
							continue;
						}
						int index2 = (num - 1000) % 1000;
						OverrideTile overrideTile = (OverrideTile)tilemap.tileSet.tileTypes[index2];
						Adjacencies adjacencies2 = tilemap.GetAdjacencies(new Vector3Int(i, j, k));
						Vector3 vector2 = new Vector3((float)i * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f, (float)j * tilemap.levelHeight + tilemap.levelHeight / 2f, (float)k * tilemap.tileWidth + tilemap.tileWidth / 2f);
						if (!dictionary.ContainsKey(num))
						{
							TempChunkData tempChunkData2 = new TempChunkData();
							tempChunkData2.tag = overrideTile.tag;
							tempChunkData2.layerMask = overrideTile.quad.rend.renderingLayerMask;
							tempChunkData2.colliderBounds = new Bounds?[max.x - min.x, max.y - min.y, max.z - min.z];
							dictionary.Add(num, tempChunkData2);
						}
						TempChunkObject tempChunkObject2 = overrideTile.GetObject(adjacencies2);
						if (tempChunkObject2 != null)
						{
							if (dictionary[num].mat == null)
							{
								dictionary[num].mat = tempChunkObject2.mat;
							}
							dictionary[num].meshes.Add(tempChunkObject2.mesh);
							dictionary[num].worldPos.Add(vector2);
							dictionary[num].rotations.Add(tempChunkObject2.rot);
						}
						dictionary[num].colliderBounds[i - min.x, j - min.y, k - min.z] = new Bounds(vector2, size);
					}
				}
			}
		}
		RebuildFromData(dictionary.Values.ToArray(), tilemap);
	}

	private List<Bounds> OptimizeBounds(Bounds?[,,] b)
	{
		List<Bounds> list = new List<Bounds>();
		for (int i = 0; i < b.GetLength(0); i++)
		{
			for (int j = 0; j < b.GetLength(1); j++)
			{
				for (int k = 0; k < b.GetLength(2); k++)
				{
					if (!b[i, j, k].HasValue)
					{
						continue;
					}
					Bounds value = b[i, j, k].Value;
					b[i, j, k] = null;
					Vector3Int one = Vector3Int.one;
					while (i + one.x < b.GetLength(0) && b[i + one.x, j, k].HasValue)
					{
						value.Encapsulate(b[i + one.x, j, k].Value);
						b[i + one.x, j, k] = null;
						one.x++;
					}
					while (j + one.y < b.GetLength(1) && WholeRowNotNull(b, i, j + one.y, k, one.x))
					{
						value.Encapsulate(b[i, j + one.y, k].Value);
						for (int l = 0; l < one.x; l++)
						{
							b[i + l, j + one.y, k] = null;
						}
						one.y++;
					}
					while (k + one.z < b.GetLength(2) && WholeSquareNotNull(b, i, j, k + one.z, one.x, one.y))
					{
						value.Encapsulate(b[i, j, k + one.z].Value);
						for (int m = 0; m < one.x; m++)
						{
							for (int n = 0; n < one.y; n++)
							{
								b[i + m, j + n, k + one.z] = null;
							}
						}
						one.z++;
					}
					list.Add(value);
				}
			}
		}
		return list;
	}

	private bool WholeRowNotNull(Bounds?[,,] b, int x, int y, int z, int width)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < width; i++)
		{
			if (!b[x + i, y, z].HasValue)
			{
				return false;
			}
		}
		return true;
	}

	private bool WholeSquareNotNull(Bounds?[,,] b, int x, int y, int z, int width, int height)
	{
		for (int i = 0; i < height; i++)
		{
			if (!WholeRowNotNull(b, x, y + i, z, width))
			{
				return false;
			}
		}
		return true;
	}

	private void RebuildFromData(TempChunkData[] chunkData, Tilemap tilemap)
	{
		Clear();
		foreach (TempChunkData tempChunkData in chunkData)
		{
			GameObject gameObject = new GameObject();
			gameObject.transform.SetParent(tilemap.mapContainer);
			gameObject.name = "MapChunk";
			if (tempChunkData.tag != null && tempChunkData.tag != "")
			{
				gameObject.tag = tempChunkData.tag;
			}
			MeshFilter meshFilter = gameObject.AddComponent<MeshFilter>();
			MeshRenderer meshRenderer = gameObject.AddComponent<MeshRenderer>();
			meshRenderer.material = tempChunkData.mat;
			meshRenderer.renderingLayerMask = tempChunkData.layerMask;
			CombineInstance[] array = new CombineInstance[tempChunkData.meshes.Count];
			for (int j = 0; j < tempChunkData.meshes.Count; j++)
			{
				array[j].mesh = tempChunkData.meshes[j];
				Quaternion q = Quaternion.Euler(Vector3.down * 90f * tempChunkData.rotations[j]);
				Matrix4x4 transform = Matrix4x4.Translate(tempChunkData.worldPos[j]) * Matrix4x4.Rotate(q);
				array[j].transform = transform;
			}
			Mesh mesh = new Mesh();
			mesh.CombineMeshes(array);
			meshFilter.sharedMesh = mesh;
			chunkPieces.Add(gameObject);
			foreach (Bounds item in OptimizeBounds(tempChunkData.colliderBounds))
			{
				BoxCollider boxCollider = gameObject.AddComponent<BoxCollider>();
				boxCollider.center = item.center;
				boxCollider.size = item.size;
			}
		}
	}

	public void Clear()
	{
		foreach (GameObject chunkPiece in chunkPieces)
		{
			UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(chunkPiece);
		}
		chunkPieces.Clear();
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TileChunkData
using UnityEngine;

public class TileChunkData : MonoBehaviour
{
	public MeshFilter meshFilter;

	public MeshRenderer rend;

	public BoxCollider[] col;
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TileData<T>
using System;

[Serializable]
public class TileData<T>
{
	public T[] data;

	public int xSize;

	public int ySize;

	public int zSize;

	public int xzSize => xSize * zSize;

	public T this[int x, int y, int z]
	{
		get
		{
			return data[xSize * zSize * y + xSize * z + x];
		}
		set
		{
			data[xSize * zSize * y + xSize * z + x] = value;
		}
	}

	public TileData(int xSize, int ySize, int zSize)
	{
		this.xSize = xSize;
		this.ySize = ySize;
		this.zSize = zSize;
		data = new T[xSize * ySize * zSize];
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TileGroupData
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

public class TileGroupData : MonoBehaviour
{
	public List<Vector3Int> otherTilePositions = new List<Vector3Int>();
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// Tilemap
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;

[ExecuteInEditMode]
public class Tilemap : MonoBehaviour
{
	public float levelHeight = 2f;

	public Vector3Int chunkSize = new Vector3Int(5, 5, 5);

	public Vector3Int gridSize = new Vector3Int(20, 5, 20);

	public TileSet tileSet;

	public HouseTileSet houseTileSet;

	public float tileWidth = 4f;

	[SerializeField]
	public TileData<int> data;

	[SerializeField]
	public TileData<GameObject> tiles;

	[SerializeField]
	public TileData<TileChunk> chunks;

	public List<GameObject> placeableObjects;

	public Transform mapContainer;

	public void InitializeData()
	{
		data = new TileData<int>(gridSize.x, gridSize.y, gridSize.z);
		tiles = new TileData<GameObject>(gridSize.x, gridSize.y, gridSize.z);
		chunks = new TileData<TileChunk>(Mathf.CeilToInt((float)gridSize.x / (float)chunkSize.x), Mathf.CeilToInt((float)gridSize.y / (float)chunkSize.y), Mathf.CeilToInt((float)gridSize.z / (float)chunkSize.z));
	}

	public void AddTileGroup(GameObject ob, List<Vector3Int> positions, int height = 1)
	{
		int value = -(positions[0].x + positions[0].y * gridSize.x + positions[0].z * gridSize.x * gridSize.y) - 1;
		for (int i = 0; i < height; i++)
		{
			foreach (Vector3Int position in positions)
			{
				if (position.y + i >= 0 && position.y + i < gridSize.y)
				{
					data[position.x, position.y + i, position.z] = value;
				}
			}
		}
		tiles[positions[0].x, positions[0].y, positions[0].z] = ob;
	}

	public void ChangeTile(Vector3Int position, int tileNum, bool rebuild = true, int rotation = 0)
	{
		if (data == null)
		{
			InitializeData();
		}
		if (position.x >= 0 && position.z >= 0 && position.x < tiles.xSize && position.z < tiles.zSize)
		{
			_ = data[position.x, position.y, position.z];
			if (data[position.x, position.y, position.z] < 0)
			{
				DestroyTileGroup(data[position.x, position.y, position.z]);
			}
			else if (data[position.x, position.y, position.z] >= 100)
			{
				DestroyTileGroup(position);
			}
			if (tileNum == -1)
			{
				data[position.x, position.y, position.z] = 0;
			}
			else
			{
				data[position.x, position.y, position.z] = ToTileCode(tileNum, rotation);
			}
			if (rebuild)
			{
				Vector3Int min = new Vector3Int(position.x - 1, position.y, position.z - 1);
				Vector3Int max = new Vector3Int(position.x + 1, position.y, position.z + 1);
				RebuildRange(min, max);
			}
		}
	}

	public int ToTileCode(int tileTypeIndex, int rotation)
	{
		return tileTypeIndex * 4 + rotation + 1;
	}

	public int ToTileTypeIndex(int tileCode, int rotation)
	{
		return (tileCode - 1 - rotation) / 4;
	}

	public void ChangeOverride(Vector3Int position, int tileNum, bool rebuild = true)
	{
		if (data == null)
		{
			InitializeData();
		}
		if (position.x >= 0 && position.z >= 0 && position.x < tiles.xSize && position.z < tiles.zSize)
		{
			if (data[position.x, position.y, position.z] < 0)
			{
				DestroyTileGroup(data[position.x, position.y, position.z]);
			}
			else if (data[position.x, position.y, position.z] >= 100 && data[position.x, position.y, position.z] < 1000)
			{
				DestroyTileGroup(position);
			}
			int num = data[position.x, position.y, position.z];
			if (num >= 1000)
			{
				num = (num - 1000) / 1000;
			}
			int value = num * 1000 + tileNum + 1000;
			data[position.x, position.y, position.z] = value;
			if (rebuild)
			{
				Vector3Int min = new Vector3Int(position.x - 1, position.y, position.z - 1);
				Vector3Int max = new Vector3Int(position.x + 1, position.y, position.z + 1);
				RebuildRange(min, max);
			}
		}
	}

	public void FillArea(Vector3Int min, Vector3Int max, int tileType)
	{
		ClearRange(min, max);
		for (int i = min.x; i <= max.x; i++)
		{
			for (int j = min.y; j <= max.y; j++)
			{
				for (int k = min.z; k <= max.z; k++)
				{
					if (i >= 0 && j >= 0 && k >= 0 && i < tiles.xSize && j < tiles.ySize && k < tiles.zSize)
					{
						ChangeTile(new Vector3Int(i, j, k), tileType, rebuild: false);
					}
				}
			}
		}
		Vector3Int min2 = new Vector3Int(min.x - 1, min.y, min.z - 1);
		Vector3Int max2 = new Vector3Int(max.x + 1, max.y, max.z + 1);
		RebuildRange(min2, max2);
	}

	public void ClearRange(Vector3Int min, Vector3Int max)
	{
		for (int i = min.x; i <= max.x; i++)
		{
			for (int j = min.y; j <= max.y; j++)
			{
				for (int k = min.z; k <= max.z; k++)
				{
					if (i < 0 || j < 0 || k < 0 || i >= tiles.xSize || j >= tiles.ySize || k >= tiles.zSize)
					{
						continue;
					}
					if (data[i, j, k] < 0)
					{
						DestroyTileGroup(data[i, j, k]);
						continue;
					}
					if (data[i, j, k] >= 100 && data[i, j, k] < 1000)
					{
						DestroyTileGroup(new Vector3Int(i, j, k));
						continue;
					}
					int num = data[i, j, k];
					GameObject gameObject = tiles[i, j, k];
					if (((num < 100 && num > 0) || num >= 1000) && gameObject != null)
					{
						UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(gameObject);
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	public void Regenerate()
	{
		Resize();
		RebuildRange(Vector3Int.zero, new Vector3Int(gridSize.x, gridSize.y, gridSize.z));
	}

	private void Resize()
	{
		TileData<int> tileData = new TileData<int>(gridSize.x, gridSize.y, gridSize.z);
		TileData<GameObject> tileData2 = new TileData<GameObject>(gridSize.x, gridSize.y, gridSize.z);
		for (int i = 0; i < gridSize.x; i++)
		{
			for (int j = 0; j < gridSize.y; j++)
			{
				for (int k = 0; k < gridSize.z; k++)
				{
					if (i < data.xSize && j < data.ySize && k < data.zSize)
					{
						tileData[i, j, k] = data[i, j, k];
					}
					if (i < tiles.xSize && j < tiles.ySize && k < tiles.zSize)
					{
						tileData2[i, j, k] = tiles[i, j, k];
					}
				}
			}
		}
		data = tileData;
		tiles = tileData2;
		if (chunks != null && chunks.data != null)
		{
			TileChunk[] array = chunks.data;
			foreach (TileChunk tileChunk in array)
			{
				if (!(tileChunk != null))
				{
					continue;
				}
				foreach (GameObject chunkPiece in tileChunk.chunkPieces)
				{
					if (chunkPiece != null)
					{
						UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(chunkPiece.gameObject);
					}
				}
			}
		}
		chunks = new TileData<TileChunk>(Mathf.CeilToInt((float)gridSize.x / (float)chunkSize.x), Mathf.CeilToInt((float)gridSize.y / (float)chunkSize.y), Mathf.CeilToInt((float)gridSize.z / (float)chunkSize.z));
	}

	public void RebuildRange(Vector3Int min, Vector3Int max)
	{
		HashSet<Vector3Int> hashSet = new HashSet<Vector3Int>();
		for (int i = min.x; i <= max.x; i++)
		{
			for (int j = min.y; j <= max.y; j++)
			{
				for (int k = min.z; k <= max.z; k++)
				{
					if (i < 0 || j < 0 || k < 0 || i >= tiles.xSize || j >= tiles.ySize || k >= tiles.zSize)
					{
						continue;
					}
					hashSet.Add(new Vector3Int(i / chunkSize.x, j / chunkSize.y, k / chunkSize.z));
					int num = data[i, j, k];
					GameObject gameObject = tiles[i, j, k];
					if ((num < 100 && num > 0) || num > 1000)
					{
						if (gameObject != null)
						{
							UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(gameObject);
						}
						if (num < 100)
						{
							Vector3 worldPos = new Vector3((float)i * tileWidth + tileWidth / 2f, (float)j * levelHeight + levelHeight / 2f, (float)k * tileWidth + tileWidth / 2f);
							TileType tileType = tileSet.tileTypes[(num - 1) / 4];
							GameObject gameObject2 = null;
							if (tileType.GetType() == typeof(BasicTile))
							{
								gameObject2 = ((BasicTile)tileType).GetObject(worldPos, (num - 1) % 4);
							}
							tiles[i, j, k] = gameObject2;
							if (gameObject2 != null)
							{
								gameObject2.transform.parent = mapContainer;
							}
						}
					}
					else if (num == 0 && gameObject != null)
					{
						UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(gameObject);
					}
				}
			}
		}
		RebuildChunks(hashSet);
	}

	private void RebuildChunks(HashSet<Vector3Int> chunkPositions)
	{
		foreach (Vector3Int chunkPosition in chunkPositions)
		{
			Vector3Int min = new Vector3Int(chunkPosition.x * chunkSize.x, chunkPosition.y * chunkSize.y, chunkPosition.z * chunkSize.z);
			Vector3Int max = new Vector3Int(Mathf.Clamp(min.x + chunkSize.x, 0, gridSize.x), Mathf.Clamp(min.y + chunkSize.y, 0, gridSize.y), Mathf.Clamp(min.z + chunkSize.z, 0, gridSize.z));
			if (chunks[chunkPosition.x, chunkPosition.y, chunkPosition.z] == null)
			{
				chunks[chunkPosition.x, chunkPosition.y, chunkPosition.z] = ScriptableObject.CreateInstance<TileChunk>();
			}
			chunks[chunkPosition.x, chunkPosition.y, chunkPosition.z].RebuildRange(this, min, max);
		}
	}

	private void DestroyTileGroup(int dataPt)
	{
		int num = -(dataPt + 1);
		Vector3Int pos = new Vector3Int(num % gridSize.x, num / gridSize.x % gridSize.y, num / (gridSize.x * gridSize.y));
		DestroyTileGroup(pos);
	}

	private void DestroyTileGroup(Vector3Int pos)
	{
		GameObject gameObject = tiles[pos.x, pos.y, pos.z];
		if (gameObject != null)
		{
			TileGroupData component = gameObject.GetComponent<TileGroupData>();
			if (component != null)
			{
				foreach (Vector3Int otherTilePosition in component.otherTilePositions)
				{
					if (tiles[otherTilePosition.x, otherTilePosition.y, otherTilePosition.z] != null)
					{
						UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(tiles[otherTilePosition.x, otherTilePosition.y, otherTilePosition.z]);
					}
					data[otherTilePosition.x, otherTilePosition.y, otherTilePosition.z] = 0;
				}
			}
			UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(gameObject);
		}
		data[pos.x, pos.y, pos.z] = 0;
	}

	private void DestroyAt(Vector3Int pos)
	{
		UnityEngine.Object.Destroy(tiles[pos.x, pos.y, pos.z]);
		data[pos.x, pos.y, pos.z] = 0;
	}

	public void SetObject(int level, Vector2Int position, int objectType)
	{
		if (position.x >= 0 && position.y >= 0 && position.x < tiles.xSize && position.y < tiles.zSize)
		{
			if (tiles[position.x, level, position.y] != null)
			{
				UnityEngine.Object.DestroyImmediate(tiles[position.x, level, position.y]);
			}
			data[position.x, level, position.y] = 200 + objectType;
			GameObject gameObject = UnityEngine.Object.Instantiate(placeableObjects[objectType]);
			tiles[position.x, level, position.y] = gameObject;
			Vector3 position2 = new Vector3((float)position.x * tileWidth + tileWidth / 2f, (float)level * levelHeight + levelHeight / 2f, (float)position.y * tileWidth + tileWidth / 2f);
			gameObject.transform.position = position2;
		}
	}

	public Adjacencies GetAdjacencies(Vector3Int position)
	{
		int num = data[position.x, position.y, position.z];
		bool flag = num >= 1000;
		if (flag)
		{
			num = (num - 1000) % 1000;
		}
		else if (num != 0)
		{
			num = ToTileTypeIndex(num, 0);
			if (tileSet.tileTypes[num].GetType() == typeof(MatSwapTile))
			{
				SmartTile baseTile = ((MatSwapTile)tileSet.tileTypes[num]).baseTile;
				num = tileSet.tileTypes.IndexOf(baseTile);
			}
			num++;
		}
		return new Adjacencies
		{
			nw = ((position.x == 0 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			n = ((position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			ne = ((position.x == data.xSize - 1 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			w = ((position.x == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			e = ((position.x == data.xSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			sw = ((position.x == 0 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			s = ((position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			se = ((position.x == data.xSize - 1 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			above = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y + 1, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_nw = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.x == 0 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y + 1, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_n = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y + 1, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_ne = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.x == data.xSize - 1 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y + 1, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_w = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.x == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y + 1, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_e = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.x == data.xSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y + 1, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_sw = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.x == 0 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y + 1, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_s = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y + 1, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			a_se = ((position.y == data.ySize - 1 || position.x == data.xSize - 1 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y + 1, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			below = ((position.y == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y - 1, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_nw = ((position.y == 0 || position.x == 0 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y - 1, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_n = ((position.y == 0 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y - 1, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_ne = ((position.y == 0 || position.x == data.xSize - 1 || position.z == data.zSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y - 1, position.z + 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_w = ((position.y == 0 || position.x == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y - 1, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_e = ((position.y == 0 || position.x == data.xSize - 1 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y - 1, position.z], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_sw = ((position.y == 0 || position.x == 0 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x - 1, position.y - 1, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_s = ((position.y == 0 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x, position.y - 1, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes),
			b_se = ((position.y == 0 || position.x == data.xSize - 1 || position.z == 0 || TileTypePart(data[position.x + 1, position.y - 1, position.z - 1], flag) != num) ? RuleType.No : RuleType.Yes)
		};
	}

	private int TileTypePart(int tileCode, bool tileOverride = false)
	{
		if (tileCode > 1000)
		{
			if (tileOverride)
			{
				return (tileCode - 1000) % 1000;
			}
			return (tileCode - 1000) / 1000;
		}
		if (tileOverride || tileCode <= 0)
		{
			return 0;
		}
		int num = ToTileTypeIndex(tileCode, 0);
		try
		{
			if (tileSet.tileTypes[num].GetType() == typeof(MatSwapTile))
			{
				SmartTile baseTile = ((MatSwapTile)tileSet.tileTypes[num]).baseTile;
				num = tileSet.tileTypes.IndexOf(baseTile);
			}
			return num + 1;
		}
		catch (Exception message)
		{
			Debug.LogError(message);
			return 0;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TreeBlocker
using System.Collections.Generic;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class TreeBlocker : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Animator anim;

	public int stateCount = 3;

	public UnityEvent onAllStatesVisited;

	private List<string> visitedStates = new List<string>();

	public void SetBlock(string blockType, bool blocked)
	{
		anim.SetBool(blockType, blocked);
		if (!visitedStates.Contains(blockType))
		{
			visitedStates.Add(blockType);
			if (visitedStates.Count == stateCount)
			{
				onAllStatesVisited.Invoke();
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TreeBlockTrigger
using UnityEngine;

public class TreeBlockTrigger : MonoBehaviour
{
	public TreeBlocker tree;

	public string blockName;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			tree.SetBlock(blockName, blocked: true);
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			tree.SetBlock(blockName, blocked: false);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TripTree
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class TripTree : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Animator anim;

	[SerializeField]
	private Tripper tripper;

	[SerializeField]
	private float cooldown = 1f;

	private bool tripping;

	private bool onCooldown;

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if ((bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>() && !tripping)
		{
			anim.SetBool("trip", value: true);
			tripper.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
			tripping = true;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (other.GetComponent<PlayerController>() != null && tripping && !onCooldown)
		{
			StartCoroutine(DoCooldown());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator DoCooldown()
	{
		onCooldown = true;
		anim.SetBool("trip", value: false);
		tripper.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(cooldown);
		tripping = false;
		onCooldown = false;
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TweenedPos
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class TweenedPos : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 posChange;

	public float time;

	private bool tweened;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	private void Awake()
	{
		startPos = base.transform.position;
	}

	public void Tween()
	{
		if (!tweened)
		{
			tweened = true;
			base.transform.DOMove(startPos + posChange, time);
		}
	}

	public void UnTween()
	{
		if (tweened)
		{
			tweened = false;
			base.transform.DOMove(startPos, time);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// TweenRot
using DG.Tweening;
using UnityEngine;

public class TweenRot : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Vector3 rotChange;

	public float time;

	private bool tweened;

	private Vector3 startRot;

	private void Awake()
	{
		startRot = base.transform.rotation.eulerAngles;
	}

	public void Tween()
	{
		if (!tweened)
		{
			tweened = true;
			base.transform.DOLocalRotate(startRot + rotChange, time);
		}
	}

	public void UnTween()
	{
		if (tweened)
		{
			tweened = false;
			base.transform.DOLocalRotate(startRot, time);
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// VolumeWeightByHeight
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Rendering;

public class VolumeWeightByHeight : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private Volume volume;

	[SerializeField]
	private Collider col;

	[SerializeField]
	private AnimationCurve curve;

	[SerializeField]
	private Light dirLight;

	[SerializeField]
	private float goalLightInt;

	private Material newSky;

	private float startFog;

	private float startLightInt;

	private bool inRange;

	private void Start()
	{
		newSky = new Material(RenderSettings.skybox);
		newSky.CopyPropertiesFromMaterial(RenderSettings.skybox);
		newSky.name = "LerpSky";
		RenderSettings.skybox = newSky;
		startFog = RenderSettings.fogDensity;
		startLightInt = dirLight.intensity;
	}

	private void OnTriggerEnter(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = true;
		}
	}

	private void OnTriggerExit(Collider other)
	{
		if (base.enabled && (bool)other.GetComponent<PlayerController>())
		{
			inRange = false;
		}
	}

	private void Update()
	{
		if (inRange)
		{
			float y = PlayerController.instance.transform.position.y;
			float y2 = col.bounds.size.y;
			float time = Mathf.Clamp((y - col.bounds.min.y) / y2, 0f, 1f);
			float num = curve.Evaluate(time);
			volume.weight = num;
			newSky.SetFloat("_Blend", num);
			RenderSettings.fogDensity = startFog * (1f - num);
			float intensity = Mathf.Lerp(startLightInt, goalLightInt, num);
			dirLight.intensity = intensity;
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// WakeUpSequence
using System.Collections;
using UnityEngine;

public class WakeUpSequence : MonoBehaviour
{
	private void Start()
	{
		StartCoroutine(DoWakeUp());
	}

	private IEnumerator DoWakeUp()
	{
		PlayerController player = PlayerController.instance;
		player.AddBlocker(this);
		yield return null;
		player.anim.CrossFade("lyingDown", 0.01f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(3f);
		player.anim.CrossFade("sitUp", 0.1f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(2f);
		player.anim.CrossFade("default", 0.25f);
		yield return new WaitForSeconds(0.3f);
		player.RemoveBlocker(this);
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// WantedPoster
using System.Collections;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using CharacterCreator;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.UI;

public class WantedPoster : MonoBehaviour
{
	[SerializeField]
	private CharacterOptions options;

	[SerializeField]
	private SpriteRenderer protoSprite;

	[SerializeField]
	private Image protoImage;

	[SerializeField]
	private bool autoGenerate = true;

	private List<GameObject> sprites = new List<GameObject>();

	private void Start()
	{
		if (autoGenerate)
		{
			StartCoroutine(GenerateOnDelay());
		}
	}

	private IEnumerator GenerateOnDelay()
	{
		yield return null;
		Generate();
	}

	public void Generate()
	{
		Generate(PlayerData.activeFile.appearance);
	}

	public void Generate(SerializeableChosenOptions appearance)
	{
		foreach (GameObject sprite in sprites)
		{
			Object.Destroy(sprite);
		}
		sprites.Clear();
		foreach (SerializeableChosenOption meshOption in appearance.meshOptions)
		{
			if (meshOption == null || !(options != null) || options.options == null || !options.options.ContainsKey(meshOption.optionType))
			{
				continue;
			}
			CharacterMeshOption[] array = options.options[meshOption.optionType];
			if (array == null)
			{
				continue;
			}
			CharacterMeshOption characterMeshOption = array[meshOption.meshIndex];
			if (!(characterMeshOption != null))
			{
				continue;
			}
			PosterElement[] posterElements = characterMeshOption.posterElements;
			foreach (PosterElement posterElement in posterElements)
			{
				if (!(posterElement.sprite != null) || (posterElement.matIndex >= 0 && posterElement.matIndex != meshOption.materialIndex))
				{
					continue;
				}
				if (protoSprite != null)
				{
					SpriteRenderer spriteRenderer = Object.Instantiate(protoSprite, protoSprite.transform.position, protoSprite.transform.rotation);
					spriteRenderer.transform.SetParent(base.transform);
					spriteRenderer.sprite = posterElement.sprite;
					spriteRenderer.sortingOrder = posterElement.sortingOrder;
					spriteRenderer.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
					spriteRenderer.transform.localScale = protoSprite.transform.localScale;
					sprites.Add(spriteRenderer.gameObject);
					if (characterMeshOption.optionType == CharacterMeshOptionType.Head)
					{
						Color color = options.posterSkinOptions[appearance.skinIndex];
						spriteRenderer.color = color;
					}
					else if (characterMeshOption.optionType == CharacterMeshOptionType.Hair || characterMeshOption.optionType == CharacterMeshOptionType.FacialHair)
					{
						Color color2 = options.posterHairOptions[meshOption.materialIndex];
						spriteRenderer.color = color2;
					}
				}
				else
				{
					Image image = Object.Instantiate(protoImage, protoImage.transform.position, protoImage.transform.rotation);
					image.transform.SetParent(base.transform);
					image.sprite = posterElement.sprite;
					image.transform.SetSiblingIndex(posterElement.sortingOrder);
					image.gameObject.SetActive(value: true);
					image.transform.localScale = protoImage.transform.localScale;
					sprites.Add(image.gameObject);
					if (characterMeshOption.optionType == CharacterMeshOptionType.Head)
					{
						Color color3 = options.posterSkinOptions[appearance.skinIndex];
						image.color = color3;
					}
					else if (characterMeshOption.optionType == CharacterMeshOptionType.Hair || characterMeshOption.optionType == CharacterMeshOptionType.FacialHair)
					{
						Color color4 = options.posterHairOptions[meshOption.materialIndex];
						image.color = color4;
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

// Assembly-CSharp, Version=0.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null
// WaypointFly
using MoreMountains.Feedbacks;
using UnityEngine;
using UnityEngine.Events;

public class WaypointFly : MonoBehaviour
{
	public Transform[] waypoints;

	public float maxSpeed;

	public AnimationCurve speedCurve;

	public MMF_Player feedbacks;

	public bool damage = true;

	public bool resetAfter;

	public UnityEvent onReset;

	private int nextWaypoint;

	private bool moving = true;

	private float totalDist;

	private float distTraveled;

	private Vector3 startPos;

	private void Awake()
	{
		startPos = base.transform.position;
		totalDist = Vector3.Distance(base.transform.position, waypoints[0].position);
		for (int i = 0; i < waypoints.Length - 1; i++)
		{
			totalDist += Vector3.Distance(waypoints[i].position, waypoints[i + 1].position);
		}
	}

	private void OnCollisionEnter(Collision collision)
	{
		if (damage)
		{
			PlayerController component = collision.collider.GetComponent<PlayerController>();
			if (component != null && !component.dead && moving)
			{
				feedbacks.transform.SetParent(null);
				feedbacks.transform.position = collision.contacts[0].point;
				feedbacks.PlayFeedbacks();
				component.Kill();
			}
		}
	}

	private void FixedUpdate()
	{
		if (!moving)
		{
			return;
		}
		float num = speedCurve.Evaluate(distTraveled / totalDist) * maxSpeed;
		Vector3 vector = Vector3.MoveTowards(base.transform.position, waypoints[nextWaypoint].position, num * Time.fixedDeltaTime);
		float num2 = Vector3.Distance(vector, base.transform.position);
		distTraveled += num2;
		if (num2 < num * Time.fixedDeltaTime - 0.001f)
		{
			nextWaypoint++;
			if (nextWaypoint >= waypoints.Length)
			{
				moving = false;
				if (resetAfter)
				{
					Restart();
					return;
				}
			}
			else
			{
				vector = Vector3.MoveTowards(vector, waypoints[nextWaypoint].position, num * Time.fixedDeltaTime - num2);
				float num3 = Vector3.Distance(vector, base.transform.position);
				distTraveled += num3;
			}
		}
		base.transform.position = vector;
	}

	public void Restart()
	{
		base.transform.position = startPos;
		nextWaypoint = 0;
		distTraveled = 0f;
		moving = true;
		base.gameObject.SetActive(value: false);
		onReset.Invoke();
	}
}
